Motivated by the high memory cost of GRAVE in General Game Playing, this paper proposes GRAVE2, GRAVER, and GRAVER2 to reduce stored nodes without sacrificing performance. These methods introduce two-level search, node recycling, and their combination to eliminate redundant node storage while preserving the original algorithm’s strength. Experimental results demonstrate that these variants achieve comparable playing strength to GRAVE while drastically reducing memory usage.
为了解决GRAVE在通用游戏竞技中因存储大量节点导致的高内存消耗问题，本文提出了GRAVE2、GRAVER和GRAVER2三种改进算法，分别通过两级搜索、节点回收及二者结合来减少存储节点数量。实验表明，这些方法显著降低了内存开销，同时保持了与原始GRAVE相当的竞技水平，使其在内存受限环境下具备实用价值。
Invariant Transformation and Resampling based Epistemic-Uncertainty Reduction
Authors: Sha Hu
First: 2026-02-26T18:22:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:22:40+00:00
Comments: 5 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
An artificial intelligence (AI) model can be viewed as a function that maps inputs to outputs in high-dimensional spaces. Once designed and well trained, the AI model is applied for inference. However, even optimized AI models can produce inference errors due to aleatoric and epistemic uncertainties. Interestingly, we observed that when inferring multiple samples based on invariant transformations of an input, inference errors can show partial independences due to epistemic uncertainty. Leveraging this insight, we propose a "resampling" based inferencing that applies to a trained AI model with multiple transformed versions of an input, and aggregates inference outputs to a more accurate result. This approach has the potential to improve inference accuracy and offers a strategy for balancing model size and performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于不变变换与重采样的认知不确定性降低
人工智能模型可视为将高维空间中的输入映射到输出的函数。一旦设计并充分训练完成，该模型即用于推理。然而，即使经过优化的AI模型仍可能因偶然性和认知不确定性而产生推理误差。有趣的是，我们观察到：当基于输入的不变变换推断多个样本时，由于认知不确定性，推理误差可表现出部分独立性。基于此洞察，我们提出一种“重采样”推理方法，该方法对训练好的AI模型应用输入的多个变换版本，并聚合推理输出以获得更精确的结果。该方法有望提升推理准确性，并提供在模型规模与性能间平衡的策略。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that epistemic uncertainty in AI models can lead to partially independent inference errors across invariant transformations of an input, this work proposes a resampling-based inference method that applies multiple transformed versions of an input to a trained model and aggregates their outputs to reduce epistemic uncertainty. The method leverages the structural invariance of inputs to generate diverse yet semantically equivalent samples, enabling the model to explore its own uncertainty and produce more robust predictions. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach consistently improves inference accuracy across multiple benchmarks, while maintaining computational efficiency and offering a practical trade-off between model size and performance.
鉴于AI模型在输入的不变变换下因认知不确定性导致的推理误差具有部分独立性，本文提出一种基于重采样的推理方法，即对同一输入的多个变换版本应用训练好的模型并聚合输出，以降低不确定性。实验结果表明，该方法相比单样本推理能稳定提升推理精度，同时保持计算可行性，并提供了一种在模型规模与性能间取得平衡的实用策略。
Evaluating Zero-Shot and One-Shot Adaptation of Small Language Models in Leader-Follower Interaction
Authors: Rafael R. Baptista, André de Lima Salgado, Ricardo V. Godoy, Marcelo Becker, Thiago Boaventura, Gustavo J. G. Lahr
First: 2026-02-26T18:20:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:20:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Leader-follower interaction is an important paradigm in human-robot interaction (HRI). Yet, assigning roles in real time remains challenging for resource-constrained mobile and assistive robots. While large language models (LLMs) have shown promise for natural communication, their size and latency limit on-device deployment. Small language models (SLMs) offer a potential alternative, but their effectiveness for role classification in HRI has not been systematically evaluated. In this paper, we present a benchmark of SLMs for leader-follower communication, introducing a novel dataset derived from a published database and augmented with synthetic samples to capture interaction-specific dynamics. We investigate two adaptation strategies: prompt engineering and fine-tuning, studied under zero-shot and one-shot interaction modes, compared with an untrained baseline. Experiments with Qwen2.5-0.5B reveal that zero-shot fine-tuning achieves robust classification performance (86.66% accuracy) while maintaining low latency (22.2 ms per sample), significantly outperforming baseline and prompt-engineered approaches. However, results also indicate a performance degradation in one-shot modes, where increased context length challenges the model's architectural capacity. These findings demonstrate that fine-tuned SLMs provide an effective solution for direct role assignment, while highlighting critical trade-offs between dialogue complexity and classification reliability on the edge.
中文标题/摘要
标题：小语言模型在领导者-跟随者交互中的零样本与一样本适应性评估
领导者-跟随者交互是人机交互（HRI）中的重要范式，但在资源受限的移动和辅助机器人中实时分配角色仍具挑战性。尽管大语言模型（LLMs）在自然对话方面表现良好，但其体积和延迟限制了设备端部署。小语言模型（SLMs）提供了潜在替代方案，但其在HRI中角色分类的有效性尚未系统评估。本文提出针对领导者-跟随者通信的SLM基准测试，引入基于已发布数据库并辅以合成样本的新数据集，以捕捉交互特定动态。我们研究两种适应策略：提示工程与微调，分别在零样本和一样本交互模式下进行，与未训练基线对比。实验表明，Qwen2.5-0.5B的零样本微调在保持低延迟（每样本22.2毫秒）的同时实现稳健分类性能（准确率86.66%），显著优于基线和提示工程方法。然而，一样本模式下性能下降，因上下文长度增加挑战了模型架构容量。结果表明，微调SLM可有效实现直接角色分配，同时揭示了边缘设备上对话复杂度与分类可靠性之间的关键权衡。
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the challenge of real-time role assignment in human-robot interaction for resource-limited robots, exploring whether small language models (SLMs) can effectively classify leader-follower roles without extensive training. The authors evaluate two adaptation methods—prompt engineering and fine-tuning—under zero-shot and one-shot conditions, using a newly constructed dataset derived from existing data and augmented with synthetic samples. Experiments with Qwen2.5-0.5B show that zero-shot fine-tuning achieves high accuracy (86.66%) with low latency (22.2 ms), outperforming both the untrained baseline and prompt-based methods. However, one-shot adaptation suffers from performance degradation due to increased context length, revealing a trade-off between dialogue complexity and model reliability on edge devices.
本研究针对资源受限机器人在人机交互中实时角色分配的挑战，评估了小型语言模型（SLM）在领导者-跟随者分类中的表现。作者构建了基于现有数据并加入合成样本的新数据集，以反映交互动态，并对比了零样本和一样本条件下提示工程与微调策略，与未训练基线模型进行比较。实验表明，Qwen2.5-0.5B在零样本微调下达到86.66%准确率且延迟低（22.2毫秒），显著优于基线和提示工程方法；而一样本模式因上下文长度增加导致模型容量不足，性能下降。
Evaluating the Diversity and Quality of LLM Generated Content
Authors: Alexander Shypula, Shuo Li, Botong Zhang, Vishakh Padmakumar, Kayo Yin, Osbert Bastani
First: 2025-04-16T23:02:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:17:44+00:00
Comments: Published at COLM 2025
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent work suggests that preference-tuning techniques -- such as Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) methods like PPO and GRPO, as well as alternatives like DPO -- reduce diversity, creating a dilemma given that these models are widely deployed in applications requiring varied outputs. We argue that diversity without consideration of quality has limited practical value. To address this issue, we introduce a framework for measuring effective semantic diversity -- diversity among outputs that meet quality thresholds -- which better reflects the practical utility of large language models (LLMs). Using open-ended tasks that require no human intervention, we find counterintuitive results: when using diversity metrics that do not explicitly consider quality, preference-tuned models -- particularly those trained via RL -- often produce outputs with lower diversity; however, these same preference-tuned models generate greater effective semantic diversity than supervised fine-tuned (SFT) or base models. Our analysis further shows another trend: while larger models may exhibit greater effective semantic diversity than smaller models, the smaller models are consistently more parameter-efficient at producing unique content within a fixed sampling budget. These findings have practical implications for applications that require diverse yet high-quality outputs, from creative assistance to synthetic data generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：评估大语言模型生成内容的多样性和质量
近期研究表明，偏好调优技术（如基于人类反馈的强化学习方法PPO和GRPO，以及替代方案DPO）会降低多样性，这与这些模型广泛部署于需要多样化输出的应用场景形成矛盾。我们认为，不考虑质量的多样性具有有限的实用价值。为解决此问题，我们提出了一种衡量有效语义多样性的框架——即满足质量阈值的输出之间的多样性，这更准确地反映了大语言模型（LLMs）的实际效用。通过无需人工干预的开放式任务，我们发现反直觉的结果：当使用未显式考虑质量的多样性度量时，偏好调优模型（特别是通过RL训练的模型）往往生成多样性更低的输出；然而，这些偏好调优模型在有效语义多样性方面优于监督微调（SFT）或基础模型。我们的分析还揭示另一趋势：虽然更大模型在有效语义多样性上可能优于小模型，但小模型在固定采样预算下生成独特内容时更具参数效率。这些发现对需要多样化且高质量输出的应用（如创意辅助和合成数据生成）具有实际意义。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the concern that preference-tuning methods like RLHF reduce output diversity while being widely used in real-world applications, this study proposes a framework to measure 'effective semantic diversity'—diversity among outputs that meet predefined quality thresholds. Using open-ended tasks without human intervention, experiments reveal that while traditional diversity metrics show lower diversity in preference-tuned models, these models actually generate greater effective semantic diversity than SFT or base models. Additionally, larger models show higher effective diversity but smaller models are more parameter-efficient at generating unique content within fixed sampling budgets, suggesting trade-offs in practical deployment.
鉴于偏好调优方法（如RLHF）可能降低输出多样性，但广泛应用于实际场景，本研究提出一种衡量有效语义多样性的框架——即满足质量阈值的输出多样性，以更贴近实际效用。在无需人工干预的开放任务中，研究发现传统多样性指标显示偏好调优模型多样性较低，但这些模型实际生成的有效语义多样性高于SFT或基线模型。此外，更大模型虽具更高有效多样性，但小模型在固定采样预算下更节省参数以生成独特内容，为需要兼顾质量与多样性的应用（如创意辅助或合成数据生成）提供了实用权衡。
Conformal Prediction with Corrupted Labels: Uncertain Imputation and Robust Re-weighting
Authors: Shai Feldman, Stephen Bates, Yaniv Romano
First: 2025-05-07T18:46:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:16:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce a framework for robust uncertainty quantification in situations where labeled training data are corrupted, through noisy or missing labels. We build on conformal prediction, a statistical tool for generating prediction sets that cover the test label with a pre-specified probability. The validity of conformal prediction, however, holds under the i.i.d assumption, which does not hold in our setting due to the corruptions in the data. To account for this distribution shift, the privileged conformal prediction (PCP) method proposed leveraging privileged information (PI) -- additional features available only during training -- to re-weight the data distribution, yielding valid prediction sets under the assumption that the weights are accurate. In this work, we analyze the robustness of PCP to inaccuracies in the weights. Our analysis indicates that PCP can still yield valid uncertainty estimates even when the weights are poorly estimated. Furthermore, we introduce uncertain imputation (UI), a new conformal method that does not rely on weight estimation. Instead, we impute corrupted labels in a way that preserves their uncertainty. Our approach is supported by theoretical guarantees and validated empirically on both synthetic and real benchmarks. Finally, we show that these techniques can be integrated into a triply robust framework, ensuring statistically valid predictions as long as at least one underlying method is valid.
中文标题/摘要
标题：带损坏标签的置信预测：不确定填补与鲁棒重加权
我们提出了一种框架，用于在标注训练数据被噪声或缺失标签污染的情况下实现鲁棒的不确定性量化。该框架基于置信预测，一种用于生成覆盖测试标签的预测集的统计工具，其有效性依赖于独立同分布（i.i.d.）假设，但在我们的场景中该假设不成立，因为数据存在污染。为应对这一分布偏移，我们提出了特权置信预测（PCP）方法，利用仅在训练阶段可用的特权信息（PI）对数据分布进行重加权，从而在权重准确的前提下生成有效的预测集。本研究分析了PCP对权重估计不准确的鲁棒性，结果表明即使权重估计不佳，PCP仍可生成有效的不确定性估计。此外，我们引入了不确定填补（UI），一种无需权重估计的新置信方法，通过保留标签的不确定性来填补损坏标签。该方法具备理论保证，并在合成数据和真实基准上得到实证验证。最后，我们证明这些技术可整合进三重鲁棒框架，只要至少一种底层方法有效，即可确保统计上有效的预测。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of generating reliable uncertainty estimates when training labels are corrupted by noise or missingness, this work proposes two methods within the conformal prediction framework: privileged conformal prediction (PCP) and uncertain imputation (UI). PCP leverages privileged information during training to re-weight data, enabling valid prediction sets under the assumption of accurate weights, while UI avoids weight estimation entirely by imputing corrupted labels while preserving their uncertainty. Experimental results show that PCP remains valid even with inaccurate weights, and UI achieves comparable or better performance without relying on weight estimation. Both methods are theoretically grounded and empirically validated on synthetic and real-world datasets, and can be combined into a triply robust framework that guarantees validity if at least one component is accurate.
为了解决训练标签被噪声或缺失污染时如何生成可靠不确定性估计的问题，本文在符合预测框架内提出了两种方法：特权符合预测（PCP）和不确定插补（UI）。PCP利用训练时特有的额外特征对数据进行重加权，从而在权重准确的前提下生成有效预测集；UI则完全不依赖权重估计，通过保留标签不确定性的方式进行插补。实验表明，即使权重估计不准确，PCP仍能保持有效性，而UI在合成与真实数据集上表现相当或更优。两种方法可组合成三重鲁棒框架，只要其中至少一种方法有效，即可保证预测的统计有效性。
Why Pass@k Optimization Can Degrade Pass@1: Prompt Interference in LLM Post-training
Authors: Anas Barakat, Souradip Chakraborty, Khushbu Pahwa, Amrit Singh Bedi
First: 2026-02-24T18:43:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:11:36+00:00
Comments: updated related work discussion
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Pass@k is a widely used performance metric for verifiable large language model tasks, including mathematical reasoning, code generation, and short-answer reasoning. It defines success if any of $k$ independently sampled solutions passes a verifier. This multi-sample inference metric has motivated inference-aware fine-tuning methods that directly optimize pass@$k$. However, prior work reports a recurring trade-off: pass@k improves while pass@1 degrades under such methods. This trade-off is practically important because pass@1 often remains a hard operational constraint due to latency and cost budgets, imperfect verifier coverage, and the need for a reliable single-shot fallback. We study the origin of this trade-off and provide a theoretical characterization of when pass@k policy optimization can reduce pass@1 through gradient conflict induced by prompt interference. We show that pass@$k$ policy gradients can conflict with pass@1 gradients because pass@$k$ optimization implicitly reweights prompts toward low-success prompts; when these prompts are what we term negatively interfering, their upweighting can rotate the pass@k update direction away from the pass@1 direction. We illustrate our theoretical findings with large language model experiments on verifiable mathematical reasoning tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：为什么Pass@k优化会损害Pass@1：大语言模型后训练中的提示干扰
Pass@k是用于可验证大语言模型任务（如数学推理、代码生成和短答案推理）的广泛使用的性能指标，定义为k个独立采样的解中任一通过验证器即为成功。这一多样本推理指标推动了直接优化pass@$k$的推理感知微调方法。然而，先前研究报道了一个反复出现的权衡：在这些方法下，pass@k提升而pass@1下降。这一权衡在实践中至关重要，因为pass@1常因延迟和成本预算、验证器覆盖不全以及需要可靠的单次回退机制而成为硬性操作约束。我们研究了这一权衡的根源，并通过梯度冲突引发的提示干扰，提供了pass@k策略优化何时会降低pass@1的理论刻画。我们表明，pass@$k$策略梯度可能与pass@1梯度冲突，因为pass@$k$优化隐式地将提示权重向低成功率提示倾斜；当这些提示被我们称为负干扰提示时，其权重增加可能使pass@k更新方向偏离pass@1方向。我们通过在可验证数学推理任务上的大语言模型实验验证了我们的理论发现。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates why optimizing for pass@k in large language models can degrade pass@1, a critical metric for real-world deployment due to latency and cost constraints. It proposes that gradient conflict arises from prompt interference: pass@k optimization implicitly upweights low-success prompts, which can negatively interfere with pass@1 performance by rotating the optimization direction away from single-sample success. The authors demonstrate this phenomenon through experiments on verifiable mathematical reasoning tasks, confirming that pass@k improvements often come at the expense of pass@1, due to the misalignment of gradients caused by prompt reweighting.
为了解决在可验证任务中优化大语言模型时pass@k提升而pass@1下降的问题，该研究分析了梯度冲突导致的性能权衡。作者指出，pass@k优化会隐式提升低成功率提示的权重，当这些提示具有负干扰效应时，会扭曲pass@k梯度方向，使其偏离pass@1目标。在数学推理任务上的实验结果证实，这种提示重加权会导致pass@1准确率下降，同时提升pass@k，验证了负干扰提示引发梯度冲突的理论分析。
ThinkOmni: Lifting Textual Reasoning to Omni-modal Scenarios via Guidance Decoding
Authors: Yiran Guan, Sifan Tu, Dingkang Liang, Linghao Zhu, Jianzhong Ju, Zhenbo Luo, Jian Luan, Yuliang Liu, Xiang Bai
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-26T18:10:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:10:41+00:00
Comments: Accept by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Omni-modal reasoning is essential for intelligent systems to understand and draw inferences from diverse data sources. While existing omni-modal large language models (OLLM) excel at perceiving diverse modalities, they lack the complex reasoning abilities of recent large reasoning models (LRM). However, enhancing the reasoning ability of OLLMs through additional training presents significant challenges, including the need for high-quality data, task-specific adaptation, and substantial computational costs. To address these limitations, we propose ThinkOmni, a training-free and data-free framework that lifts textual reasoning to omni-modal scenarios. ThinkOmni introduces two key components: 1) LRM-as-a-Guide, which leverages off-the-shelf LRMs to guide the OLLM decoding process; 2) Stepwise Contrastive Scaling, which adaptively balances perception and reasoning signals without manual hyperparameter tuning. Experiments on six multi-modal reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that ThinkOmni consistently delivers performance improvements, with main results achieving 70.2 on MathVista and 75.5 on MMAU. Overall, ThinkOmni offers a flexible and generalizable solution for omni-modal reasoning and provides new insights into the generalization and application of reasoning capabilities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ThinkOmni：通过引导解码将文本推理提升至全模态场景
全模态推理对于智能系统理解并从多样化数据源中推断至关重要。尽管现有的全模态大语言模型（OLLM）擅长感知多种模态，但缺乏近期大型推理模型（LRM）的复杂推理能力。然而，通过额外训练增强OLLM的推理能力面临诸多挑战，包括高质量数据需求、任务特定适配及高昂计算成本。为解决这些问题，我们提出ThinkOmni，一种无需训练且无需数据的框架，将文本推理能力提升至全模态场景。ThinkOmni包含两个关键组件：1）LRM-as-a-Guide，利用现成的LRM引导OLLM解码过程；2）分步对比缩放，自适应平衡感知与推理信号，无需手动调参。在六个多模态推理基准测试中，ThinkOmni持续提升性能，主要结果在MathVista上达70.2，在MMAU上达75.5。总体而言，ThinkOmni为全模态推理提供了一种灵活且可泛化的解决方案，并为推理能力的泛化与应用提供了新见解。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance omni-modal large language models (OLLMs) with complex reasoning without costly retraining, ThinkOmni proposes a training-free, data-free framework that transfers textual reasoning to multi-modal contexts. It employs LRM-as-a-Guide to steer OLLM decoding using pre-trained large reasoning models, and Stepwise Contrastive Scaling to dynamically balance perception and reasoning signals without manual tuning. Experiments across six benchmarks show consistent gains, achieving 70.2 on MathVista and 75.5 on MMAU, demonstrating its effectiveness and generalizability.
为在不进行额外训练和数据标注的前提下提升多模态大语言模型的推理能力，ThinkOmni提出了一种无训练、无数据的框架，将文本推理能力迁移到多模态场景中。其核心机制包括：利用现成的大推理模型指导多模态模型的解码过程（LRM-as-a-Guide），以及通过逐步对比缩放动态平衡感知与推理信号（Stepwise Contrastive Scaling），无需手动调参。在六个多模态推理基准测试中，该方法表现稳定，分别在MathVista和MMAU上达到70.2和75.5的性能，验证了其在多模态推理任务中的有效性与泛化能力。
DRESS: A Continuous Framework for Structural Graph Refinement
Authors: Eduar Castrillo Velilla
First: 2026-02-24T12:18:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:10:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Weisfeiler-Lehman (WL) hierarchy is a cornerstone framework for graph isomorphism testing and structural analysis. However, scaling beyond 1-WL to 3-WL and higher requires tensor-based operations that scale as $\mathcal{O}(n^3)$ or $\mathcal{O}(n^4)$, making them computationally prohibitive for large graphs. In this paper, we start from the Original-DRESS equation (Castrillo, León, and Gómez, 2018) -- a parameter-free, continuous dynamical system on edges -- and show that it distinguishes the prism graph from $K_{3,3}$, a pair that 1-WL provably cannot separate. We then generalize it to Motif-DRESS, which replaces triangle neighborhoods with arbitrary structural motifs and converges to a unique fixed point under three sufficient conditions, and further to Generalized-DRESS, an abstract template parameterized by the choice of neighborhood operator, aggregation function and norm. Finally, we introduce $Δ$-DRESS, which runs DRESS on each node-deleted subgraph $G \setminus \{v\}$, connecting the framework to the Kelly--Ulam reconstruction conjecture. Both Motif-DRESS and $Δ$-DRESS empirically distinguish Strongly Regular Graphs (SRGs) -- such as the Rook and Shrikhande graphs -- that confound 3-WL. Our results establish the DRESS family as a highly scalable framework that empirically surpasses both 1-WL and 3-WL on well-known benchmark graphs, without the prohibitive $\mathcal{O}(n^4)$ computational cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DRESS：结构图细化的连续框架
Weisfeiler-Lehman（WL）层次结构是图同构测试与结构分析的核心框架。然而，将WL扩展至3-WL及以上需要基于张量的操作，其计算复杂度为$\mathcal{O}(n^3)$或$\mathcal{O}(n^4)$，对大规模图而言计算代价过高。本文从Castrillo、León和Gómez（2018）提出的原始DRESS方程——一个无参数的边上的连续动力系统——出发，证明其能区分棱柱图与$K_{3,3}$，而1-WL对此对无法区分。随后，我们将其推广为Motif-DRESS，用任意结构模式替代三角邻域，并在三个充分条件下收敛至唯一不动点；进一步推广为Generalized-DRESS，其为一个抽象模板，由邻域操作符、聚合函数和范数参数化。最后，我们引入$Δ$-DRESS，其在每个删除节点的子图$G \setminus \{v\}$上运行DRESS，将框架与Kelly-Ulam重构猜想相联系。Motif-DRESS和$Δ$-DRESS在实验上能区分强正则图（SRGs）——如车棋图和Shrikhande图——这些图会混淆3-WL。我们的结果表明，DRESS家族是一个高度可扩展的框架，在知名基准图上实证上超越1-WL和3-WL，且无需$\mathcal{O}(n^4)$的高计算代价。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational intractability of higher-order Weisfeiler-Lehman methods for large graphs, this paper introduces DRESS, a continuous dynamical system on graph edges that can distinguish graphs 1-WL cannot, such as the prism and K_{3,3}. It generalizes the original formulation to Motif-DRESS using arbitrary structural motifs and Generalized-DRESS via parameterized neighborhood, aggregation, and norm choices, all converging to fixed points under mild conditions. The framework further extends to Δ-DRESS, which runs DRESS on node-deleted subgraphs, linking it to graph reconstruction theory. Empirical results show that both Motif-DRESS and Δ-DRESS successfully distinguish Strongly Regular Graphs like Rook and Shrikhande graphs that evade 3-WL, while maintaining computational efficiency without the O(n^4) cost of traditional higher-order WL.
为解决高阶Weisfeiler-Lehman测试在大规模图上计算不可行的问题，本文提出DRESS框架，一种基于连续动力系统的图结构精炼方法。从原始DRESS方程出发，推广至使用任意结构模式的Motif-DRESS和参数化的Generalized-DRESS，并引入Δ-DRESS在节点删除子图上运行。实验证明，Motif-DRESS与Δ-DRESS能区分3-WL无法分辨的强正则图（如Rook和Shrikhande图），并在多个基准图上实测优于1-WL和3-WL，且避免了高阶WL的O(n⁴)计算开销。
A Proper Scoring Rule for Virtual Staining
Authors: Samuel Tonks, Steve Hood, Ryan Musso, Ceridwen Hopely, Steve Titus, Minh Doan, Iain Styles, Alexander Krull
First: 2026-02-26T18:09:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:09:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative virtual staining (VS) models for high-throughput screening (HTS) can provide an estimated posterior distribution of possible biological feature values for each input and cell. However, when evaluating a VS model, the true posterior is unavailable. Existing evaluation protocols only check the accuracy of the marginal distribution over the dataset rather than the predicted posteriors. We introduce information gain (IG) as a cell-wise evaluation framework that enables direct assessment of predicted posteriors. IG is a strictly proper scoring rule and comes with a sound theoretical motivation allowing for interpretability, and for comparing results across models and features. We evaluate diffusion- and GAN-based models on an extensive HTS dataset using IG and other metrics and show that IG can reveal substantial performance differences other metrics cannot.
中文标题/摘要
标题：虚拟染色的恰当评分规则
用于高通量筛选（HTS）的生成式虚拟染色（VS）模型可为每个输入和细胞提供可能的生物特征值的后验分布估计。然而，在评估VS模型时，真实的后验分布不可用。现有评估协议仅检查数据集上的边际分布准确性，而非预测的后验分布。我们引入信息增益（IG）作为细胞级评估框架，可直接评估预测的后验分布。IG是一种严格恰当的评分规则，具有坚实的理论基础，支持可解释性，并允许在不同模型和特征间进行比较。我们在广泛HTS数据集上使用IG及其他指标评估基于扩散和GAN的模型，结果表明IG能揭示其他指标无法发现的显著性能差异。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to evaluate generative virtual staining models without access to true posterior distributions, this work introduces information gain (IG) as a strictly proper scoring rule that directly assesses predicted posteriors at the cell level, offering theoretical interpretability and cross-model comparability. IG is applied alongside other metrics to evaluate diffusion and GAN-based models on a large high-throughput screening dataset, revealing significant performance differences that other metrics fail to capture.
为了解决在缺乏真实后验分布情况下评估生成虚拟染色模型的问题，本文提出信息增益作为细胞级评分规则，直接评估预测后验分布。与仅评估边缘分布准确性的现有方法不同，信息增益是一种严格恰当评分规则，具备理论基础，支持可解释性及跨模型比较。在广泛HTS数据集上对扩散和GAN模型的实验表明，信息增益能揭示其他指标无法发现的显著性能差异。
Inferential Mechanics Part 1: Causal Mechanistic Theories of Machine Learning in Chemical Biology with Implications
Authors: Ilya Balabin, Thomas M. Kaiser
First: 2026-02-26T18:09:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:09:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Machine learning techniques are now routinely encountered in research laboratories across the globe. Impressive progress has been made through ML and AI techniques with regards to large data set processing. This progress has increased the ability of the experimenter to digest data and make novel predictions regarding phenomena of interest. However, machine learning predictors generated from data sets taken from the natural sciences are often treated as black boxes which are used broadly and generally without detailed consideration of the causal structure of the data set of interest. Work has been attempted to bring causality into discussions of machine learning models of natural phenomena; however, a firm and unified theoretical treatment is lacking. This series of three papers explores the union of chemical theory, biological theory, probability theory and causality that will correct current causal flaws of machine learning in the natural sciences. This paper, Part 1 of the series, provides the formal framework of the foundational causal structure of phenomena in chemical biology and is extended to machine learning through the novel concept of focus, defined here as the ability of a machine learning algorithm to narrow down to a hidden underpinning mechanism in large data sets. Initial proof of these principles on a family of Akt inhibitors is also provided. The second paper containing Part 2 will provide a formal exploration of chemical similarity, and Part 3 will present extensive experimental evidence of how hidden causal structures weaken all machine learning in chemical biology. This series serves to establish for chemical biology a new kind of mathematical framework for modeling mechanisms in Nature without the need for the tools of reductionism: inferential mechanics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推断力学第一部分：化学生物学中机器学习的因果机制理论及其影响
机器学习技术如今在全球研究实验室中已广泛应用。通过机器学习和人工智能技术，大数据集处理取得了显著进展，这增强了实验人员消化数据并就所关注现象做出新颖预测的能力。然而，从自然科学数据集中生成的机器学习预测模型常被视为“黑箱”，被广泛而笼统地使用，而未对所关注数据集的因果结构进行详细考虑。尽管已有尝试将因果性引入自然现象机器学习模型的讨论，但尚缺乏坚实且统一的理论处理。本系列三篇论文探讨了化学理论、生物理论、概率论与因果性相结合的框架，旨在纠正当前机器学习在自然科学中的因果缺陷。本论文为系列的第一部分，提供了化学生物学现象基础因果结构的形式化框架，并通过“焦点”这一新颖概念扩展至机器学习领域——“焦点”被定义为机器学习算法在大数据集中识别隐藏底层机制的能力。本文还初步验证了这些原理在Akt抑制剂家族中的应用。第二篇论文（Part 2）将正式探讨化学相似性，第三篇（Part 3）将提供大量实验证据，说明隐藏的因果结构如何削弱化学生物学中的所有机器学习方法。本系列旨在为化学生物学建立一种新的数学框架，用于建模自然界的机制，而无需依赖还原论工具：推断力学。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to address causal blind spots in machine learning applications within chemical biology, this paper proposes a formal causal framework grounded in chemical and biological theory, extended to machine learning via the novel concept of 'focus'—the ability of algorithms to identify hidden mechanistic structures in large datasets. The method integrates probability and causality to model natural phenomena without reductionism, establishing a new paradigm called 'inferential mechanics'. Initial validation is demonstrated using a family of Akt inhibitors, showing that machine learning models can be guided toward mechanistic insights rather than mere pattern recognition. The results suggest that incorporating causal structure improves interpretability and predictive power in chemical biology.
为弥补机器学习在化学生物学中缺乏因果解释的问题，本文提出融合化学、生物、概率与因果理论的形式化框架，引入‘聚焦’概念——即机器学习识别大型数据集中隐藏机制的能力，并通过Akt抑制剂数据初步验证。结果表明，机器学习模型可被引导至机制性解释而非纯统计模式，为建立无需还原论的‘推断力学’新范式奠定基础。
The logic of KM belief update is contained in the logic of AGM belief revision
Authors: Giacomo Bonanno
First: 2026-02-26T18:09:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:09:02+00:00
Comments: arXiv admin note: text overlap with arXiv:2310.11506. text overlap with arXiv:2310.11506
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
For each axiom of KM belief update we provide a corresponding axiom in a modal logic containing three modal operators: a unimodal belief operator $B$, a bimodal conditional operator $>$ and the unimodal necessity operator $\square$. We then compare the resulting logic to the similar logic obtained from converting the AGM axioms of belief revision into modal axioms and show that the latter contains the former. Denoting the latter by $\mathcal L_{AGM}$ and the former by $\mathcal L_{KM}$ we show that every axiom of $\mathcal L_{KM}$ is a theorem of $\mathcal L_{AGM}$. Thus AGM belief revision can be seen as a special case of KM belief update. For the strong version of KM belief update we show that the difference between $\mathcal L_{KM}$ and $\mathcal L_{AGM}$ can be narrowed down to a single axiom, which deals exclusively with unsurprising information, that is, with formulas that were not initially disbelieved.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KM信念更新的逻辑包含在AGM信念修订的逻辑中
我们为每个KM信念更新公理提供一个对应的模态逻辑公理，该逻辑包含三个模态算子：单模态信念算子B、双模态条件算子>和单模态必然性算子□。然后我们将所得逻辑与从AGM信念修订公理转换为模态公理所得的类似逻辑进行比较，证明后者包含前者。记后者为L_{AGM}，前者为L_{KM}，我们证明L_{KM}中的每个公理都是L_{AGM}中的定理。因此，AGM信念修订可视为KM信念更新的一个特例。对于KM信念更新的强版本，我们证明L_{KM}与L_{AGM}之间的差异可归结为一个单一公理，该公理专门处理非令人惊讶的信息，即最初未被否定的公式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to formalize belief update within a modal logic framework, the paper establishes a correspondence between KM belief update axioms and a modal logic system featuring belief, conditional, and necessity operators. It demonstrates that every axiom of the KM logic is derivable in the AGM belief revision logic, thereby showing that KM belief update is a special case of AGM revision. For the strong version of KM, the distinction between the two logics reduces to a single axiom governing unsurprising information—formulas not initially disbelieved—highlighting a nuanced boundary between the two belief change models.
为比较信念更新与信念修订框架，本文证明KM信念更新逻辑完全包含于AGM信念修订逻辑中。通过将KM的每个公理转化为包含信念、条件和必然性三个模态算子的模态公理，作者证明所有KM公理均可在AGM逻辑中推导得出。进一步地，对于强版本的KM信念更新，二者差异仅归结于一个涉及“非意外信息”（即初始未被否定的信息）的公理，从而表明AGM逻辑是更一般的框架，涵盖KM逻辑。
A Mixture-of-Experts Model for Multimodal Emotion Recognition in Conversations
Authors: Soumya Dutta, Smruthi Balaji, Sriram Ganapathy
First: 2026-02-26T18:08:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:08:40+00:00
Comments: Accepted to Elsevier Computer Speech and Language. 30 pages, 9 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Emotion Recognition in Conversations (ERC) presents unique challenges, requiring models to capture the temporal flow of multi-turn dialogues and to effectively integrate cues from multiple modalities. We propose Mixture of Speech-Text Experts for Recognition of Emotions (MiSTER-E), a modular Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) framework designed to decouple two core challenges in ERC: modality-specific context modeling and multimodal information fusion. MiSTER-E leverages large language models (LLMs) fine-tuned for both speech and text to provide rich utterance-level embeddings, which are then enhanced through a convolutional-recurrent context modeling layer. The system integrates predictions from three experts-speech-only, text-only, and cross-modal-using a learned gating mechanism that dynamically weighs their outputs. To further encourage consistency and alignment across modalities, we introduce a supervised contrastive loss between paired speech-text representations and a KL-divergence-based regulariza-tion across expert predictions. Importantly, MiSTER-E does not rely on speaker identity at any stage. Experiments on three benchmark datasets-IEMOCAP, MELD, and MOSI-show that our proposal achieves 70.9%, 69.5%, and 87.9% weighted F1-scores respectively, outperforming several baseline speech-text ERC systems. We also provide various ablations to highlight the contributions made in the proposed approach.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于对话中多模态情绪识别的专家混合模型
对话情绪识别（ERC）具有独特挑战，要求模型捕捉多轮对话的时间流并有效融合多模态线索。我们提出MiSTER-E（用于情绪识别的语音-文本专家混合模型），一种模块化专家混合（MoE）框架，旨在解耦ERC中的两个核心挑战：模态特定上下文建模与多模态信息融合。MiSTER-E利用针对语音和文本微调的大语言模型（LLMs）生成丰富的语句级嵌入，并通过卷积-循环上下文建模层增强。系统通过学习门控机制动态加权三个专家（仅语音、仅文本、跨模态）的预测结果。为进一步促进模态间的一致性与对齐，我们引入配对语音-文本表示的监督对比损失及专家预测间的KL散度正则化。重要的是，MiSTER-E在任何阶段均不依赖说话人身份。在三个基准数据集（IEMOCAP、MELD、MOSI）上的实验表明，我们的方法分别取得70.9%、69.5%和87.9%的加权F1分数，优于多个基线语音-文本ERC系统。我们还提供多种消融实验以突出所提方法的贡献。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to handle temporal dynamics and multimodal integration in conversational emotion recognition, the paper introduces MiSTER-E, a Mixture-of-Experts model that separates modality-specific context modeling from multimodal fusion using speech and text LLMs. The system employs a convolutional-recurrent layer to enhance utterance embeddings and combines three expert outputs—speech-only, text-only, and cross-modal—via a learned gating mechanism. A supervised contrastive loss and KL-divergence regularization promote modality alignment without relying on speaker identity. Experiments on IEMOCAP, MELD, and MOSI show MiSTER-E achieves F1 scores of 70.9%, 69.5%, and 87.9%, outperforming several baselines.
为应对对话中情绪识别需同时处理时序动态与多模态融合的挑战，作者提出MiSTER-E模型，通过模块化专家架构分离模态特异性上下文建模与多模态融合任务，利用针对语音和文本微调的大语言模型生成语句级嵌入，并通过卷积-循环层增强。系统结合三个专家（语音独有、文本独有、跨模态）的预测，通过学习门控机制动态加权。引入监督对比损失和KL散度正则化以增强模态间一致性。在IEMOCAP、MELD和MOSI三个基准数据集上，模型分别取得70.9%、69.5%和87.9%的加权F1分数，优于现有语音-文本情绪识别基线，且不依赖说话人身份。
PRIMA: Pre-training with Risk-integrated Image-Metadata Alignment for Medical Diagnosis via LLM
Authors: Yiqing Wang, Chunming He, Ming-Chen Lu, Mercy Pawar, Leslie Niziol, Maria Woodward, Sina Farsiu
First: 2026-02-26T18:07:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:07:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Medical diagnosis requires the effective synthesis of visual manifestations and clinical metadata. However, existing methods often treat metadata as isolated tags, failing to exploit the rich semantic knowledge embedded in clinical descriptions. We propose PRIMA (Pre-training with Risk-integrated Image-Metadata Alignment), a framework that integrates domain-specific knowledge into multi-modal representation learning. We first curate an expert corpus of risk-disease correlations via Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) to refine Clinical ModernBERT, embedding diagnostic priors into the text encoder. To bridge the modality gap, we introduce a dual-encoder pre-training strategy utilizing DINOv3 and our refined BERT, optimized by a suite of four complementary loss functions. These losses are designed to capture multi-granular semantic alignment and handle the ambiguity of clinical correlations through soft labels. Finally, we leverage Qwen-3 to fuse these aligned features for precise disease classification. Extensive experiments demonstrate that PRIMA effectively harmonizes pixel-level features with abstract clinical expertise, significantly outperforming other state-of-the-art methods. Notably, our framework achieves superior robustness without the need for massive data collection or exhaustive computational resources. Our code will be made public upon acceptance.

Conformalized Neural Networks for Federated Uncertainty Quantification under Dual Heterogeneity
Authors: Quang-Huy Nguyen, Jiaqi Wang, Wei-Shinn Ku
First: 2026-02-26T18:07:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:07:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Federated learning (FL) faces challenges in uncertainty quantification (UQ). Without reliable UQ, FL systems risk deploying overconfident models at under-resourced agents, leading to silent local failures despite seemingly satisfactory global performance. Existing federated UQ approaches often address data heterogeneity or model heterogeneity in isolation, overlooking their joint effect on coverage reliability across agents. Conformal prediction is a widely used distribution-free UQ framework, yet its applications in heterogeneous FL settings remains underexplored. We provide FedWQ-CP, a simple yet effective approach that balances empirical coverage performance with efficiency at both global and agent levels under the dual heterogeneity. FedWQ-CP performs agent-server calibration in a single communication round. On each agent, conformity scores are computed on calibration data and a local quantile threshold is derived. Each agent then transmits only its quantile threshold and calibration sample size to the server. The server simply aggregates these thresholds through a weighted average to produce a global threshold. Experimental results on seven public datasets for both classification and regression demonstrate that FedWQ-CP empirically maintains agent-wise and global coverage while producing the smallest prediction sets or intervals.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向双重异质性的联邦学习置信度量化中的保形神经网络
联邦学习（FL）在不确定性量化（UQ）方面面临挑战。缺乏可靠的UQ可能导致FL系统在资源匮乏的代理节点部署过于自信的模型，尽管全局性能看似满意，但实际存在静默的本地失败。现有联邦UQ方法通常单独处理数据异质性或模型异质性，忽视二者共同作用对各代理节点覆盖可靠性的影响。保形预测是一种广泛使用的无分布假设UQ框架，但在异质性FL场景中的应用仍待探索。我们提出FedWQ-CP，一种简单而有效的方案，在双重异质性下兼顾全局与代理节点的实证覆盖性能与效率。FedWQ-CP在单次通信轮次内完成代理-服务器校准。每个代理在校准数据上计算保形分数并推导本地分位数阈值，仅向服务器传输该阈值和校准样本量。服务器通过加权平均聚合这些阈值生成全局阈值。在七个公开数据集上的实验表明，FedWQ-CP在保持代理级与全局覆盖的同时，生成最小的预测集或区间。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for reliable uncertainty quantification in federated learning under dual heterogeneity, this paper introduces FedWQ-CP, a conformalized neural network approach that calibrates prediction sets at both agent and server levels within a single communication round. Each agent computes conformity scores on local calibration data to derive a quantile threshold, transmitting only this threshold and sample size to the server, which aggregates them via weighted averaging to form a global threshold. Experiments across seven public datasets show FedWQ-CP maintains consistent coverage at both agent and global levels while producing the smallest prediction sets or intervals, outperforming existing methods in efficiency and coverage reliability.
为解决联邦学习在双重异质性下不确定性量化不可靠的问题，本文提出FedWQ-CP方法，通过单轮通信完成各节点的校准。每个节点基于本地校准数据计算一致性分数，推导局部分位数阈值，并仅向服务器发送该阈值与样本量，服务器通过加权平均聚合阈值生成全局阈值。实验表明，FedWQ-CP在七组公开数据集上同时保持节点级与全局覆盖率，且预测集或区间最小，优于现有方法。
ManifoldGD: Training-Free Hierarchical Manifold Guidance for Diffusion-Based Dataset Distillation
Authors: Ayush Roy, Wei-Yang Alex Lee, Rudrasis Chakraborty, Vishnu Suresh Lokhande
First: 2026-02-26T18:07:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:07:10+00:00
Comments: CVPE 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In recent times, large datasets hinder efficient model training while also containing redundant concepts. Dataset distillation aims to synthesize compact datasets that preserve the knowledge of large-scale training sets while drastically reducing storage and computation. Recent advances in diffusion models have enabled training-free distillation by leveraging pre-trained generative priors; however, existing guidance strategies remain limited. Current score-based methods either perform unguided denoising or rely on simple mode-based guidance toward instance prototype centroids (IPC centroids), which often are rudimentary and suboptimal. We propose Manifold-Guided Distillation (ManifoldGD), a training-free diffusion-based framework that integrates manifold consistent guidance at every denoising timestep. Our method employs IPCs computed via a hierarchical, divisive clustering of VAE latent features, yielding a multi-scale coreset of IPCs that captures both coarse semantic modes and fine intra-class variability. Using a local neighborhood of the extracted IPC centroids, we create the latent manifold for each diffusion denoising timestep. At each denoising step, we project the mode-alignment vector onto the local tangent space of the estimated latent manifold, thus constraining the generation trajectory to remain manifold-faithful while preserving semantic consistency. This formulation improves representativeness, diversity, and image fidelity without requiring any model retraining. Empirical results demonstrate consistent gains over existing training-free and training-based baselines in terms of FID, l2 distance among real and synthetic dataset embeddings, and classification accuracy, establishing ManifoldGD as the first geometry-aware training-free data distillation framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ManifoldGD：基于扩散模型的无训练分层流形引导数据蒸馏
近期，大型数据集虽能提升模型性能，但存在冗余概念，且存储与计算成本高昂。数据蒸馏旨在合成紧凑数据集，保留大规模训练集的知识，同时大幅降低存储与计算开销。扩散模型的最新进展使无训练蒸馏成为可能，通过利用预训练生成先验；然而现有引导策略仍显不足。当前基于分数的方法要么无引导去噪，要么仅依赖简单模式引导至实例原型中心（IPC中心），往往粗糙且次优。我们提出Manifold-Guided Distillation（ManifoldGD），一种无训练的扩散框架，每一步去噪均整合流形一致引导。该方法通过VAE潜在特征的分层划分聚类计算IPC，生成多尺度IPC核心集，捕捉粗粒度语义模式与细粒度类内变异。利用提取的IPC中心局部邻域，为每个扩散去噪步骤构建潜在流形。每步去噪时，将模式对齐向量投影至估计流形的局部切空间，从而约束生成轨迹保持流形一致性并保留语义一致性。该方法在无需模型重训练前提下，提升代表性、多样性与图像保真度。实验证明，ManifoldGD在FID、真实与合成数据集嵌入的L2距离、分类准确率等指标上显著优于现有无训练与有训练基线，是首个几何感知的无训练数据蒸馏框架。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to distill large datasets into compact, semantically rich representations without retraining, the paper introduces ManifoldGD, a training-free diffusion-based framework that guides generation via manifold-consistent constraints at each denoising step. It computes instance prototype centroids (IPCs) through hierarchical divisive clustering of VAE latent features, forming a multi-scale coreset capturing both coarse semantics and fine intra-class variation. For each timestep, it projects mode-alignment vectors onto the local tangent space of the estimated latent manifold, ensuring generation remains faithful to the underlying data geometry. Experiments show ManifoldGD outperforms existing training-free and training-based methods in FID, embedding distance, and classification accuracy, establishing it as the first geometry-aware training-free distillation approach.
为解决大尺度数据集冗余且训练效率低的问题，ManifoldGD提出一种无需训练的扩散模型数据蒸馏框架，通过引入流形一致性引导提升合成数据质量。该方法通过分层划分VAE潜在特征计算实例原型中心（IPCs），构建多尺度代表性子集以捕捉语义模式与类内差异。在每一步去噪过程中，将模式对齐向量投影至局部流形切空间，确保生成轨迹保持流形一致性与语义连贯性。实验表明，该方法在FID、真实与合成数据嵌入距离及分类准确率上均优于现有基线，是首个几何感知的无训练数据蒸馏框架。
Phase Transitions for Feature Learning in Neural Networks
Authors: Andrea Montanari, Zihao Wang
First: 2026-02-01T20:47:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:06:09+00:00
Comments: 75 pages; 17 pdf figures; v2 is a minor revision of v1
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
According to a popular viewpoint, neural networks learn from data by first identifying low-dimensional representations, and subsequently fitting the best model in this space. Recent works provide a formalization of this phenomenon when learning multi-index models. In this setting, we are given $n$ i.i.d. pairs $({\boldsymbol x}_i,y_i)$, where the covariate vectors ${\boldsymbol x}_i\in\mathbb{R}^d$ are isotropic, and responses $y_i$ only depend on ${\boldsymbol x}_i$ through a $k$-dimensional projection ${\boldsymbol Θ}_*^{\sf T}{\boldsymbol x}_i$. Feature learning amounts to learning the latent space spanned by ${\boldsymbol Θ}_*$. In this context, we study the gradient descent dynamics of two-layer neural networks under the proportional asymptotics $n,d\to\infty$, $n/d\toδ$, while the dimension of the latent space $k$ and the number of hidden neurons $m$ are kept fixed. Earlier work establishes that feature learning via polynomial-time algorithms is possible if $δ> δ_{\text{alg}}$, for $δ_{\text{alg}}$ a threshold depending on the data distribution, and is impossible (within a certain class of algorithms) below $δ_{\text{alg}}$. Here we derive an analogous threshold $δ_{\text{NN}}$ for two-layer networks. Our characterization of $δ_{\text{NN}}$ opens the way to study the dependence of learning dynamics on the network architecture and training algorithm. The threshold $δ_{\text{NN}}$ is determined by the following scenario. Training first visits points for which the gradient of the empirical risk is large and learns the directions spanned by these gradients. Then the gradient becomes smaller and the dynamics becomes dominated by negative directions of the Hessian. The threshold $δ_{\text{NN}}$ corresponds to a phase transition in the spectrum of the Hessian in this second phase.
中文标题/摘要
标题：神经网络特征学习中的相变
根据一种流行观点，神经网络通过首先识别低维表示，然后在此空间中拟合最佳模型来从数据中学习。近期研究为学习多索引模型时的这一现象提供了形式化描述。在此设定下，我们给定n个独立同分布的样本对(xi, yi)，其中协变量向量xi ∈ Rd是各向同性的，响应yi仅通过k维投影Θ*Txi依赖于xi。特征学习等价于学习由Θ*张成的潜在空间。 在此背景下，我们研究在比例渐近n, d → ∞，n/d → δ，且潜在空间维度k和隐藏神经元数m保持固定时，两层神经网络的梯度下降动力学。先前工作表明，当δ > δ_alg时，多项式时间内可实现特征学习，其中δ_alg是依赖于数据分布的阈值；低于δ_alg时（在特定算法类中）则不可能实现。本文推导出两层网络的类似阈值δ_NN。我们对δ_NN的刻画为研究学习动力学如何依赖于网络结构和训练算法开辟了道路。 阈值δ_NN由以下情景决定：训练首先访问梯度较大的点并学习这些梯度所张成的方向；随后梯度变小，动力学主要由Hessian矩阵的负方向主导。阈值δ_NN对应于第二阶段Hessian谱的相变。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the idea that neural networks learn by discovering low-dimensional latent structures, this paper investigates feature learning in two-layer networks under proportional asymptotics where sample size n and dimension d grow with n/d → δ, while latent dimension k and hidden units m are fixed. The authors analyze gradient descent dynamics and identify a phase transition threshold δ_NN, analogous to a previously known algorithmic threshold δ_alg, beyond which feature learning becomes possible. δ_NN is determined by a spectral transition in the Hessian matrix: early training follows high-gradient directions, but later dynamics are dominated by negative Hessian eigenvalues, marking the onset of feature learning.
该文研究在样本量n与特征维度d按比例δ = n/d增长、而潜在维度k和隐藏单元数m固定的情况下，两层神经网络的梯度下降动态。动机源于神经网络通过学习低维潜在结构进行表征学习的假设。作者推导出一个相变阈值δ_NN，决定特征学习是否可行：当δ低于该阈值时，Hessian矩阵的负特征值主导训练动态，导致学习失败；当δ高于该阈值时，梯度下降能成功识别真实投影矩阵Θ*所张成的潜在子空间。该阈值源于训练过程中从梯度主导到Hessian主导的动态转变。
PoSh: Using Scene Graphs To Guide LLMs-as-a-Judge For Detailed Image Descriptions
Authors: Amith Ananthram, Elias Stengel-Eskin, Lorena A. Bradford, Julia Demarest, Adam Purvis, Keith Krut, Robert Stein, Rina Elster Pantalony, Mohit Bansal, Kathleen McKeown
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-21T20:30:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:05:42+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026. 26 pages, 9 figures. Metric/benchmark available at https://github.com/amith-ananthram/posh
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While vision-language models (VLMs) have advanced into detailed image description, evaluation remains a challenge. Standard metrics (e.g. CIDEr, SPICE) were designed for short texts and tuned to recognize errors that are now uncommon, such as object misidentification. In contrast, long texts require sensitivity to attribute and relation attachments and scores that localize errors to particular text spans. In this work, we introduce PoSh, a metric for detailed image description that uses scene graphs as structured rubrics to guide LLMs-as-a-Judge, producing aggregate scores grounded in fine-grained errors (e.g. mistakes in compositional understanding). PoSh is replicable, interpretable and a better proxy for human raters than existing metrics (including GPT4o-as-a-Judge). To validate PoSh, we introduce a challenging new dataset, DOCENT. This novel benchmark contains artwork, paired with expert-written references, and model-generated descriptions, augmented with granular and coarse judgments of their quality from art history students. Thus, DOCENT enables evaluating both detailed image description metrics and detailed image description itself in a challenging new domain. We show that PoSh achieves stronger correlations (+0.05 Spearman $ρ$) with the human judgments in DOCENT than the best open-weight alternatives, is robust to image type (using CapArena, an existing dataset of web imagery) and is a capable reward function, outperforming standard supervised fine-tuning. Then, using PoSh, we characterize the performance of open and closed models in describing the paintings, sketches and statues in DOCENT and find that foundation models struggle to achieve full, error-free coverage of images with rich scene dynamics, establishing a demanding new task to gauge VLM progress. Through both PoSh and DOCENT, we hope to enable advances in important areas such as assistive text generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PoSh：利用场景图指导LLM作为裁判生成详细图像描述
尽管视觉-语言模型（VLMs）已能生成详细图像描述，但评估仍具挑战。标准指标（如CIDEr、SPICE）为短文本设计，针对如今罕见的错误（如物体误识别）进行调优。相比之下，长文本需敏感于属性与关系的附着，并能将错误定位到特定文本片段。本文提出PoSh，一种基于场景图作为结构化评分标准、引导LLM作为裁判生成细粒度错误评分的详细图像描述评估指标。PoSh可复现、可解释，且比现有指标（包括GPT4o-as-a-Judge）更接近人类评分。为验证PoSh，我们引入新基准数据集DOCENT，包含艺术品、专家撰写参考描述及模型生成描述，并由艺术史学生提供细粒度与粗粒度质量判断。DOCENT使评估详细图像描述指标与描述本身成为可能，且在新挑战领域中进行。我们表明，PoSh在DOCENT中与人类评分的相关性（Spearman ρ）优于现有开源替代方案+0.05，对图像类型鲁棒（使用CapArena现有网络图像数据集），且作为奖励函数优于标准监督微调。通过PoSh，我们刻画了开源与闭源模型在DOCENT中对绘画、素描与雕像的描述表现，发现基础模型难以完全无误覆盖富含场景动态的图像，确立了衡量VLM进展的新挑战任务。通过PoSh与DOCENT，我们希望推动重要领域如辅助文本生成的发展。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inadequacy of existing metrics for evaluating detailed image descriptions, this work introduces PoSh, a novel evaluation method that leverages scene graphs as structured rubrics to guide large language models acting as judges, enabling fine-grained error detection and localized scoring. PoSh is validated on DOCENT, a new benchmark featuring artwork with expert references and student-generated quality judgments, demonstrating stronger correlation with human ratings than prior metrics including GPT4o-as-a-Judge. Experiments show PoSh is robust across image types and effective as a reward function, outperforming supervised fine-tuning, while revealing that foundation models still struggle to fully capture complex scene dynamics in artistic imagery.
为解决现有指标在评估详细图像描述时的不足，本文提出PoSh方法，利用场景图作为结构化评分标准，引导大语言模型担任评委，实现细粒度错误定位与评分。PoSh在新基准DOCENT上得到验证，该基准包含艺术作品、专家参考描述及学生生成的质量判断，结果显示其与人类评分的相关性优于现有指标（包括GPT4o-as-a-Judge）。实验表明PoSh对图像类型鲁棒，且作为奖励函数优于监督微调，同时揭示基础模型在捕捉复杂场景动态方面仍存在困难，为视觉语言模型的发展设定了新的挑战。
The Spacetime of Diffusion Models: An Information Geometry Perspective
Authors: Rafał Karczewski, Markus Heinonen, Alison Pouplin, Søren Hauberg, Vikas Garg
Venue: ICLR 2026 Oral
First: 2025-05-23T06:16:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:04:18+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026 (Oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We present a novel geometric perspective on the latent space of diffusion models. We first show that the standard pullback approach, utilizing the deterministic probability flow ODE decoder, is fundamentally flawed. It provably forces geodesics to decode as straight segments in data space, effectively ignoring any intrinsic data geometry beyond the ambient Euclidean space. Complementing this view, diffusion also admits a stochastic decoder via the reverse SDE, which enables an information geometric treatment with the Fisher-Rao metric. However, a choice of $x_T$ as the latent representation collapses this metric due to memorylessness. We address this by introducing a latent spacetime $z=(x_t,t)$ that indexes the family of denoising distributions $p(x_0 | x_t)$ across all noise scales, yielding a nontrivial geometric structure. We prove these distributions form an exponential family and derive simulation-free estimators for curve lengths, enabling efficient geodesic computation. The resulting structure induces a principled Diffusion Edit Distance, where geodesics trace minimal sequences of noise and denoise edits between data. We also demonstrate benefits for transition path sampling in molecular systems, including constrained variants such as low-variance transitions and region avoidance. Code is available at: https://github.com/rafalkarczewski/spacetime-geometry.
中文标题/摘要
标题：扩散模型的时空：信息几何视角
我们从几何视角提出了一种对扩散模型潜在空间的新理解。首先，我们证明标准的拉回方法（利用确定性概率流ODE解码器）存在根本性缺陷，它必然迫使测地线在数据空间中解码为直线段，从而忽略数据空间中超出欧几里得空间的内在几何结构。此外，扩散模型还可通过反向SDE获得随机解码器，从而支持基于Fisher-Rao度量的信息几何处理。然而，若将x_T作为潜在表示，则该度量因无记忆性而坍缩。我们通过引入潜在时空z=(x_t, t)来解决此问题，该时空索引所有噪声尺度下的去噪分布p(x_0|x_t)族，从而产生非平凡几何结构。我们证明这些分布构成指数族，并推导出无需模拟的曲线长度估计器，实现高效测地线计算。由此结构诱导出一种原理性的扩散编辑距离，其中测地线追踪数据间最小噪声与去噪编辑序列。我们还展示了其在分子系统转移路径采样中的优势，包括低方差转移和区域规避等约束变体。代码见：https://github.com/rafalkarczewski/spacetime-geometry。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of standard diffusion model decoders in capturing intrinsic data geometry, this work introduces a spacetime framework for latent representations by embedding time as a coordinate. It critiques the deterministic pullback approach for forcing straight-line geodesics in data space and instead proposes a stochastic decoder via reverse SDEs, enabling an information geometric treatment using the Fisher-Rao metric. To resolve the metric collapse caused by choosing initial noise as latent, the authors define a latent spacetime z=(x_t, t) that parameterizes denoising distributions across noise scales, revealing an exponential family structure. This yields simulation-free curve length estimators for efficient geodesic computation, leading to a principled Diffusion Edit Distance that minimizes noise and denoise edits between data points. Experiments show improved performance in transition path sampling for molecular systems, including low-variance transitions and region avoidance.
为解决标准扩散模型解码器无法捕捉数据内在几何结构的问题，本文提出通过将时间作为坐标嵌入构建潜变量时空框架。文章批评确定性拉回方法强制数据空间中测地线为直线，转而提出通过逆SDE的随机解码器，结合费雪-罗亚度量进行信息几何处理。为解决以初始噪声作为潜变量导致度量坍缩的问题，作者构建潜变量时空 $z=(x_t,t)$，证明去噪分布族 $p(x_0|x_t)$ 构成指数族，从而实现无需模拟的测地线计算，并定义了基于最小噪声与去噪编辑序列的扩散编辑距离。实验表明该方法在分子系统过渡路径采样中表现更优，包括低方差过渡与区域规避能力。
Towards Long-Form Spatio-Temporal Video Grounding
Authors: Xin Gu, Bing Fan, Jiali Yao, Zhipeng Zhang, Yan Huang, Cheng Han, Heng Fan, Libo Zhang
First: 2026-02-26T18:04:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:04:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In real scenarios, videos can span several minutes or even hours. However, existing research on spatio-temporal video grounding (STVG), given a textual query, mainly focuses on localizing targets in short videos of tens of seconds, typically less than one minute, which limits real-world applications. In this paper, we explore Long-Form STVG (LF-STVG), which aims to locate targets in long-term videos. Compared with short videos, long-term videos contain much longer temporal spans and more irrelevant information, making it difficult for existing STVG methods that process all frames at once. To address this challenge, we propose an AutoRegressive Transformer architecture for LF-STVG, termed ART-STVG. Unlike conventional STVG methods that require the entire video sequence to make predictions at once, ART-STVG treats the video as streaming input and processes frames sequentially, enabling efficient handling of long videos. To model spatio-temporal context, we design spatial and temporal memory banks and apply them to the decoders. Since memories from different moments are not always relevant to the current frame, we introduce simple yet effective memory selection strategies to provide more relevant information to the decoders, significantly improving performance. Furthermore, instead of parallel spatial and temporal localization, we propose a cascaded spatio-temporal design that connects the spatial decoder to the temporal decoder, allowing fine-grained spatial cues to assist complex temporal localization in long videos. Experiments on newly extended LF-STVG datasets show that ART-STVG significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods, while achieving competitive performance on conventional short-form STVG.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向长时序视频时空定位的研究
在真实场景中，视频时长可达数分钟甚至数小时。然而，现有时空视频定位（STVG）研究在给定文本查询时，主要聚焦于定位数十秒、通常不足一分钟的短视频中的目标，这限制了其实际应用。本文探索长时序STVG（LF-STVG），旨在定位长时序视频中的目标。与短视频相比，长时序视频包含更长的时间跨度和更多无关信息，使得现有一次性处理所有帧的STVG方法难以应对。为解决此挑战，我们提出一种自回归Transformer架构ART-STVG用于LF-STVG。与传统STVG方法需一次性处理完整视频序列不同，ART-STVG将视频视为流式输入，逐帧处理，从而高效处理长视频。为建模时空上下文，我们设计空间与时间记忆库并应用于解码器。由于不同时刻的记忆未必与当前帧相关，我们引入简单而有效的记忆选择策略，为解码器提供更相关的信息，显著提升性能。此外，我们提出级联式时空设计，将空间解码器连接至时间解码器，使精细的空间线索辅助长视频中复杂的时序定位。在新扩展的LF-STVG数据集上的实验表明，ART-STVG显著优于现有最先进方法，同时在传统短时序STVG任务上也保持竞争力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to localize targets in long-form videos—often spanning minutes or hours—this paper addresses the limitations of existing spatio-temporal video grounding methods, which are optimized for short clips under one minute. The authors propose ART-STVG, an AutoRegressive Transformer architecture that processes video frames sequentially as streaming input, avoiding the computational burden of processing entire long videos at once. To capture spatio-temporal context, the model employs spatial and temporal memory banks with adaptive selection mechanisms to filter irrelevant historical information. A cascaded design connects spatial and temporal decoders, allowing spatial cues to refine temporal predictions. Experiments on extended long-form datasets demonstrate that ART-STVG significantly outperforms prior state-of-the-art methods while maintaining competitive performance on short-form benchmarks.
为解决现有时空视频定位方法难以处理长视频（数分钟至数小时）的问题，本文提出ART-STVG，一种面向长视频的自回归Transformer架构。该方法将视频帧作为流式输入逐帧处理，避免一次性处理全部帧导致的效率瓶颈；通过空间与时间记忆库结合选择机制，过滤无关上下文；并采用空间引导时间的级联结构，使空间线索辅助复杂时间定位。在扩展的长视频数据集上实验表明，ART-STVG显著优于现有最先进方法，同时在短视频任务上仍保持竞争力。
Abstracted Gaussian Prototypes for True One-Shot Concept Learning
Authors: Chelsea Zou, Kenneth J. Kurtz
First: 2024-08-30T12:50:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:03:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce a cluster-based generative image segmentation framework to encode higher-level representations of visual concepts based on one-shot learning inspired by the Omniglot Challenge. The inferred parameters of each component of a Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM) represent a distinct topological subpart of a visual concept. Sampling new data from these parameters generates augmented subparts to build a more robust prototype for each concept, i.e., the Abstracted Gaussian Prototype (AGP). This framework addresses one-shot classification tasks using a cognitively-inspired similarity metric and addresses one-shot generative tasks through a novel AGP-VAE pipeline employing variational autoencoders (VAEs) to generate new class variants. Results from human judges reveal that the generative pipeline produces novel examples and classes of visual concepts that are broadly indistinguishable from those made by humans. The proposed framework leads to impressive, but not state-of-the-art, classification accuracy; thus, the contribution is two-fold: 1) the system is low in theoretical and computational complexity yet achieves the standard of 'true' one-shot learning by operating in a fully standalone manner unlike existing approaches that draw heavily on pre-training or knowledge engineering; and 2) in contrast with existing neural network approaches, the AGP approach addresses the importance of broad task capability emphasized in the Omniglot challenge (successful performance on classification and generative tasks). These two points are critical in advancing our understanding of how learning and reasoning systems can produce viable, robust, and flexible concepts based on literally no more than a single example.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于真正单样本概念学习的抽象高斯原型
我们提出了一种基于聚类的生成图像分割框架，受Omniglot挑战启发，通过单样本学习编码视觉概念的高层表示。高斯混合模型（GMM）每个组件的推断参数代表视觉概念的一个独特拓扑子部分。从这些参数采样生成增强子部分，构建每个概念更稳健的原型，即抽象高斯原型（AGP）。该框架通过认知启发的相似度度量解决单样本分类任务，并通过新颖的AGP-VAE管道（使用变分自编码器VAE）解决单样本生成任务。人类评判结果显示，生成管道产生的视觉概念新实例和新类别与人类生成的难以区分。该框架虽取得令人印象深刻但非最先进分类精度，贡献有二：1）系统理论与计算复杂度低，且以完全独立方式运行，不同于依赖预训练或知识工程的现有方法，实现真正的单样本学习；2）与现有神经网络方法不同，AGP方法强调Omniglot挑战中强调的广泛任务能力（分类与生成任务均表现成功）。这两点对推进我们理解学习与推理系统如何仅凭单个示例生成可行、稳健且灵活的概念至关重要。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for truly one-shot visual concept learning as defined by the Omniglot Challenge, this work proposes Abstracted Gaussian Prototypes (AGP), a cluster-based generative framework that uses Gaussian Mixture Models to encode visual concepts from single examples. Each GMM component represents a topological subpart of the concept, and sampling from these parameters generates augmented prototypes to form robust AGPs. The method supports both classification via a cognitively-inspired similarity metric and generation through an AGP-VAE pipeline. Experimental results show that generated examples are indistinguishable from human-made ones, and while classification accuracy is impressive but not state-of-the-art, the framework’s key contributions lie in its low complexity, standalone operation without pre-training, and its dual capability to handle both classification and generation tasks — a rare trait among neural approaches.
为实现真正的一次性视觉概念学习，无需依赖预训练或外部知识，该研究提出抽象高斯原型（AGP）框架，基于高斯混合模型对单例图像进行聚类编码。每个GMM组件代表概念的一个拓扑子部分，通过采样生成增强原型以构建鲁棒表示。该方法支持基于认知启发相似度度量的分类，以及通过AGP-VAE管道进行生成。实验表明生成样本与人类制作样本难以区分，虽然分类精度尚非最优，但其核心贡献在于低复杂度、独立运行能力，以及同时支持分类与生成的广域任务能力——契合Omniglot挑战对全面任务表现的要求。
PGVMS: A Prompt-Guided Unified Framework for Virtual Multiplex IHC Staining with Pathological Semantic Learning
Authors: Fuqiang Chen, Ranran Zhang, Wanming Hu, Deboch Eyob Abera, Yue Peng, Boyun Zheng, Yiwen Sun, Jing Cai, Wenjian Qin
Venue: IEEE Transactions on Medical Imaging, 2026
First: 2026-02-26T18:03:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:03:24+00:00
Comments: Accepted by TMI
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Immunohistochemical (IHC) staining enables precise molecular profiling of protein expression, with over 200 clinically available antibody-based tests in modern pathology. However, comprehensive IHC analysis is frequently limited by insufficient tissue quantities in small biopsies. Therefore, virtual multiplex staining emerges as an innovative solution to digitally transform H&E images into multiple IHC representations, yet current methods still face three critical challenges: (1) inadequate semantic guidance for multi-staining, (2) inconsistent distribution of immunochemistry staining, and (3) spatial misalignment across different stain modalities. To overcome these limitations, we present a prompt-guided framework for virtual multiplex IHC staining using only uniplex training data (PGVMS). Our framework introduces three key innovations corresponding to each challenge: First, an adaptive prompt guidance mechanism employing a pathological visual language model dynamically adjusts staining prompts to resolve semantic guidance limitations (Challenge 1). Second, our protein-aware learning strategy (PALS) maintains precise protein expression patterns by direct quantification and constraint of protein distributions (Challenge 2). Third, the prototype-consistent learning strategy (PCLS) establishes cross-image semantic interaction to correct spatial misalignments (Challenge 3).
中文标题/摘要
标题：PGVMS：一种基于提示引导的统一框架，用于病理语义学习的虚拟多重免疫组化染色
免疫组化（IHC）染色可实现蛋白质表达的精确分子分型，现代病理学中已有超过200种基于抗体的临床检测方法。然而，小活检样本中组织量不足常限制全面的IHC分析。因此，虚拟多重染色作为一种创新方案，可将H&E图像数字化转换为多种IHC表现形式，但现有方法仍面临三大关键挑战：（1）多重染色缺乏语义引导；（2）免疫组化染色分布不一致；（3）不同染色模式间空间错位。为克服这些限制，我们提出仅使用单染色训练数据的提示引导虚拟多重IHC染色框架（PGVMS）。该框架针对每个挑战引入三项关键创新：首先，采用病理视觉语言模型的自适应提示引导机制，动态调整染色提示以解决语义引导不足问题（挑战1）；其次，蛋白质感知学习策略（PALS）通过直接量化与约束蛋白质分布，保持精确的蛋白质表达模式（挑战2）；第三，原型一致学习策略（PCLS）建立跨图像语义交互以校正空间错位（挑战3）。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the clinical need to perform comprehensive IHC analysis despite limited tissue samples, this paper introduces PGVMS, a prompt-guided unified framework for virtual multiplex IHC staining using only uniplex training data. It addresses three key challenges: insufficient semantic guidance, inconsistent protein distribution, and spatial misalignment across stains. The method employs an adaptive prompt guidance mechanism powered by a pathological visual language model to enhance semantic alignment, a protein-aware learning strategy (PALS) to constrain protein expression patterns, and a prototype-consistent learning strategy (PCLS) to correct spatial misalignment through cross-image semantic interaction. Experimental results demonstrate that PGVMS significantly improves staining accuracy and consistency compared to existing methods, achieving superior performance in both qualitative and quantitative evaluations across multiple IHC targets.
为解决小活检样本中组织量不足导致的全面IHC分析受限问题，本文提出PGVMS框架，仅利用单染色训练数据实现虚拟多色IHC染色。针对语义引导不足、染色分布不一致和空间错位三大挑战，PGVMS引入三项创新：基于病理视觉语言模型的自适应提示引导机制、通过直接量化约束蛋白分布的蛋白感知学习策略（PALS），以及建立跨图像语义交互的原型一致学习策略（PCLS）。实验表明，PGVMS在多个基准数据集上显著优于现有方法，有效提升了染色保真度与空间一致性，达到当前最优性能。
LineGraph2Road: Structural Graph Reasoning on Line Graphs for Road Network Extraction
Authors: Zhengyang Wei, Renzhi Jing, Yiyi He, Jenny Suckale
First: 2026-02-26T18:02:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:02:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The accurate and automatic extraction of roads from satellite imagery is critical for applications in navigation and urban planning, significantly reducing the need for manual annotation. Many existing methods decompose this task into keypoint extraction and connectedness prediction, but often struggle to capture long-range dependencies and complex topologies. Here, we propose LineGraph2Road, a framework that improves connectedness prediction by formulating it as binary classification over edges in a constructed global but sparse Euclidean graph, where nodes are keypoints extracted from segmentation masks and edges connect node pairs within a predefined distance threshold, representing potential road segments. To better learn structural link representation, we transform the original graph into its corresponding line graph and apply a Graph Transformer on it for connectedness prediction. This formulation overcomes the limitations of endpoint-embedding fusion on set-isomorphic links, enabling rich link representations and effective relational reasoning over the global structure. Additionally, we introduce an overpass/underpass head to resolve multi-level crossings and a coupled NMS strategy to preserve critical connections. We evaluate LineGraph2Road on three benchmarks: City-scale, SpaceNet, and Global-scale, and show that it achieves state-of-the-art results on two key metrics, TOPO-F1 and APLS. It also captures fine visual details critical for real-world deployment. We will make our code publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LineGraph2Road：基于线图结构图推理的道路网络提取
从卫星图像中准确自动提取道路对导航和城市规划应用至关重要，可大幅减少人工标注需求。许多现有方法将该任务分解为关键点提取和连通性预测，但常难以捕捉长距离依赖和复杂拓扑结构。本文提出LineGraph2Road框架，通过将连通性预测建模为构建的全局稀疏欧几里得图中边的二分类问题来提升预测效果，其中节点为从分割掩码中提取的关键点，边连接预设距离阈值内的节点对，代表潜在道路段。为更好地学习结构链接表示，我们将原始图转换为其对应的线图，并在该图上应用图变换器进行连通性预测。该建模方式克服了端点嵌入融合在集合同构链接上的局限性，实现丰富的链接表示和全局结构上的有效关系推理。此外，我们引入过路/穿行头以解决多层交叉，以及耦合NMS策略以保留关键连接。我们在City-scale、SpaceNet和Global-scale三个基准上评估LineGraph2Road，结果在TOPO-F1和APLS两个关键指标上达到当前最优，同时捕捉到对实际部署至关重要的细粒度视觉细节。我们将公开代码。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for accurate, automated road extraction from satellite imagery to support navigation and urban planning, this paper introduces LineGraph2Road, a method that enhances connectedness prediction by modeling road segments as edges in a sparse Euclidean graph built from detected keypoints. The framework transforms this graph into its line graph and applies a Graph Transformer to learn structural link representations, overcoming limitations of traditional endpoint fusion. It further incorporates an overpass/underpass head and coupled NMS to handle crossings and preserve critical connections. Evaluated on City-scale, SpaceNet, and Global-scale benchmarks, LineGraph2Road achieves state-of-the-art performance on TOPO-F1 and APLS metrics while preserving fine visual details essential for real-world applications.
为支持导航与城市规划，自动从卫星图像中精确提取道路至关重要，现有方法常难以建模长距离依赖与复杂拓扑结构。LineGraph2Road将连通性预测重构为稀疏欧几里得图中边的二分类任务，图节点由分割掩码提取的关键点构成，边连接预设距离内的点对。通过将其转换为线图并应用图变换器，该框架有效学习结构化链接表示，克服端点嵌入融合在集合同构链接上的局限。引入过路/立交头与耦合NMS策略以处理多层交叉并保留关键连接。在City-scale、SpaceNet与Global-scale三个基准上，其在TOPO-F1与APLS两项关键指标上达到最先进水平，同时保留对实际部署至关重要的细粒度视觉细节。
BRIDGE: Borderless Reconfiguration for Inclusive and Diverse Gameplay Experience via Embodiment Transformation
Authors: Hayato Saiki, Chunggi Lee, Hikari Takahashi, Tica Lin, Hidetada Kishi, Kaori Tachibana, Yasuhiro Suzuki, Hanspeter Pfister, Kenji Suzuki
First: 2026-02-26T18:01:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:01:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training resources for parasports are limited, reducing opportunities for athletes and coaches to engage with sport-specific movements and tactical coordination. To address this gap, we developed BRIDGE, a system that integrates a reconstruction pipeline, which detects and tracks players from broadcast video to generate 3D play sequences, with an embodiment-aware visualization framework that decomposes head, trunk, and wheelchair base orientations to represent attention, intent, and mobility. We evaluated BRIDGE in two controlled studies with 20 participants (10 national wheelchair basketball team players and 10 amateur players). The results showed that BRIDGE significantly enhanced the perceived naturalness of player postures and made tactical intentions easier to understand. In addition, it supported functional classification by realistically conveying players' capabilities, which in turn improved participants' sense of self-efficacy. This work advances inclusive sports learning and accessible coaching practices, contributing to more equitable access to tactical resources in parasports.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BRIDGE：通过具身转换实现无边界重构，促进包容性与多样化的游戏体验
残障体育训练资源有限，降低了运动员和教练员接触专项动作与战术协调的机会。为解决这一问题，我们开发了BRIDGE系统，该系统整合了从广播视频中检测并追踪球员以生成三维比赛序列的重建流程，以及一个具身感知的可视化框架，该框架将头部、躯干和轮椅基座的姿态分解，以表征注意力、意图和移动性。我们在20名参与者（10名国家轮椅篮球队员和10名业余球员）的两项受控研究中评估了BRIDGE。结果表明，BRIDGE显著提升了球员姿态的自然感，并使战术意图更易理解。此外，它通过真实传达球员能力，支持功能分级，从而增强了参与者的自我效能感。本研究推动了包容性体育学习与无障碍教练实践，促进了残障体育中战术资源的更公平获取。

Motivated by the scarcity of training resources for parasports, BRIDGE was designed to enhance coaching and learning through embodied visualization. The system combines a video reconstruction pipeline that tracks players from broadcast footage to generate 3D play sequences, with an embodiment-aware framework that decomposes head, trunk, and wheelchair base orientations to convey attention, intent, and mobility. In two controlled studies with 20 participants—10 elite wheelchair basketball players and 10 amateurs—BRIDGE significantly improved perceived naturalness of player postures and clarity of tactical intent, while also supporting functional classification by accurately reflecting players’ capabilities, thereby boosting participants’ self-efficacy.
