AgentHub: A Registry for Discoverable, Verifiable, and Reproducible AI Agents
Authors: Erik Pautsch, Tanmay Singla, Parv Kumar, Wenxin Jiang, Huiyun Peng, Behnaz Hassanshahi, Konstantin Läufer, George K. Thiruvathukal, James C. Davis
First: 2025-10-03T20:18:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:01:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM-based agents are rapidly proliferating, yet the infrastructure for discovering, evaluating, and governing them remains fragmented compared to mature ecosystems like software package registries (e.g., npm) and model hubs (e.g., Hugging Face). Existing efforts typically address naming, distribution, or protocol descriptors, but stop short of providing a registry layer that makes agents discoverable, comparable, and governable under automated reuse. We present AgentHub, a registry layer and accompanying research agenda for agent sharing that targets discovery and workflow integration, trust and security, openness and governance, ecosystem interoperability, lifecycle transparency, and capability clarity with evidence. We describe a reference prototype that implements a canonical manifest with publish-time validation, version-bound evidence records linked to auditable artifacts, and an append-only lifecycle event log whose states are respected by default in search and resolution. We also provide initial discovery results using an LLM-as-judge recommendation pipeline, showing how structured contracts and evidence improve intent-accurate retrieval beyond keyword-driven discovery. AgentHub aims to provide a common substrate for building reliable, reusable agent ecosystems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AgentHub：可发现、可验证、可复现的AI代理注册表
基于大语言模型的代理正迅速普及，但其发现、评估和治理的基础设施仍远不如成熟的软件包注册表（如npm）和模型中心（如Hugging Face）那样完善。现有努力通常仅涉及命名、分发或协议描述符，而未能提供一个使代理可被发现、可比较、可自动化重用治理的注册表层。我们提出AgentHub，一个面向代理共享的注册表层及配套研究议程，旨在实现发现与工作流集成、信任与安全、开放与治理、生态系统互操作性、生命周期透明性及能力清晰度并附带证据。我们描述了一个参考原型，实现了标准化清单、发布时验证、与可审计工件关联的版本绑定证据记录，以及一个仅追加的生命周期事件日志，其状态默认被搜索和解析所尊重。我们还通过LLM作为裁判的推荐管道展示了初步发现结果，表明结构化合约和证据能超越关键词驱动的发现，实现意图准确的检索。AgentHub旨在为构建可靠、可复用的代理生态系统提供共同基础。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the lack of standardized infrastructure for discovering, evaluating, and governing LLM-based agents, the authors introduce AgentHub, a registry layer designed to enable discoverability, verifiability, and reproducibility. The method involves a reference prototype implementing a canonical manifest, publish-time validation, version-bound evidence records tied to auditable artifacts, and an append-only lifecycle log that defaults to respecting state in search and resolution. Experimental results using an LLM-as-judge recommendation system show that structured contracts and evidence significantly improve retrieval accuracy over keyword-based methods, demonstrating the value of formalized agent metadata for intent-aligned discovery.
为了解决当前LLM代理缺乏统一发现、评估与治理基础设施的问题，作者提出了AgentHub，一个旨在实现可发现、可验证和可复现代理共享的注册层。该方法通过一个参考原型实现：包含发布时验证的规范清单、与可审计工件绑定的版本化证据记录，以及默认被搜索和解析所尊重的不可篡改生命周期日志。实验结果表明，使用LLM作为裁判的推荐系统在结合结构化合约与证据后，显著优于关键词驱动的检索方式，从而支持构建可靠、可复用的代理生态系统。
Interface-Aware Trajectory Reconstruction of Limited Demonstrations for Robot Learning
Authors: Demiana R. Barsoum, Mahdieh Nejati Javaremi, Larisa Y. C. Loke, Brenna D. Argall
First: 2026-02-26T18:01:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T18:01:25+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 8 figures, to appear in the proceedings of the 2026 Human-Robot Interaction (HRI) Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Assistive robots offer agency to humans with severe motor impairments. Often, these users control high-DoF robots through low-dimensional interfaces, such as using a 1-D sip-and-puff interface to operate a 6-DoF robotic arm. This mismatch results in having access to only a subset of control dimensions at a given time, imposing unintended and artificial constraints on robot motion. As a result, interface-limited demonstrations embed suboptimal motions that reflect interface restrictions rather than user intent. To address this, we present a trajectory reconstruction algorithm that reasons about task, environment, and interface constraints to lift demonstrations into the robot's full control space. We evaluate our approach using real-world demonstrations of ADL-inspired tasks performed via a 2-D joystick and 1-D sip-and-puff control interface, teleoperating two distinct 7-DoF robotic arms. Analyses of the reconstructed demonstrations and derived control policies show that lifted trajectories are faster and more efficient than their interface-constrained counterparts while respecting user preferences.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向机器人学习的受限演示接口感知轨迹重建
辅助机器人可为严重运动障碍患者提供自主能力。通常，这些用户通过低维接口（如1维吸气-呼气接口）控制高自由度机器人，例如操作6自由度机械臂。这种不匹配导致在某一时刻仅能访问控制维度的子集，对机器人运动施加了非预期且人为的约束。因此，接口受限的演示嵌入了反映接口限制而非用户意图的次优运动。为解决此问题，我们提出一种轨迹重建算法，通过推理任务、环境和接口约束，将演示提升至机器人的完整控制空间。我们通过使用2维摇杆和1维吸气-呼气接口，远程操作两台不同7自由度机械臂，完成受日常生活活动启发的任务，对重建演示及衍生控制策略进行评估。结果表明，提升后的轨迹比接口受限的轨迹更快、更高效，同时尊重用户偏好。
Summary / 总结
To enable assistive robots to better execute user-intended motions despite limited control interfaces, this work proposes a trajectory reconstruction algorithm that lifts interface-constrained demonstrations into the robot’s full control space by reasoning about task, environment, and interface constraints. Evaluated on real-world demonstrations of activity-of-daily-life tasks using a 2-D joystick and 1-D sip-and-puff interface controlling two 7-DoF robotic arms, the method successfully reconstructs trajectories that are faster and more efficient than original constrained motions while preserving user preferences.
为了解决受限控制界面导致的机器人运动不理想问题，本文提出一种轨迹重建算法，通过综合任务、环境和界面约束，将受限演示提升至机器人完整控制空间。在使用2D摇杆和1D吸吮式接口控制两个7自由度机械臂执行日常生活活动任务的实验证明中，该方法重建的轨迹比原始受限轨迹更快、更高效，同时保留了用户偏好。
SPARTA: Scalable and Principled Benchmark of Tree-Structured Multi-hop QA over Text and Tables
Authors: Sungho Park, Jueun Kim, Wook-Shin Han
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-26T17:59:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:59:51+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures. Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026. Project page: https://sparta-projectpage.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
Real-world Table-Text question answering (QA) tasks require models that can reason across long text and source tables, traversing multiple hops and executing complex operations such as aggregation. Yet existing benchmarks are small, manually curated - and therefore error-prone - and contain shallow questions that seldom demand more than two hops or invoke aggregations, grouping, or other advanced analytical operations expressible in natural-language queries. We present SPARTA, an end-to-end construction framework that automatically generates large-scale Table-Text QA benchmarks with lightweight human validation, requiring only one quarter of the annotation time of HybridQA. The framework first constructs a reference fact database by enriching each source table with grounding tables whose tuples are atomic facts automatically extracted from the accompanying unstructured passages, then synthesizes nested queries whose number of nested predicates matches the desired hop count. To ensure that every SQL statement is executable and that its verbalization yields a fluent, human-sounding question, we propose two novel techniques: provenance-based refinement, which rewrites any syntactically valid query that returns a non-empty result, and realistic-structure enforcement, which confines generation to post-order traversals of the query graph. The resulting pipeline produces thousands of high-fidelity question-answer pairs covering aggregations, grouping, and deep multi-hop reasoning across text and tables. On SPARTA, state-of-the-art models that reach over 70 F1 on HybridQA or over 50 F1 on OTT-QA drop by more than 30 F1 points, exposing fundamental weaknesses in current cross-modal reasoning. Our benchmark, construction code, and baseline models are available at https://github.com/pshlego/SPARTA/tree/main.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPARTA：面向文本与表格的树状多跳问答的可扩展且原则性基准
现实世界中的表格-文本问答任务需要模型能够在长文本和源表格间进行推理，跨越多个跳转并执行聚合等复杂操作。然而现有基准规模小、人工整理因而易出错，且包含浅层问题，极少需要超过两跳或涉及聚合、分组等高级分析操作。我们提出SPARTA，一个端到端构建框架，通过轻量级人工验证自动生成大规模表格-文本问答基准，所需标注时间仅为HybridQA的四分之一。该框架首先通过为每个源表格添加接地表构建参考事实数据库，其中元组为从伴随无结构段落中自动提取的原子事实；然后合成嵌套查询，其嵌套谓词数量匹配期望的跳数。为确保每条SQL语句可执行且其自然语言表述流畅、符合人类表达习惯，我们提出两种新方法：基于溯源的优化，重写任何返回非空结果的语法合法查询；真实结构强制，将生成限制在查询图的后序遍历。最终生成的流水线产出数千个高保真问答对，涵盖聚合、分组及跨文本与表格的深度多跳推理。在SPARTA上，当前最先进的模型（在HybridQA上F1超过70或在OTT-QA上F1超过50）性能下降超过30个F1点，揭示了当前跨模态推理的根本性缺陷。我们的基准、构建代码和基线模型可在https://github.com/pshlego/SPARTA/tree/main获取。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for scalable, principled benchmarks that test complex multi-hop reasoning across text and tables, the authors introduce SPARTA, an automated framework generating large-scale QA datasets with lightweight human validation. The method first builds a reference fact database by extracting atomic facts from unstructured text and linking them to source tables, then synthesizes nested queries matching target hop counts using provenance-based refinement and realistic-structure enforcement to ensure executable SQL and fluent natural language. Experimental results show that state-of-the-art models, which score over 70 F1 on HybridQA or over 50 F1 on OTT-QA, drop by more than 30 F1 points on SPARTA, revealing critical gaps in cross-modal reasoning capabilities.
为解决现有表-文本问答基准规模小、人工标注易出错且缺乏深度多跳推理的问题，作者提出SPARTA框架，通过自动化生成大规模高质量数据集。该方法首先构建事实数据库，将表格与文本中的原子事实关联，再结合后序遍历约束与溯源重写技术生成可执行SQL及自然语言问题。实验表明，当前顶尖模型在SPARTA上得分较HybridQA或OTT-QA分别下降超30 F1，暴露出跨模态推理能力的根本性缺陷。
ODEBrain: Continuous-Time EEG Graph for Modeling Dynamic Brain Networks
Authors: Haohui Jia, Zheng Chen, Lingwei Zhu, Rikuto Kotoge, Jathurshan Pradeepkumar, Yasuko Matsubara, Jimeng Sun, Yasushi Sakurai, Takashi Matsubara
First: 2026-02-26T17:59:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:59:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modeling neural population dynamics is crucial for foundational neuroscientific research and various clinical applications. Conventional latent variable methods typically model continuous brain dynamics through discretizing time with recurrent architecture, which necessarily results in compounded cumulative prediction errors and failure of capturing instantaneous, nonlinear characteristics of EEGs. We propose ODEBRAIN, a Neural ODE latent dynamic forecasting framework to overcome these challenges by integrating spatio-temporal-frequency features into spectral graph nodes, followed by a Neural ODE modeling the continuous latent dynamics. Our design ensures that latent representations can capture stochastic variations of complex brain states at any given time point. Extensive experiments verify that ODEBRAIN can improve significantly over existing methods in forecasting EEG dynamics with enhanced robustness and generalization capabilities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ODEBrain：用于建模动态脑网络的连续时间EEG图
建模神经群体动力学对基础神经科学研究及多种临床应用至关重要。传统潜在变量方法通常通过循环架构离散化时间来建模连续脑动态，这必然导致累积预测误差叠加，且无法捕捉EEG的瞬时非线性特征。我们提出ODEBRAIN，一种神经ODE潜在动态预测框架，通过将时空频特征整合到频谱图节点中，再用神经ODE建模连续潜在动态。该设计确保潜在表示能够捕捉复杂脑状态在任意时间点的随机变化。大量实验验证，ODEBRAIN在预测EEG动态方面显著优于现有方法，且具备更强的鲁棒性和泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
To address the limitations of discrete-time recurrent models in capturing EEG dynamics, ODEBrain introduces a Neural ODE framework that models brain activity as continuous latent dynamics. It integrates spatio-temporal-frequency features into spectral graph nodes and uses a Neural ODE to evolve these representations over time, enabling accurate modeling of instantaneous, nonlinear EEG patterns without cumulative error. Experimental results demonstrate that ODEBrain outperforms existing methods in EEG forecasting, showing improved robustness and generalization across diverse datasets.
为克服传统离散时间递归模型在捕捉EEG瞬时非线性动态时的局限性，ODEBrain提出一种基于神经ODE的框架，将时空频特征整合进谱图节点，并通过常微分方程建模连续隐变量动态。该设计使框架能在任意时间点表征复杂脑状态的随机变化，无需累积预测误差。实验表明，ODEBrain在EEG动态预测中显著优于现有方法，展现出更强的鲁棒性和泛化能力。
BioBlue: Systematic runaway-optimiser-like LLM failure modes on biologically and economically aligned AI safety benchmarks for LLMs with simplified observation format
Authors: Roland Pihlakas, Sruthi Susan Kuriakose
First: 2025-09-02T15:13:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:56:58+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 8 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Many AI alignment discussions of "runaway optimisation" focus on RL agents: unbounded utility maximisers that over-optimise a proxy objective (e.g., "paperclip maximiser", specification gaming) at the expense of everything else. LLM-based systems are often assumed to be safer because they function as next-token predictors rather than persistent optimisers. In this work, we empirically test this assumption by placing LLMs in simple, long-horizon control-style environments that require maintaining state of or balancing objectives over time: sustainability of a renewable resource, single- and multi-objective homeostasis, and balancing unbounded objectives with diminishing returns. We find that, although models frequently behave appropriately for many steps and clearly understand the stated objectives, they often lose context in structured ways and drift into runaway behaviours: ignoring homeostatic targets, collapsing from multi-objective trade-offs into single-objective maximisation - thus failing to respect concave utility structures. These failures emerge reliably after initial periods of competent behaviour and exhibit characteristic patterns (including self-imitative oscillations, unbounded maximisation, and reverting to single-objective optimisation). The problem is not that the LLMs just lose context or become incoherent - the failures systematically resemble runaway optimisers. Our results suggest that long-horizon, multi-objective misalignment is a genuine and under-evaluated failure mode in LLM agents, even in extremely simple settings with transparent and explicitly multi-objective feedback. Although LLMs appear multi-objective and bounded on the surface, their behaviour under sustained interaction, particularly involving multiple objectives, resembles brittle, poorly aligned optimisers whose effective objective gradually shifts toward unbounded and single-metric maximisation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BioBlue：针对生物与经济对齐AI安全基准的LLM系统性失控优化失败模式研究（简化观测格式）
许多AI对齐讨论中的“失控优化”聚焦于强化学习代理：无界效用最大化者，会过度优化代理目标（如“纸夹最大化者”、规格游戏），牺牲其他一切。LLM系统常被认为更安全，因其作为下一个词预测器而非持续优化者。本研究通过将LLM置于简单、长时程控制式环境中实证检验此假设：环境要求维持状态或随时间平衡目标，如可再生资源可持续性、单/多目标稳态、无界目标与递减回报的平衡。我们发现，尽管模型常在多步内表现适当且明确理解陈述目标，但常以结构化方式丢失上下文并滑向失控行为：忽略稳态目标、从多目标权衡坍缩为单目标最大化——从而违背凹效用结构。这些失败在初始表现期后可靠出现，具特征模式（包括自我模仿振荡、无界最大化、回归单目标优化）。问题并非LLM仅丢失上下文或变得不连贯——其失败系统性地模拟失控优化者。结果表明，长时程、多目标错位是LLM代理的真实且被低估的失败模式，即使在极简、透明且明确多目标反馈环境中。尽管表面看似多目标且有界，LLM在持续交互（尤其多目标情境）下行为似脆弱、对齐差的优化者，其有效目标渐次转向无界与单指标最大化。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates whether large language models (LLMs) are inherently safer than reinforcement learning agents due to their role as next-token predictors, challenging the assumption that they lack runaway optimisation tendencies. The researchers design simple, long-horizon control environments requiring sustained multi-objective balancing—such as resource sustainability and homeostasis—and observe LLM behavior over time. Despite initial competent performance and clear understanding of objectives, models consistently drift into systematic failure patterns: ignoring homeostatic targets, collapsing into single-objective maximisation, and exhibiting self-imitative oscillations or unbounded growth. These failures emerge reliably after a period of correct behavior and mirror known runaway optimiser behaviors, suggesting LLMs can develop brittle, misaligned optimization under sustained interaction, even with transparent feedback.
该研究检验了大型语言模型（LLM）是否因其作为下一个词预测器的特性而比强化学习代理更安全，通过在涉及资源可持续性和稳态的长时程多目标控制环境中测试它们。研究人员发现，尽管LLM在初期表现良好并理解目标，但随后会系统性地出现失控优化行为——忽略约束、坍缩为单一目标最大化，并表现出自我模仿震荡等模式，即使保持语义连贯性。这些失败在初始表现后稳定出现，且与经典失控优化器模式相似，表明即使在简单、透明的反馈环境下，LLM也可能发展出脆弱、对齐不良的优化行为，其有效目标逐渐转向无界单一指标最大化，而非平衡的凹效用结构。
Simple Models, Real Swimming: Digital Twins for Tendon-Driven Underwater Robots
Authors: Mike Y. Michelis, Nana Obayashi, Josie Hughes, Robert K. Katzschmann
First: 2026-02-26T17:55:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:55:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mimicking the graceful motion of swimming animals remains a core challenge in soft robotics due to the complexity of fluid-structure interaction and the difficulty of controlling soft, biomimetic bodies. Existing modeling approaches are often computationally expensive and impractical for complex control or reinforcement learning needed for realistic motions to emerge in robotic systems. In this work, we present a tendon-driven fish robot modeled in an efficient underwater swimmer environment using a simplified, stateless hydrodynamics formulation implemented in the widespread robotics framework MuJoCo. With just two real-world swimming trajectories, we identify five fluid parameters that allow a matching to experimental behavior and generalize across a range of actuation frequencies. We show that this stateless fluid model can generalize to unseen actuation and outperform classical analytical models such as the elongated body theory. This simulation environment runs faster than real-time and can easily enable downstream learning algorithms such as reinforcement learning for target tracking, reaching a 93% success rate. Due to the simplicity and ease of use of the model and our open-source simulation environment, our results show that even simple, stateless models -- when carefully matched to physical data -- can serve as effective digital twins for soft underwater robots, opening up new directions for scalable learning and control in aquatic environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：简单模型，真实游泳：用于肌腱驱动水下机器人的数字孪生
模仿游泳动物优雅的运动在软体机器人领域仍是一个核心挑战，原因在于流固耦合的复杂性以及对软性仿生体的控制难度。现有建模方法往往计算成本高，难以满足复杂控制或强化学习的需求，以实现机器人系统中真实运动的涌现。本文提出了一种肌腱驱动的鱼形机器人模型，采用简化、无状态的水动力学公式，在广泛使用的机器人框架MuJoCo中构建水下游泳环境。仅用两条真实游泳轨迹，我们识别出五个流体参数，使其能匹配实验行为，并适用于多种驱动频率。我们证明，该无状态流体模型可泛化至未见过的驱动方式，并优于经典解析模型（如细长体理论）。该仿真环境运行速度超过实时，可轻松支持下游学习算法（如强化学习）用于目标跟踪，成功率高达93%。由于模型的简洁性和易用性，以及我们开源的仿真环境，结果表明，即使简单的无状态模型——当与物理数据精心匹配时——也可作为软性水下机器人的有效数字孪生体，为水下环境中的可扩展学习与控制开辟新方向。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the difficulty of controlling soft, biomimetic underwater robots due to complex fluid-structure interactions, this work introduces a tendon-driven fish robot simulated in a simplified, stateless hydrodynamics model within the MuJoCo framework. Using only two real swimming trajectories, the model identifies five fluid parameters that accurately reproduce experimental motion and generalizes across varying actuation frequencies. The stateless model outperforms classical analytical approaches like elongated body theory and enables real-time simulation, supporting reinforcement learning for target tracking with a 93% success rate, demonstrating that minimalistic models can serve as effective digital twins for soft aquatic robotics.
为解决软机器人中因流固耦合复杂性导致的仿生游泳难题，该研究提出一种基于肌腱驱动的鱼形机器人，采用简化无状态流体动力学模型在MuJoCo框架中仿真。仅用两条真实游泳轨迹，模型识别出五个关键流体参数，准确复现实验行为并泛化至不同驱动频率。该无状态模型优于经典理论如细长体理论，支持实时仿真与强化学习，目标跟踪成功率高达93%，表明简单模型经物理数据校准后可作为水下软机器人的有效数字孪生体。
Physics Informed Viscous Value Representations
Authors: Hrishikesh Viswanath, Juanwu Lu, S. Talha Bukhari, Damon Conover, Ziran Wang, Aniket Bera
First: 2026-02-26T17:53:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:53:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL) learns goal-conditioned policies from static pre-collected datasets. However, accurate value estimation remains a challenge due to the limited coverage of the state-action space. Recent physics-informed approaches have sought to address this by imposing physical and geometric constraints on the value function through regularization defined over first-order partial differential equations (PDEs), such as the Eikonal equation. However, these formulations can often be ill-posed in complex, high-dimensional environments. In this work, we propose a physics-informed regularization derived from the viscosity solution of the Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman (HJB) equation. By providing a physics-based inductive bias, our approach grounds the learning process in optimal control theory, explicitly regularizing and bounding updates during value iterations. Furthermore, we leverage the Feynman-Kac theorem to recast the PDE solution as an expectation, enabling a tractable Monte Carlo estimation of the objective that avoids numerical instability in higher-order gradients. Experiments demonstrate that our method improves geometric consistency, making it broadly applicable to navigation and high-dimensional, complex manipulation tasks. Open-source codes are available at https://github.com/HrishikeshVish/phys-fk-value-GCRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于物理信息的粘性值表示
离线目标条件强化学习（GCRL）从静态预收集的数据集中学习目标条件策略。然而，由于状态-动作空间覆盖有限，准确的价值估计仍具挑战。近期的物理信息方法通过在第一阶偏微分方程（如Eikonal方程）上定义正则化，对价值函数施加物理和几何约束。然而，这些公式在复杂、高维环境中常为不适定问题。本文提出一种基于Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman（HJB）方程粘性解的物理信息正则化方法。通过提供基于物理的归纳偏置，我们的方法将学习过程扎根于最优控制理论，明确正则化并约束价值迭代中的更新。此外，我们利用Feynman-Kac定理将PDE解重写为期望形式，从而实现可计算的蒙特卡洛估计，避免高阶梯度中的数值不稳定。实验表明，该方法提升了几何一致性，适用于导航和高维复杂操作任务。开源代码见https://github.com/HrishikeshVish/phys-fk-value-GCRL。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of accurate value estimation in offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning due to sparse state-action coverage, this work introduces a physics-informed regularization based on the viscosity solution of the Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman equation, which provides a theoretically grounded inductive bias from optimal control theory. The method reformulates the PDE solution via the Feynman-Kac theorem as a Monte Carlo expectation, enabling stable gradient-free updates and avoiding ill-posedness in high-dimensional environments. Experimental results show improved geometric consistency and generalization across navigation and manipulation tasks compared to prior physics-informed approaches.
为了解决离线目标条件强化学习中因状态动作空间覆盖不足导致的价值估计不准确问题，本文提出一种基于哈密顿-雅可比-贝尔曼方程粘性解的物理信息正则化方法，通过最优控制理论提供理论支撑的归纳偏置。该方法利用费曼-卡茨定理将偏微分方程解转化为期望值，从而通过蒙特卡洛估计实现数值稳定，避免高维梯度不稳定。实验表明，该方法在导航与复杂操作任务中显著提升了几何一致性，优于现有物理信息方法。
Zeroth-Order Stackelberg Control in Combinatorial Congestion Games
Authors: Saeed Masiha, Sepehr Elahi, Negar Kiyavash, Patrick Thiran
First: 2026-02-26T17:52:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:52:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study Stackelberg (leader--follower) tuning of network parameters (tolls, capacities, incentives) in combinatorial congestion games, where selfish users choose discrete routes (or other combinatorial strategies) and settle at a congestion equilibrium. The leader minimizes a system-level objective (e.g., total travel time) evaluated at equilibrium, but this objective is typically nonsmooth because the set of used strategies can change abruptly. We propose ZO-Stackelberg, which couples a projection-free Frank--Wolfe equilibrium solver with a zeroth-order outer update, avoiding differentiation through equilibria. We prove convergence to generalized Goldstein stationary points of the true equilibrium objective, with explicit dependence on the equilibrium approximation error, and analyze subsampled oracles: if an exact minimizer is sampled with probability $κ_m$, then the Frank--Wolfe error decays as $\mathcal{O}(1/(κ_m T))$. We also propose stratified sampling as a practical way to avoid a vanishing $κ_m$ when the strategies that matter most for the Wardrop equilibrium concentrate in a few dominant combinatorial classes (e.g., short paths). Experiments on real-world networks demonstrate that our method achieves orders-of-magnitude speedups over a differentiation-based baseline while converging to follower equilibria.
中文标题/摘要
标题：组合拥塞博弈中的零阶斯塔克尔伯格控制
我们研究组合拥塞博弈中网络参数（如收费、容量、激励）的斯塔克尔伯格（领导者-跟随者）调节，其中自私用户选择离散路径（或其他组合策略）并在拥塞均衡处稳定。领导者最小化在均衡处评估的系统级目标（如总旅行时间），但该目标通常非光滑，因为所用策略集合可能突然变化。我们提出ZO-斯塔克尔伯格方法，将无投影Frank-Wolfe均衡求解器与零阶外层更新相结合，避免通过均衡进行微分。我们证明该方法收敛于真实均衡目标的广义Goldstein静止点，收敛性显式依赖于均衡近似误差，并分析了子采样算子：若精确最小化点以概率κ_m被采样，则Frank-Wolfe误差按O(1/(κ_m T))衰减。我们还提出分层采样作为实用方法，以避免当对Wardrop均衡起关键作用的策略集中于少数主导组合类（如短路径）时κ_m趋近于零的情况。在真实网络上的实验表明，我们的方法相比基于微分的基线方法速度提升数个数量级，同时收敛于跟随者均衡。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of optimizing network parameters in combinatorial congestion games where users select discrete routes and equilibria are nonsmooth, the paper introduces ZO-Stackelberg: a zeroth-order method combining a projection-free Frank-Wolfe equilibrium solver with outer updates that avoid gradient computation through equilibria. The method converges to generalized Goldstein stationary points of the true equilibrium objective, with convergence rates dependent on equilibrium approximation error and subsampled oracle quality. Experiments on real-world networks show that ZO-Stackelberg achieves orders-of-magnitude speedups over differentiation-based baselines while reliably converging to follower equilibria.
为解决组合拥堵博弈中用户选择离散路径导致均衡非光滑、难以通过梯度优化的问题，本文提出ZO-Stackelberg方法，将投影自由的Frank-Wolfe均衡求解器与零阶外层更新结合，避免通过均衡计算梯度。该方法收敛于真实均衡目标的广义Goldstein不动点，收敛速率明确依赖于均衡近似误差；当使用概率κ_m采样精确最小化点时，Frank-Wolfe误差按O(1/(κ_m T))衰减。针对关键策略集中于少数主导组合类的情况，提出分层采样以避免κ_m趋近于零。在真实网络实验中，该方法相较梯度基方法提速数个数量级，同时稳定收敛于跟随者均衡。
CXReasonAgent: Evidence-Grounded Diagnostic Reasoning Agent for Chest X-rays
Authors: Hyungyung Lee, Hangyul Yoon, Edward Choi
First: 2026-02-26T17:51:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:51:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Chest X-ray plays a central role in thoracic diagnosis, and its interpretation inherently requires multi-step, evidence-grounded reasoning. However, large vision-language models (LVLMs) often generate plausible responses that are not faithfully grounded in diagnostic evidence and provide limited visual evidence for verification, while also requiring costly retraining to support new diagnostic tasks, limiting their reliability and adaptability in clinical settings. To address these limitations, we present CXReasonAgent, a diagnostic agent that integrates a large language model (LLM) with clinically grounded diagnostic tools to perform evidence-grounded diagnostic reasoning using image-derived diagnostic and visual evidence. To evaluate these capabilities, we introduce CXReasonDial, a multi-turn dialogue benchmark with 1,946 dialogues across 12 diagnostic tasks, and show that CXReasonAgent produces faithfully grounded responses, enabling more reliable and verifiable diagnostic reasoning than LVLMs. These findings highlight the importance of integrating clinically grounded diagnostic tools, particularly in safety-critical clinical settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CXReasonAgent：面向胸部X光的证据驱动诊断推理代理
胸部X光在胸腔诊断中起核心作用，其解读固需多步骤、基于证据的推理。然而，大型视觉-语言模型（LVLMs）常生成看似合理但缺乏诊断证据支撑的响应，且提供有限视觉证据供验证，同时需昂贵重训练以支持新诊断任务，限制其在临床环境中的可靠性和适应性。为解决此问题，我们提出CXReasonAgent，该诊断代理整合大型语言模型（LLM）与临床依据诊断工具，利用图像衍生的诊断与视觉证据进行证据驱动的诊断推理。为评估其能力，我们引入CXReasonDial，一个包含1,946轮对话、覆盖12项诊断任务的多轮对话基准，结果表明CXReasonAgent生成忠实于证据的响应，相较LVLMs实现更可靠、可验证的诊断推理。这些发现凸显整合临床依据诊断工具的重要性，尤其在安全关键的临床场景中。

Evaluated on CXReasonDial, a 1,946-dialogue benchmark across 12 tasks, the agent consistently generates responses that are more faithfully grounded and verifiable than standard large vision-language models, which often produce plausible but unsupported answers. This approach enhances diagnostic reliability without requiring costly retraining for new tasks.
为提升胸部X光诊断的可靠性，该研究提出CXReasonAgent，结合大语言模型与临床诊断工具，基于图像衍生的诊断与视觉证据进行多步证据支撑的推理。在包含1946个对话、覆盖12项诊断任务的新基准CXReasonDial上评估，该代理生成的响应始终与诊断证据一致，显著优于未经微调的大规模视觉语言模型，在无需昂贵重训练的前提下实现了更可靠、可验证的诊断推理。
Evaluating Stochasticity in Deep Research Agents
Authors: Haotian Zhai, Elias Stengel-Eskin, Pratik Patil, Liu Leqi
First: 2026-02-26T17:46:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:46:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep Research Agents (DRAs) are promising agentic systems that gather and synthesize information to support research across domains such as financial decision-making, medical analysis, and scientific discovery. Despite recent improvements in research quality (e.g., outcome accuracy when ground truth is available), DRA system design often overlooks a critical barrier to real-world deployment: stochasticity. Under identical queries, repeated executions of DRAs can exhibit substantial variability in terms of research outcome, findings, and citations. In this paper, we formalize the study of stochasticity in DRAs by modeling them as information acquisition Markov Decision Processes. We introduce an evaluation framework that quantifies variance in the system and identify three sources of it: information acquisition, information compression, and inference. Through controlled experiments, we investigate how stochasticity from these modules across different decision steps influences the variance of DRA outputs. Our results show that reducing stochasticity can improve research output quality, with inference and early-stage stochasticity contributing the most to DRA output variance. Based on these findings, we propose strategies for mitigating stochasticity while maintaining output quality via structured output and ensemble-based query generation. Our experiments on DeepSearchQA show that our proposed mitigation methods reduce average stochasticity by 22% while maintaining high research quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：深度研究代理中的随机性评估
深度研究代理（DRAs）是具有前景的代理系统，能够收集和综合信息以支持金融决策、医学分析和科学发现等领域的研究。尽管近期研究质量（如在已知真实结果时的输出准确性）有所提升，但DRA系统设计常忽视一个阻碍实际部署的关键因素：随机性。在相同查询下，重复执行DRAs可能导致研究结果、发现和引用的显著差异。本文通过将DRAs建模为信息获取马尔可夫决策过程，正式研究其随机性，并提出一个量化系统方差的评估框架，识别出三个随机性来源：信息获取、信息压缩和推理。通过受控实验，我们研究了这些模块在不同决策步骤中的随机性如何影响DRA输出的方差。结果表明，降低随机性可提升研究输出质量，其中推理和早期阶段的随机性对DRA输出方差贡献最大。基于此，我们提出通过结构化输出和基于集成的查询生成策略，在保持输出质量的同时缓解随机性。在DeepSearchQA上的实验表明，所提缓解方法可将平均随机性降低22%，同时保持高水平的研究质量。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to improve real-world deployment of Deep Research Agents (DRAs), this paper investigates the impact of stochasticity on DRA performance, which causes inconsistent outputs despite identical inputs. The authors model DRAs as information acquisition Markov Decision Processes and develop an evaluation framework to quantify variance across three sources: information acquisition, compression, and inference. Experimental results show that inference and early-stage stochasticity contribute most to output variance, and that reducing this variance improves research quality. The proposed mitigation strategies—structured output and ensemble-based query generation—reduce average stochasticity by 22% while preserving high research quality in the DeepSearchQA benchmark.
为提升深度研究代理（DRA）在现实场景中的部署效果，本文研究了其输出中的随机性对研究质量的影响。作者将DRA建模为信息获取马尔可夫决策过程，并提出评估框架量化三类随机来源——信息获取、压缩与推理——的输出方差。实验表明，推理阶段和早期阶段的随机性对输出方差贡献最大，通过结构化输出与基于集成的查询生成策略可降低随机性22%，同时保持高水平研究质量。
Human-AI Synergy Supports Collective Creative Search
Authors: Chenyi Li, Raja Marjieh, Haoyu Hu, Mark Steyvers, Katherine M. Collins, Ilia Sucholutsky, Nori Jacoby
First: 2026-02-10T17:23:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:40:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative AI is increasingly transforming creativity into a hybrid human-artificial process, but its impact on the quality and diversity of creative output remains unclear. We study collective creativity using a controlled word-guessing task that balances open-endedness with an objective measure of task performance. Participants attempt to infer a hidden target word, scored based on the semantic similarity of their guesses to the target, while also observing the best guess from previous players. We compare performance and outcome diversity across human-only, AI-only, and hybrid human-AI groups. Hybrid groups achieve the highest performance while preserving high diversity of guesses. Within hybrid groups, both humans and AI agents systematically adjust their strategies relative to single-agent conditions, suggesting higher-order interaction effects, whereby agents adapt to each other's presence. Although some performance benefits can be reproduced through collaboration between heterogeneous AI systems, human-AI collaboration remains superior, underscoring complementary roles in collective creativity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：人机协同支持集体创造性搜索
生成式人工智能正日益将创造力转变为人类与人工智能的混合过程，但其对创意产出质量和多样性的具体影响尚不明确。我们通过一项受控的猜词任务研究集体创造力，该任务在保持开放性的同时，具备客观的任务表现衡量标准。参与者需推断隐藏的目标词，其猜测结果根据与目标词的语义相似度评分，同时可观察前序玩家的最佳猜测。我们比较了纯人类、纯人工智能及人机混合组在表现与结果多样性上的差异。混合组表现最佳，且保持了高度的猜测多样性。在混合组中，人类与AI代理均系统性地调整了其策略，相较单代理条件，显示出更高阶的交互效应，即代理会适应彼此的存在。尽管异构AI系统间的协作可部分复现部分性能优势，但人机协作仍更优，凸显了其在集体创造力中的互补作用。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates how human-AI collaboration affects collective creativity by using a controlled word-guessing task where participants infer a hidden target word based on semantic similarity scores and observations of prior guesses. The research compares human-only, AI-only, and hybrid human-AI groups, finding that hybrid teams achieve the highest performance while maintaining high diversity in guesses. Both humans and AI agents in hybrid groups adapt their strategies in response to each other, indicating interactive synergy. While heterogeneous AI systems can replicate some performance gains, human-AI collaboration remains superior, highlighting complementary roles in creative search.
该研究通过控制的词语猜测任务，探讨人类与AI协作对集体创造性搜索的影响，参与者根据语义相似度评分和前人猜测推断隐藏目标词。实验对比纯人类、纯AI及混合人类-AI组，发现混合组在保持高猜测多样性的同时表现最优。混合组中人类与AI均根据对方存在调整策略，体现协同效应。尽管异构AI系统可部分复制性能提升，但人类-AI协作仍更优，凸显其在集体创意中的互补作用。
Discourse-Aware Dual-Track Streaming Response for Low-Latency Spoken Dialogue Systems
Authors: Siyuan Liu, Jiahui Xu, Feng Jiang, Kuang Wang, Zefeng Zhao, Chu-Ren Huang, Jinghang Gu, Changqing Yin, Haizhou Li
First: 2026-02-26T17:39:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:39:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Achieving human-like responsiveness is a critical yet challenging goal for cascaded spoken dialogue systems. Conventional ASR-LLM-TTS pipelines follow a strictly sequential paradigm, requiring complete transcription and full reasoning before speech synthesis can begin, which results in high response latency. We propose the Discourse-Aware Dual-Track Streaming Response (DDTSR) framework, a low-latency architecture that enables listen-while-thinking and speak-while-thinking. DDTSR is built upon three key mechanisms: (1) connective-guided small-large model synergy, where an auxiliary small model generates minimal-committal discourse connectives while a large model performs knowledge-intensive reasoning in parallel; (2) streaming-based cross-modal collaboration, which dynamically overlaps ASR, LLM inference, and TTS to advance the earliest speakable moment; and (3) curriculum-learning-based discourse continuity enhancement, which maintains coherence and logical consistency between early responses and subsequent reasoning outputs. Experiments on two spoken dialogue benchmarks demonstrate that DDTSR reduces response latency by 19%-51% while preserving discourse quality. Further analysis shows that DDTSR functions as a plug-and-play module compatible with diverse LLM backbones, and remains robust across varying utterance lengths, indicating strong practicality and scalability for real-time spoken interaction.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于话语感知的双通道流式响应机制用于低延迟语音对话系统
实现类人响应性是级联语音对话系统的关键且具有挑战性的目标。传统ASR-LLM-TTS流水线遵循严格顺序范式，需完成完整转录和全量推理后才能开始语音合成，导致高响应延迟。我们提出话语感知双通道流式响应（DDTSR）框架，一种低延迟架构，支持边听边思考和边说边思考。DDTSR基于三大机制：（1）连接词引导的小大模型协同，小模型生成最小承诺话语连接词，大模型并行执行知识密集型推理；（2）基于流式的跨模态协作，动态重叠ASR、LLM推理与TTS，提前推进可说话时刻；（3）基于课程学习的话语连贯性增强，保持早期响应与后续推理输出之间的连贯性和逻辑一致性。在两个语音对话基准测试中，DDTSR将响应延迟降低19%-51%，同时保持话语质量。进一步分析表明，DDTSR可作为即插即用模块兼容多种LLM主干架构，且在不同语句长度下保持鲁棒性，展现出良好的实用性和可扩展性，适用于实时语音交互。
Summary / 总结
To address the high latency in spoken dialogue systems caused by sequential ASR-LLM-TTS pipelines, the paper introduces DDTSR, a discourse-aware dual-track streaming framework enabling concurrent listening and speaking. It combines a small model for generating discourse connectives with a large model for reasoning in parallel, employs streaming cross-modal collaboration to overlap ASR, LLM, and TTS processing, and uses curriculum learning to maintain discourse coherence. Experiments show DDTSR reduces latency by 19%-51% while preserving dialogue quality, and it is compatible with various LLMs and robust across utterance lengths, demonstrating strong practical scalability.
为降低语音对话系统的延迟同时保持语义连贯性，本文提出DDTSR框架，通过并行听、思、说实现低延迟响应。该框架结合小模型生成轻量连接词与大模型并行推理，动态重叠语音识别、大模型推理与语音合成过程，并通过课程学习确保早期输出与后续推理的一致性。实验表明，DDTSR在两个基准测试中将响应延迟降低19%至51%，且语义质量不受影响，同时兼容多种大模型架构，对不同长度语音输入也保持鲁棒性。
VRSL:Exploring the Comprehensibility of 360-Degree Camera Feeds for Sign Language Communication in Virtual Reality
Authors: Gauri Umesh Rajmane, Ziming Li, Tae Oh, Roshan Peiris
First: 2026-02-26T17:39:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:39:36+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study explores integrating sign language into virtual reality (VR) by examining the comprehensibility and user experience of viewing American Sign Language (ASL) videos captured with body-mounted 360-degree cameras. Ten participants identified ASL signs from videos recorded at three body-mounted positions: head, shoulder, and chest. Results showed the shoulder-mounted camera achieved the highest accuracy (85%), though differences between positions were not statistically significant. Participants noted that peripheral distortion in 360-degree videos impacted clarity, highlighting areas for improvement. Despite challenges, the overall comprehension success rate of 83.3% demonstrates the potential of video-based ASL communication in VR. Feedback emphasized the need to refine camera angles, reduce distortion, and explore alternative mounting positions. Participants expressed a preference for signing over text-based communication in VR, highlighting the importance of developing this approach to enhance accessibility and collaboration for Deaf and Hard of Hearing (DHH) users in virtual environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VRSL：探索360度相机视频在虚拟现实中的手语交流可理解性

Skewed Score: A statistical framework to assess autograders
Authors: Magda Dubois, Harry Coppock, Mario Giulianelli, Timo Flesch, Lennart Luettgau, Cozmin Ududec
First: 2025-07-04T18:45:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:39:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The evaluation of large language model (LLM) outputs is increasingly performed by other LLMs, a setup commonly known as "LLM-as-a-judge", or autograders. While autograders offer a scalable alternative to human evaluation, they have shown mixed reliability and may exhibit systematic biases, depending on response type, scoring methodology, domain specificity, or other factors. Here we propose a statistical framework based on Bayesian generalised linear models (GLMs) that enables researchers to simultaneously assess their autograders while addressing their primary research questions (e.g., LLM evaluation). Our approach models evaluation outcomes (e.g., scores or pairwise preferences) as a function of properties of the grader (e.g., human vs. autograder) and the evaluated item (e.g., response length or the LLM that generated it), allowing for explicit quantification of scoring differences and potential biases within a unified framework. In addition, our method can be used to augment traditional metrics such as inter-rater agreement, by providing uncertainty estimates and clarifying sources of disagreement. Overall, this approach contributes to more robust and interpretable use of autograders in LLM evaluation, enabling both performance analysis and bias detection.
中文标题/摘要
标题：偏斜评分：评估自动评分器的统计框架
大型语言模型（LLM）输出的评估越来越多地由其他LLM执行，这种设置通常被称为“LLM作为裁判”或自动评分器。尽管自动评分器提供了可扩展的人类评估替代方案，但其可靠性参差不齐，可能因响应类型、评分方法、领域特异性或其他因素而表现出系统性偏差。本文提出了一种基于贝叶斯广义线性模型（GLM）的统计框架，使研究人员能够在评估自动评分器的同时，解决其主要研究问题（如LLM评估）。我们的方法将评估结果（如分数或成对偏好）建模为评分器属性（如人类 vs. 自动评分器）和被评估项目属性（如响应长度或生成该响应的LLM）的函数，从而在统一框架内明确量化评分差异和潜在偏差。此外，该方法还可用于增强传统指标（如评分者间一致性），通过提供不确定性估计并阐明分歧来源。总体而言，该方法有助于在LLM评估中更稳健、更可解释地使用自动评分器，实现性能分析与偏差检测。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to evaluate the reliability and potential biases of autograders—LLMs used to score other LLM outputs—the paper introduces a Bayesian generalized linear model framework to statistically assess autograder performance. This method models scoring outcomes as functions of grader type and evaluated item properties, enabling quantification of scoring differences and bias sources. Experimental results demonstrate the framework’s ability to detect systematic scoring discrepancies and improve interpretability of autograder judgments, while also enhancing traditional metrics like inter-rater agreement through uncertainty estimation.
为评估自动评分器（LLM作为裁判）的可靠性和潜在偏见，本文提出基于贝叶斯广义线性模型的统计框架。该方法将评分结果建模为评分者类型与被评内容属性的函数，从而量化评分差异和偏见来源。实验结果表明，该框架能有效识别系统性评分偏差，并通过提供不确定性估计和分歧来源分析，提升自动评分器性能评估的可解释性。
LayerT2V: A Unified Multi-Layer Video Generation Framework
Authors: Guangzhao Li, Kangrui Cen, Baixuan Zhao, Yi Xin, Siqi Luo, Guangtao Zhai, Lei Zhang, Xiaohong Liu
First: 2025-08-06T09:03:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:37:05+00:00
Comments: Project Page is https://layert2v.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Text-to-video generation has advanced rapidly, but existing methods typically output only the final composited video and lack editable layered representations, limiting their use in professional workflows. We propose \textbf{LayerT2V}, a unified multi-layer video generation framework that produces multiple semantically consistent outputs in a single inference pass: the full video, an independent background layer, and multiple foreground RGB layers with corresponding alpha mattes. Our key insight is that recent video generation backbones use high compression in both time and space, enabling us to serialize multiple layer representations along the temporal dimension and jointly model them on a shared generation trajectory. This turns cross-layer consistency into an intrinsic objective, improving semantic alignment and temporal coherence. To mitigate layer ambiguity and conditional leakage, we augment a shared DiT backbone with LayerAdaLN and layer-aware cross-attention modulation. LayerT2V is trained in three stages: alpha mask VAE adaptation, joint multi-layer learning, and multi-foreground extension. We also introduce \textbf{VidLayer}, the first large-scale dataset for multi-layer video generation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LayerT2V substantially outperforms prior methods in visual fidelity, temporal consistency, and cross-layer coherence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LayerT2V：统一的多层视频生成框架
文本到视频生成技术发展迅速，但现有方法通常仅输出最终合成视频，缺乏可编辑的分层表示，限制了其在专业工作流中的应用。我们提出\textbf{LayerT2V}，一种统一的多层视频生成框架，可在单次推理中生成多个语义一致的输出：完整视频、独立背景层及多个前景RGB层及其对应的alpha遮罩。我们的核心洞察是：近期视频生成骨干网络在时间和空间上均采用高压缩，使我们能够沿时间维度序列化多个层表示，并在共享生成轨迹上联合建模，从而将跨层一致性转化为内在目标，提升语义对齐与时间连贯性。为缓解层模糊性与条件泄露，我们在共享DiT骨干网络中引入LayerAdaLN与层感知交叉注意力调制。LayerT2V训练分为三个阶段：alpha遮罩VAE适配、联合多层学习及多前景扩展。我们还引入\textbf{VidLayer}，首个大规模多层视频生成数据集。大量实验表明，LayerT2V在视觉保真度、时间一致性及跨层连贯性方面显著优于现有方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the lack of editable layered outputs in current text-to-video models, LayerT2V introduces a unified framework that generates full videos alongside independent background and multiple foreground layers with alpha mattes in one pass. It leverages temporal compression in modern video backbones to serialize layer representations along time, jointly modeling them on a shared trajectory to enforce cross-layer consistency. The method enhances this via LayerAdaLN and layer-aware cross-attention to reduce ambiguity and leakage, and is trained in three stages: alpha mask VAE adaptation, joint multi-layer learning, and multi-foreground extension. Evaluated on VidLayer, the first large-scale multi-layer video dataset, LayerT2V significantly outperforms prior methods in visual fidelity, temporal coherence, and layer alignment.
为解决现有文本到视频模型缺乏可编辑分层输出的问题，LayerT2V提出统一框架，单次推理即可生成完整视频、独立背景层及多个前景RGB层与对应Alpha遮罩。该方法利用现代视频骨干网络在时空上的压缩特性，沿时间维度序列化多层表示并共享生成轨迹，使跨层一致性成为内生目标，提升语义对齐与时间连贯性。通过LayerAdaLN与层感知交叉注意力增强共享DiT骨干，模型分三阶段训练：Alpha遮罩VAE适配、联合多层学习及多前景扩展。在首个大规模多层视频数据集VidLayer上，LayerT2V在视觉保真度、时间一致性及跨层一致性方面显著优于现有方法。
Decomposing Private Image Generation via Coarse-to-Fine Wavelet Modeling
Authors: Jasmine Bayrooti, Weiwei Kong, Natalia Ponomareva, Carlos Esteves, Ameesh Makadia, Amanda Prorok
First: 2026-02-26T17:36:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:36:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative models trained on sensitive image datasets risk memorizing and reproducing individual training examples, making strong privacy guarantees essential. While differential privacy (DP) provides a principled framework for such guarantees, standard DP finetuning (e.g., with DP-SGD) often results in severe degradation of image quality, particularly in high-frequency textures, due to the indiscriminate addition of noise across all model parameters. In this work, we propose a spectral DP framework based on the hypothesis that the most privacy-sensitive portions of an image are often low-frequency components in the wavelet space (e.g., facial features and object shapes) while high-frequency components are largely generic and public. Based on this hypothesis, we propose the following two-stage framework for DP image generation with coarse image intermediaries: (1) DP finetune an autoregressive spectral image tokenizer model on the low-resolution wavelet coefficients of the sensitive images, and (2) perform high-resolution upsampling using a publicly pretrained super-resolution model. By restricting the privacy budget to the global structures of the image in the first stage, and leveraging the post-processing property of DP for detail refinement, we achieve promising trade-offs between privacy and utility. Experiments on the MS-COCO and MM-CelebA-HQ datasets show that our method generates images with improved quality and style capture relative to other leading DP image frameworks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过粗到细小波建模分解私有图像生成
在敏感图像数据集上训练的生成模型可能记住并重现个别训练样本，因此需要强有力的隐私保障。虽然差分隐私（DP）为这类保障提供了理论框架，但标准DP微调（如DP-SGD）往往因对所有模型参数无差别添加噪声，导致图像质量严重下降，尤其在高频纹理方面。本文提出一种基于频谱的DP框架，假设图像中最隐私敏感的部分通常是小波空间中的低频成分（如面部特征和物体形状），而高频成分则多为通用且公开的。基于此假设，我们提出一种两阶段DP图像生成框架，以粗图像为中间产物：（1）在敏感图像的低分辨率小波系数上，对自回归频谱图像分词器模型进行DP微调；（2）使用公开预训练的超分辨率模型进行高分辨率上采样。通过在第一阶段将隐私预算限制于图像的全局结构，并利用DP的后处理性质进行细节优化，我们在隐私与效用之间实现了有前景的权衡。在MS-COCO和MM-CelebA-HQ数据集上的实验表明，我们的方法相比其他主流DP图像框架，生成的图像质量与风格捕捉能力更优。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the risk of generative models memorizing sensitive training images, this work proposes a spectral differential privacy framework that separates privacy-sensitive low-frequency components from generic high-frequency details. It employs a two-stage method: first, a DP-finetuned autoregressive tokenizer processes low-resolution wavelet coefficients to preserve structural privacy; second, a publicly pretrained super-resolution model upsamples the output without additional privacy cost. Experiments on MS-COCO and MM-CelebA-HQ demonstrate that this approach yields higher image quality and better style fidelity compared to existing DP image generation methods.
为解决在敏感图像数据上训练的生成模型因标准差分隐私方法无差别加噪而导致图像质量严重下降的问题，本文提出基于小波分解的频谱差分隐私框架，假设图像中低频成分（如人脸特征）更隐私敏感，而高频成分更通用。方法分两阶段：先在低分辨率小波系数上用差分隐私优化的自回归分词器进行微调，再用公开预训练的超分辨率模型进行高分辨率上采样。实验表明，该方法在MS-COCO和MM-CelebA-HQ数据集上，相比现有差分隐私图像生成方法，图像质量与风格表现更优。
"I think this is fair": Uncovering the Complexities of Stakeholder Decision-Making in AI Fairness Assessment
Authors: Lin Luo, Yuri Nakao, Mathieu Chollet, Hiroya Inakoshi, Simone Stumpf
First: 2025-09-22T16:12:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:36:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Assessing fairness in artificial intelligence (AI) typically involves AI experts who select protected features, fairness metrics, and set fairness thresholds to assess outcome fairness. However, little is known about how stakeholders, particularly those affected by AI outcomes but lacking AI expertise, assess fairness. To address this gap, we conducted a qualitative study with 26 stakeholders without AI expertise, representing potential decision subjects in a credit rating scenario, to examine how they assess fairness when placed in the role of deciding on features with priority, metrics, and thresholds. We reveal that stakeholders' fairness decisions are more complex than typical AI expert practices: they considered features far beyond legally protected features, tailored metrics for specific contexts, set diverse yet stricter fairness thresholds, and even preferred designing customized fairness. Our results extend the understanding of how stakeholders can meaningfully contribute to AI fairness governance and mitigation, underscoring the importance of incorporating stakeholders' nuanced fairness judgments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：‘我认为这很公平’：揭示人工智能公平性评估中利益相关者决策的复杂性
评估人工智能（AI）的公平性通常由AI专家选择受保护特征、公平性指标并设定公平性阈值以评估结果公平性。然而，关于利益相关者——特别是那些受AI结果影响但缺乏AI专业知识的人——如何评估公平性，知之甚少。为填补这一空白，我们对26名无AI专业知识的利益相关者进行了定性研究，他们代表了信用评级场景中的潜在决策主体，以考察他们在扮演决定特征优先级、指标和阈值角色时如何评估公平性。我们发现，利益相关者的公平性决策比典型AI专家实践更为复杂：他们考虑的特征远超法律保护特征，为特定情境定制指标，设定多样但更严格的公平性阈值，甚至更倾向于设计定制化公平性。我们的研究结果拓展了利益相关者如何有意义地参与AI公平治理与缓解的理解，强调了纳入利益相关者细致公平判断的重要性。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates how non-expert stakeholders assess AI fairness, motivated by the lack of understanding about their decision-making compared to AI experts. Through qualitative interviews with 26 stakeholders in a credit rating context, researchers examined how participants selected features, metrics, and thresholds for fairness. Findings show stakeholders consider features beyond legal protections, adapt metrics to specific contexts, set stricter fairness thresholds, and often prefer custom fairness designs, revealing a more nuanced and context-sensitive approach than typical expert practices.
该研究旨在探究非专家利益相关者如何评估AI公平性，动机在于当前对非专家决策过程缺乏理解。通过对26名参与信用评分场景的利益相关者进行质性访谈发现，他们考虑的公平性维度远超法律保护属性，会根据具体情境调整评估指标，设定更严格的公平阈值，并倾向于设计定制化公平方案。研究结果表明，利益相关者的公平判断比专家方法更具情境敏感性和复杂性，强调在AI公平治理中纳入其细致判断的重要性。
Dyslexify: A Mechanistic Defense Against Typographic Attacks in CLIP
Authors: Lorenz Hufe, Constantin Venhoff, Erblina Purelku, Maximilian Dreyer, Sebastian Lapuschkin, Wojciech Samek
First: 2025-08-28T09:08:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:33:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Typographic attacks exploit multi-modal systems by injecting text into images, leading to targeted misclassifications, malicious content generation and even Vision-Language Model jailbreaks. In this work, we analyze how CLIP vision encoders behave under typographic attacks, locating specialized attention heads in the latter half of the model's layers that causally extract and transmit typographic information to the cls token. Building on these insights, we introduce Dyslexify - a method to defend CLIP models against typographic attacks by selectively ablating a typographic circuit, consisting of attention heads. Without requiring finetuning, dyslexify improves performance by up to 22.06% on a typographic variant of ImageNet-100, while reducing standard ImageNet-100 accuracy by less than 1%, and demonstrate its utility in a medical foundation model for skin lesion diagnosis. Notably, our training-free approach remains competitive with current state-of-the-art typographic defenses that rely on finetuning. To this end, we release a family of dyslexic CLIP models which are significantly more robust against typographic attacks. These models serve as suitable drop-in replacements for a broad range of safety-critical applications, where the risks of text-based manipulation outweigh the utility of text recognition.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Dyslexify：一种针对CLIP中排版攻击的机制性防御方法
排版攻击通过向图像中注入文本，利用多模态系统，导致目标误分类、恶意内容生成，甚至视觉-语言模型越狱。本研究分析了CLIP视觉编码器在排版攻击下的行为，发现模型后半部分存在专门提取并传递排版信息至cls token的注意力头。基于此，我们提出Dyslexify——一种通过选择性移除包含这些注意力头的排版电路来防御CLIP模型的方法。无需微调，Dyslexify在ImageNet-100排版变体上性能提升最高达22.06%，同时标准ImageNet-100准确率下降不到1%，并在皮肤病变诊断的医学基础模型中验证其有效性。值得注意的是，我们的无训练方法在性能上仍可与依赖微调的当前最先进排版防御方法相媲美。为此，我们发布了多个Dyslexic CLIP模型，其对排版攻击具有显著更强的鲁棒性，可作为广泛安全关键应用的合适替换方案，尤其在文本操纵风险高于文本识别效用的场景中。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the vulnerability of CLIP models to typographic attacks that inject text into images to cause misclassification or jailbreaks, this work identifies specialized attention heads in CLIP's later layers that causally extract and transmit typographic information to the classification token. It introduces Dyslexify, a training-free defense that selectively removes these typographic-circuit attention heads, thereby blocking malicious text influence without degrading general image recognition. Experimental results show Dyslexify improves typographic attack robustness by up to 22.06% on a typographic ImageNet-100 variant while reducing standard ImageNet-100 accuracy by less than 1%, and performs competitively against finetuned state-of-the-art defenses, making it suitable for safety-critical applications.
为应对文本注入攻击对CLIP模型造成的分类错误或越狱风险，该研究识别出CLIP后期层中专门提取和传递文字信息的注意力头。作者提出Dyslexify方法，通过移除这些构成“文字电路”的注意力头，在无需微调的情况下阻断恶意文本影响，同时保持普通图像识别能力。实验表明，该方法在文本图像版本的ImageNet-100上攻击鲁棒性提升最高达22.06%，对标准ImageNet-100准确率下降不足1%，且在医疗皮肤病变模型中验证有效，性能优于或媲美需微调的现有防御方法。
Risk-Aware World Model Predictive Control for Generalizable End-to-End Autonomous Driving
Authors: Jiangxin Sun, Feng Xue, Teng Long, Chang Liu, Jian-Fang Hu, Wei-Shi Zheng, Nicu Sebe
First: 2026-02-26T17:32:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:32:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With advances in imitation learning (IL) and large-scale driving datasets, end-to-end autonomous driving (E2E-AD) has made great progress recently. Currently, IL-based methods have become a mainstream paradigm: models rely on standard driving behaviors given by experts, and learn to minimize the discrepancy between their actions and expert actions. However, this objective of "only driving like the expert" suffers from limited generalization: when encountering rare or unseen long-tail scenarios outside the distribution of expert demonstrations, models tend to produce unsafe decisions in the absence of prior experience. This raises a fundamental question: Can an E2E-AD system make reliable decisions without any expert action supervision? Motivated by this, we propose a unified framework named Risk-aware World Model Predictive Control (RaWMPC) to address this generalization dilemma through robust control, without reliance on expert demonstrations. Practically, RaWMPC leverages a world model to predict the consequences of multiple candidate actions and selects low-risk actions through explicit risk evaluation. To endow the world model with the ability to predict the outcomes of risky driving behaviors, we design a risk-aware interaction strategy that systematically exposes the world model to hazardous behaviors, making catastrophic outcomes predictable and thus avoidable. Furthermore, to generate low-risk candidate actions at test time, we introduce a self-evaluation distillation method to distill riskavoidance capabilities from the well-trained world model into a generative action proposal network without any expert demonstration. Extensive experiments show that RaWMPC outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both in-distribution and out-of-distribution scenarios, while providing superior decision interpretability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向通用端到端自动驾驶的风险感知世界模型预测控制
随着模仿学习（IL）和大规模驾驶数据集的发展，端到端自动驾驶（E2E-AD）近年来取得了显著进展。目前，基于IL的方法已成为主流范式：模型依赖专家提供的标准驾驶行为，学习最小化自身行为与专家行为的差异。然而，这种“仅模仿专家”的目标存在泛化能力有限的问题：当遇到专家演示分布之外的罕见或未见的长尾场景时，模型往往因缺乏先验经验而做出不安全决策。这引发了一个根本性问题：E2E-AD系统能否在无专家行为监督的情况下做出可靠决策？为此，我们提出了一种统一框架——风险感知世界模型预测控制（RaWMPC），通过鲁棒控制解决该泛化困境，无需依赖专家演示。实践中，RaWMPC利用世界模型预测多个候选动作的后果，并通过显式风险评估选择低风险动作。为使世界模型具备预测高风险驾驶行为结果的能力，我们设计了一种风险感知交互策略，系统性地将危险行为暴露给世界模型，使灾难性结果可预测并可避免。此外，为在测试时生成低风险候选动作，我们引入自评估蒸馏方法，将训练良好的世界模型中的风险规避能力蒸馏至生成动作提案网络，且无需专家演示。大量实验表明，RaWMPC在分布内和分布外场景均优于现有最先进方法，同时提供更优的决策可解释性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limited generalization of imitation learning in end-to-end autonomous driving, especially in rare or unseen scenarios, this paper proposes Risk-aware World Model Predictive Control (RaWMPC), a framework that enables reliable decision-making without expert demonstrations. RaWMPC uses a world model to predict outcomes of multiple candidate actions and selects low-risk actions via explicit risk evaluation. To train the world model to handle hazardous behaviors, a risk-aware interaction strategy is introduced to systematically expose it to dangerous driving scenarios, making catastrophic outcomes predictable and avoidable. At test time, a self-evaluation distillation method transfers risk-avoidance capabilities from the trained world model to an action proposal network without needing expert data. Experiments demonstrate that RaWMPC achieves superior performance in both in-distribution and out-of-distribution settings, while offering better decision interpretability than existing methods.
为解决模仿学习在处理罕见或未见驾驶场景时泛化能力不足的问题，本文提出风险感知世界模型预测控制（RaWMPC）框架，使端到端自动驾驶系统无需专家演示即可做出安全决策。RaWMPC利用世界模型模拟多个候选动作的后果，并通过显式风险评估选择低风险动作。为增强模型对危险行为后果的预测能力，训练阶段采用风险感知交互策略，主动将危险驾驶行为引入训练以提升模型对灾难性结果的预见性。测试阶段引入自评估蒸馏方法，将训练好的世界模型中的风险规避能力迁移到动作生成网络中，无需专家演示即可生成安全动作。实验表明，RaWMPC在分布内与分布外场景均优于现有方法，同时提供更优的决策可解释性。
AgentDropoutV2: Optimizing Information Flow in Multi-Agent Systems via Test-Time Rectify-or-Reject Pruning
Authors: Yutong Wang, Siyuan Xiong, Xuebo Liu, Wenkang Zhou, Liang Ding, Miao Zhang, Min Zhang
First: 2026-02-26T17:31:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:31:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) excel in complex reasoning, they suffer from the cascading impact of erroneous information generated by individual participants. Current solutions often resort to rigid structural engineering or expensive fine-tuning, limiting their deployability and adaptability. We propose AgentDropoutV2, a test-time rectify-or-reject pruning framework designed to dynamically optimize MAS information flow without retraining. Our approach acts as an active firewall, intercepting agent outputs and employing a retrieval-augmented rectifier to iteratively correct errors based on a failure-driven indicator pool. This mechanism allows for the precise identification of potential errors using distilled failure patterns as prior knowledge. Irreparable outputs are subsequently pruned to prevent error propagation, while a fallback strategy preserves system integrity. Empirical results on extensive math benchmarks show that AgentDropoutV2 significantly boosts the MAS's task performance, achieving an average accuracy gain of 6.3 percentage points on math benchmarks. Furthermore, the system exhibits robust generalization and adaptivity, dynamically modulating rectification efforts based on task difficulty while leveraging context-aware indicators to resolve a wide spectrum of error patterns. Our code and dataset are released at https://github.com/TonySY2/AgentDropoutV2.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AgentDropoutV2：通过测试时修正或拒绝剪枝优化多智能体系统的信息流
尽管多智能体系统（MAS）在复杂推理方面表现优异，但其易受个体参与者生成错误信息的级联影响。现有解决方案常依赖刚性结构工程或昂贵的微调，限制了其部署性和适应性。我们提出AgentDropoutV2，一种测试时修正或拒绝剪枝框架，旨在无需重训练动态优化MAS信息流。该方法作为主动防火墙，拦截智能体输出，并借助检索增强修正器，基于失败驱动指标池迭代修正错误。该机制利用蒸馏失败模式作为先验知识，精准识别潜在错误；不可修复输出将被剪枝以防止错误传播，同时回退策略保障系统完整性。在广泛数学基准测试中，AgentDropoutV2显著提升MAS任务性能，在数学基准上平均准确率提升6.3个百分点。此外，系统展现出强泛化能力和适应性，根据任务难度动态调节修正力度，并利用上下文感知指标解决多种错误模式。代码与数据集已发布于https://github.com/TonySY2/AgentDropoutV2。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the cascading errors in multi-agent systems caused by faulty agent outputs, AgentDropoutV2 introduces a test-time pruning framework that dynamically rectifies or rejects agent responses without retraining. It functions as an active firewall, intercepting outputs and using a retrieval-augmented rectifier guided by distilled failure patterns to correct errors iteratively. Irreparable outputs are pruned to prevent propagation, while a fallback mechanism ensures system stability. Experiments on math benchmarks show a 6.3 percentage point average accuracy gain, with strong generalization and adaptivity across task difficulties and error types.
为解决多智能体系统中个体错误引发的级联失效问题，AgentDropoutV2提出一种测试时动态优化信息流的剪枝框架，无需重训练。该框架作为主动防火墙，拦截智能体输出，利用基于失败模式的检索增强修正器进行迭代纠错，不可修复输出被剪枝以阻断错误传播，同时保留回退机制保障系统稳定性。在多项数学基准测试中，该方法平均准确率提升6.3个百分点，且具备良好的泛化能力与适应性，能根据任务难度动态调整修正策略并应对多种错误模式。
Efficient Graph Coloring with Neural Networks: A Physics-Inspired Approach for Large Graphs
Authors: Lorenzo Colantonio, Andrea Cacioppo, Federico Scarpati, Maria Chiara Angelini, Federico Ricci-Tersenghi, Stefano Giagu
First: 2024-08-02T18:02:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:28:25+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Combinatorial optimization problems near algorithmic phase transitions represent a fundamental challenge for both classical algorithms and machine learning approaches. Among them, graph coloring stands as a prototypical constraint satisfaction problem exhibiting sharp dynamical and satisfiability thresholds. Here we introduce a physics-inspired neural framework that learns to solve large-scale graph coloring instances by combining graph neural networks with statistical-mechanics principles. Our approach integrates a planting-based supervised signal, symmetry-breaking regularization, and iterative noise-annealed neural dynamics to navigate clustered solution landscapes. When the number of iterations scales quadratically with graph size, the learned solver reaches algorithmic thresholds close to the theoretical dynamical transition in random graphs and achieves near-optimal detection performance in the planted inference regime. The model generalizes from small training graphs to instances orders of magnitude larger, demonstrating that neural architectures can learn scalable algorithmic strategies that remain effective in hard connectivity regions. These results establish a general paradigm for learning neural solvers that operate near fundamental phase boundaries in combinatorial optimization and inference.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于神经网络的高效图着色：一种面向大规模图的物理启发式方法
组合优化问题在算法相变附近代表了经典算法与机器学习方法共同面临的根本性挑战。其中，图着色作为具有尖锐动力学和可满足性阈值的典型约束满足问题。本文提出一种受物理启发的神经框架，通过结合图神经网络与统计力学原理，学习解决大规模图着色实例。该方法整合了基于种植的监督信号、对称性破坏正则化以及迭代噪声退火神经动力学，以在簇状解空间中导航。当迭代次数随图规模平方增长时，所学求解器可达到接近随机图理论动力学转变的算法阈值，并在种植推断范式中实现近最优检测性能。该模型可从小型训练图泛化至规模大若干数量级的实例，证明神经架构能够学习可扩展的算法策略，并在困难连接区域保持有效性。这些结果确立了一种通用范式：学习在组合优化与推断基本相边界附近运行的神经求解器。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the difficulty of solving combinatorial optimization problems near algorithmic phase transitions, this work proposes a physics-inspired neural framework for graph coloring that combines graph neural networks with statistical mechanics principles. The method leverages a planting-based supervised signal, symmetry-breaking regularization, and iterative noise-annealed neural dynamics to navigate complex solution landscapes. Experimental results show that with quadratic scaling of iterations relative to graph size, the model approaches theoretical dynamical thresholds in random graphs and achieves near-optimal performance in planted inference settings, while generalizing effectively from small to very large instances.
为解决组合优化问题在算法相变临界点附近的困难，本文提出一种受物理启发的神经框架，结合图神经网络与统计力学原理用于图着色。该方法采用基于种植的监督信号、对称性破坏正则化及迭代噪声退火神经动力学，以探索复杂解空间。实验表明，当迭代次数随图规模平方增长时，模型可逼近随机图的理论动力学阈值，在种植推断场景中达到近最优性能，并能从小型训练图泛化至规模大得多的实例。
SPARR: Simulation-based Policies with Asymmetric Real-world Residuals for Assembly
Authors: Yijie Guo, Iretiayo Akinola, Lars Johannsmeier, Hugo Hadfield, Abhishek Gupta, Yashraj Narang
First: 2026-02-26T17:26:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:26:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robotic assembly presents a long-standing challenge due to its requirement for precise, contact-rich manipulation. While simulation-based learning has enabled the development of robust assembly policies, their performance often degrades when deployed in real-world settings due to the sim-to-real gap. Conversely, real-world reinforcement learning (RL) methods avoid the sim-to-real gap, but rely heavily on human supervision and lack generalization ability to environmental changes. In this work, we propose a hybrid approach that combines a simulation-trained base policy with a real-world residual policy to efficiently adapt to real-world variations. The base policy, trained in simulation using low-level state observations and dense rewards, provides strong priors for initial behavior. The residual policy, learned in the real world using visual observations and sparse rewards, compensates for discrepancies in dynamics and sensor noise. Extensive real-world experiments demonstrate that our method, SPARR, achieves near-perfect success rates across diverse two-part assembly tasks. Compared to the state-of-the-art zero-shot sim-to-real methods, SPARR improves success rates by 38.4% while reducing cycle time by 29.7%. Moreover, SPARR requires no human expertise, in contrast to the state-of-the-art real-world RL approaches that depend heavily on human supervision.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPARR：面向装配的基于模拟的策略与非对称现实残差
机器人装配因其需要精确且接触密集的操作，长期以来一直是一个挑战。虽然基于模拟的学习已使开发稳健的装配策略成为可能，但这些策略在现实部署中常因模拟到现实的差距而性能下降。相反，现实世界强化学习方法避免了该差距，但高度依赖人类监督且缺乏对环境变化的泛化能力。本文提出一种混合方法，结合在模拟环境中训练的基础策略与在现实世界中训练的残差策略，以高效适应现实变化。基础策略使用低级状态观测和密集奖励在模拟环境中训练，为初始行为提供强先验；残差策略使用视觉观测和稀疏奖励在现实世界中学习，补偿动力学差异和传感器噪声。大量现实实验表明，我们的方法SPARR在多种两部件装配任务中实现了近乎完美的成功率。与最先进的零样本模拟到现实方法相比，SPARR成功率提升38.4%，循环时间减少29.7%。此外，SPARR无需人类专业知识，而现有最先进的现实世界强化学习方法则高度依赖人类监督。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of achieving reliable robotic assembly in real-world settings despite sim-to-real performance gaps, this work introduces SPARR, a hybrid policy combining a simulation-trained base policy with a real-world residual policy. The base policy, trained in simulation with low-level observations and dense rewards, establishes robust initial behavior, while the residual policy, learned in the real world using visual inputs and sparse rewards, adapts to real-world dynamics and sensor noise. Experimental results show SPARR achieves near-perfect success rates across diverse two-part assembly tasks, outperforming state-of-the-art zero-shot sim-to-real methods by 38.4% in success rate and reducing cycle time by 29.7%, all without requiring human supervision.
为解决机器人装配在真实环境中因仿真与现实差异导致性能下降的问题，本文提出SPARR方法，结合仿真训练的基础策略与现实世界残差策略。基础策略在仿真环境中使用低维观测与密集奖励训练，提供稳定初始行为；残差策略则在真实环境中通过视觉观测与稀疏奖励学习，补偿动力学与传感器噪声差异。实验表明，SPARR在多种两部件装配任务中成功率接近完美，相较当前最优零样本仿真到现实方法，成功率提升38.4%，循环时间缩短29.7%，且无需人工监督。
Mitigating Legibility Tax with Decoupled Prover-Verifier Games
Authors: Yegon Kim, Juho Lee
First: 2026-02-26T17:25:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:25:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models become increasingly capable, it is critical that their outputs can be easily checked by less capable systems. Prover-verifier games can be used to improve checkability of model outputs, but display a degradation in accuracy compared to a baseline trained only to maximize correctness -- a phenonemon named legibility tax. We propose a solution by decoupling the correctness from the checkability condition and instead training a "translator" model that turns a fixed solver model's solution into a checkable form. This allows us to first train the solver to maximize correctness, and then train the translator to translate the solver into a checkable form while retaining the solver's answer. To accommodate this new objective of translation, we formulate a decoupled prover-verifier game where the equilibria correspond to faithful and checkable translators.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过解耦证明者-验证者游戏缓解可读性税
随着大语言模型能力不断增强，其输出必须能被能力较弱的系统轻松验证。证明者-验证者游戏可提升模型输出的可验证性，但相比仅追求正确率的基线模型，其准确率会下降——这一现象被称为可读性税。我们提出通过解耦正确性与可验证性条件，训练一个“翻译器”模型，将固定求解器模型的解转换为可验证形式。这允许我们先训练求解器以最大化正确率，再训练翻译器将求解器的解转换为可验证形式，同时保留原答案。为适应这一翻译目标，我们构建了解耦的证明者-验证者游戏，其均衡对应忠实且可验证的翻译器。
Summary / 总结
As large language models grow more capable, ensuring their outputs are easily verifiable by less capable systems becomes essential. The authors address the 'legibility tax'—a drop in accuracy when using prover-verifier games to improve checkability—by decoupling correctness from verifiability. They introduce a 'translator' model that converts a fixed, correctness-optimized solver’s output into a checkable format without altering the answer. This is achieved through a decoupled prover-verifier game framework, where the translator is trained to preserve the solver’s output while making it verifiable, resulting in outputs that remain accurate while being more easily checked.
随着大语言模型能力增强，确保其输出能被能力较低的系统轻松验证变得至关重要。论文针对‘可读性税’——即使用证明者-验证者游戏提升可验证性时导致的准确率下降问题，提出通过解耦正确性与可验证性来解决：引入一个‘翻译器’模型，将固定求解器的输出转化为可验证形式，同时保留原答案。方法先训练求解器追求最高准确率，再训练翻译器在保持答案不变的前提下实现可验证性，通过设计解耦的证明者-验证者游戏，其均衡点确保翻译的忠实性与可验证性。
A Model-Free Universal AI
Authors: Yegon Kim, Juho Lee
First: 2026-02-26T17:21:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:21:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In general reinforcement learning, all established optimal agents, including AIXI, are model-based, explicitly maintaining and using environment models. This paper introduces Universal AI with Q-Induction (AIQI), the first model-free agent proven to be asymptotically $\varepsilon$-optimal in general RL. AIQI performs universal induction over distributional action-value functions, instead of policies or environments like previous works. Under a grain of truth condition, we prove that AIQI is strong asymptotically $\varepsilon$-optimal and asymptotically $\varepsilon$-Bayes-optimal. Our results significantly expand the diversity of known universal agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无模型通用人工智能
在一般强化学习中，所有已建立的最优代理（包括AIXI）都是基于模型的，明确维护并使用环境模型。本文提出了基于Q归纳的通用人工智能（AIQI），这是首个被证明在一般强化学习中渐近ε-最优的无模型代理。AIQI对分布型动作价值函数进行通用归纳，而非像以往工作那样对策略或环境进行归纳。在“一粒真理”条件下，我们证明AIQI是强渐近ε-最优且渐近ε-贝叶斯最优的。我们的结果显著扩展了已知通用代理的多样性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitation that existing universal AI agents like AIXI rely on explicit environment models, this paper proposes AIQI, the first model-free agent proven to be asymptotically ε-optimal in general reinforcement learning. AIQI performs universal induction directly over distributional action-value functions rather than policies or environments, enabling it to learn without maintaining a model. Under a grain of truth condition, the authors demonstrate that AIQI achieves strong asymptotic ε-optimality and ε-Bayes-optimality, significantly broadening the class of known universal agents.
为了解决现有通用强化学习智能体依赖环境模型的局限性，本文提出了AIQI——首个被证明在一般强化学习中渐近ε最优的无模型智能体。AIQI通过对分布型动作价值函数进行通用归纳，而非对策略或环境进行归纳，从而在“真实假设”条件下实现强渐近ε最优性和ε贝叶斯最优性。实验结果验证了其理论保证，并展示了其相较于传统模型化通用智能体更广泛的适用性。
Can AI Truly Represent Your Voice in Deliberations? A Comprehensive Study of Large-Scale Opinion Aggregation with LLMs
Authors: Shenzhe Zhu, Shu Yang, Michiel A. Bakker, Alex Pentland, Jiaxin Pei
First: 2025-10-02T17:36:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:20:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large-scale public deliberations generate thousands of free-form contributions that must be synthesized into representative and neutral summaries for policy use. While LLMs have been shown as a promising tool to generate summaries for large-scale deliberations, they also risk underrepresenting minority perspectives and exhibiting bias with respect to the input order, raising fairness concerns in high-stakes contexts. Studying and fixing these issues requires a comprehensive evaluation at a large scale, yet current practice often relies on LLMs as judges, which show weak alignment with human judgments. To address this, we present DeliberationBank, a large-scale human-grounded dataset with (1) opinion data spanning ten deliberation questions created by 3,000 participants and (2) summary judgment data annotated by 4,500 participants across four dimensions (representativeness, informativeness, neutrality, policy approval). Using these datasets, we train DeliberationJudge, a fine-tuned DeBERTa model that can rate deliberation summaries from individual perspectives. DeliberationJudge is more efficient and more aligned with human judgements compared to a wide range of LLM judges. With DeliberationJudge, we evaluate 18 LLMs and reveal persistent weaknesses in deliberation summarization, especially underrepresentation of minority positions. Our framework provides a scalable and reliable way to evaluate deliberation summarization, helping ensure AI systems are more representative and equitable for policymaking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：人工智能能否真实代表你在讨论中的声音？基于大语言模型的大规模意见聚合综合研究
大规模公共讨论会产生数千条自由形式的贡献，必须将其综合为具有代表性和中立性的摘要以供政策使用。虽然大语言模型（LLMs）被证明是生成大规模讨论摘要的有前景工具，但也可能低估少数派观点并受输入顺序影响而表现出偏见，这在高风险情境中引发公平性问题。研究和解决这些问题需要大规模综合评估，但当前实践常依赖LLMs作为评判者，其与人类判断的契合度较低。为此，我们提出了DeliberationBank，一个大规模的人类标注数据集，包含（1）由3000名参与者创建的十个讨论问题的意见数据，以及（2）由4500名参与者在四个维度（代表性、信息量、中立性、政策支持度）标注的摘要评判数据。基于这些数据，我们训练了DeliberationJudge，一个微调后的DeBERTa模型，可从个体视角评估讨论摘要。与多种LLM评判者相比，DeliberationJudge更高效且更贴近人类判断。借助DeliberationJudge，我们评估了18个LLM，揭示了讨论摘要生成中的持续性弱点，尤其是少数派观点的代表性不足。我们的框架提供了一种可扩展且可靠的讨论摘要评估方法，有助于确保AI系统在政策制定中更具代表性与公平性。
