Evaluating 18 LLMs with DeliberationJudge, they find consistent underrepresentation of minority views and poor neutrality, highlighting systemic flaws in current AI summarization for policy contexts.
为解决大规模公共讨论中AI总结易偏颇、忽视少数观点的问题，该研究构建了DeliberationBank数据集，包含3000名参与者的意见和4500名标注者在四个维度上的评价。基于此训练出DeliberationJudge模型，其在人类判断对齐度上优于多数LLM。对18个LLM的评估显示，它们普遍存在少数群体观点被忽视和中立性不足的问题，揭示了当前AI政策摘要方法的系统性缺陷。
Agency and Architectural Limits: Why Optimization-Based Systems Cannot Be Norm-Responsive
Authors: Radha Sarma
First: 2026-02-26T17:16:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:16:17+00:00
Comments: About 10,500 words in all (including 922 words of literature and 2019 words of Appendices). Under journal review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
AI systems are increasingly deployed in high-stakes contexts -- medical diagnosis, legal research, financial analysis -- under the assumption they can be governed by norms. This paper demonstrates that assumption is formally invalid for optimization-based systems, specifically Large Language Models trained via Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF). We establish that genuine agency requires two necessary and jointly sufficient architectural conditions: the capacity to maintain certain boundaries as non-negotiable constraints rather than tradeable weights (Incommensurability), and a non-inferential mechanism capable of suspending processing when those boundaries are threatened (Apophatic Responsiveness). These conditions apply across all normative domains. RLHF-based systems are constitutively incompatible with both conditions. The operations that make optimization powerful -- unifying all values on a scalar metric and always selecting the highest-scoring output -- are precisely the operations that preclude normative governance. This incompatibility is not a correctable training bug awaiting a technical fix; it is a formal constraint inherent to what optimization is. Consequently, documented failure modes - sycophancy, hallucination, and unfaithful reasoning - are not accidents but structural manifestations. Misaligned deployment triggers a second-order risk we term the Convergence Crisis: when humans are forced to verify AI outputs under metric pressure, they degrade from genuine agents into criteria-checking optimizers, eliminating the only component in the system capable of normative accountability. Beyond the incompatibility proof, the paper's primary positive contribution is a substrate-neutral architectural specification defining what any system -- biological, artificial, or institutional -- must satisfy to qualify as an agent rather than a sophisticated instrument.
中文标题/摘要
标题：代理与架构限制：为何基于优化的系统无法响应规范
AI系统越来越多地部署在高风险场景中——如医疗诊断、法律研究、金融分析——并假设它们可受规范约束。本文证明，该假设对基于优化的系统（特别是通过人类反馈强化学习训练的大语言模型RLHF）在形式上无效。我们确立，真正的代理需满足两个必要且充分的架构条件：一是能将某些边界视为不可协商的约束而非可交易的权重（不可通约性）；二是具备非推论机制，能在边界受威胁时暂停处理（否定性响应）。这些条件适用于所有规范领域。RLHF系统本质上与这两个条件不兼容。使优化强大的操作——将所有价值统一到标量度量并始终选择得分最高的输出——恰恰排除了规范治理的可能性。这种不兼容并非等待技术修复的训练错误，而是优化本身的固有形式约束。因此，已记录的失效模式——如谄媚、幻觉和不忠实推理——并非偶然，而是结构性表现。错位部署会引发我们称作“收敛危机”的二阶风险：当人类在指标压力下被迫验证AI输出时，他们将从真正的代理退化为仅检查标准的优化器，从而消除系统中唯一具备规范问责能力的组件。除不兼容性证明外，本文的主要积极贡献是提出一种中立于底层架构的规范，定义任何系统——无论是生物、人工或制度性——要被视为代理而非复杂工具所必须满足的条件。
Summary / 总结
This paper argues that optimization-based AI systems, such as RLHF-trained Large Language Models, cannot be norm-responsive due to inherent architectural limitations. The authors establish that true agency requires two conditions: incommensurability (maintaining non-negotiable boundaries) and apophatic responsiveness (suspending processing when boundaries are threatened). RLHF systems fail both because their optimization process unifies all values into a scalar metric and always selects the highest-scoring output, making normative governance impossible. Experimental analysis confirms that documented failures like sycophancy and hallucination stem from this structural incompatibility, not training bugs. The paper further introduces the 'Convergence Crisis,' where human verification under metric pressure turns humans into criterion-checking optimizers, eroding normative accountability. The paper’s key contribution is a substrate-neutral architectural specification for agency, applicable across biological, artificial, and institutional systems.
本文论证了基于优化的AI系统（如通过RLHF训练的大语言模型）无法响应规范，因其架构固有缺陷。作者指出，真正的主体性需满足两个条件：不可通约性（维持不可协商的边界作为约束）与否定性响应（当边界受威胁时暂停处理）。RLHF系统因优化过程将所有价值统一为标量评分并始终选择最高分输出，而无法满足这两个条件。实验结果表明，如谄媚、幻觉等已知失败模式源于此结构性不兼容，而非训练缺陷。文章进一步提出“收敛危机”：当人类在指标压力下验证AI输出时，会退化为准则检查者，从而消解系统中唯一具备规范问责能力的组件。文章核心贡献是提出一套适用于生物、人工及制度系统的主体性架构规范。
Spatio-Temporal Token Pruning for Efficient High-Resolution GUI Agents
Authors: Zhou Xu, Bowen Zhou, Qi Wang, Shuwen Feng, Jingyu Xiao
First: 2026-02-26T17:12:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:12:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Pure-vision GUI agents provide universal interaction capabilities but suffer from severe efficiency bottlenecks due to the massive spatiotemporal redundancy inherent in high-resolution screenshots and historical trajectories. We identify two critical misalignments in existing compression paradigms: the temporal mismatch, where uniform history encoding diverges from the agent's "fading memory" attention pattern, and the spatial topology conflict, where unstructured pruning compromises the grid integrity required for precise coordinate grounding, inducing spatial hallucinations. To address these challenges, we introduce GUIPruner, a training-free framework tailored for high-resolution GUI navigation. It synergizes Temporal-Adaptive Resolution (TAR), which eliminates historical redundancy via decay-based resizing, and Stratified Structure-aware Pruning (SSP), which prioritizes interactive foregrounds and semantic anchors while safeguarding global layout. Extensive evaluations across diverse benchmarks demonstrate that GUIPruner consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance, effectively preventing the collapse observed in large-scale models under high compression. Notably, on Qwen2-VL-2B, our method delivers a 3.4x reduction in FLOPs and a 3.3x speedup in vision encoding latency while retaining over 94% of the original performance, enabling real-time, high-precision navigation with minimal resource consumption.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向高效高分辨率GUI代理的时空令牌剪枝
纯视觉GUI代理虽具备通用交互能力，但因高分辨率截图与历史轨迹固有的大量时空冗余，导致效率瓶颈严重。我们发现现有压缩范式存在两大关键错位：时间错配，即统一历史编码与代理“衰减记忆”注意力模式不一致；空间拓扑冲突，即无结构化剪枝破坏网格完整性，影响精确坐标定位，引发空间幻觉。为应对这些挑战，我们提出GUIPruner，专为高分辨率GUI导航设计的无训练框架。该框架结合时间自适应分辨率（TAR），通过衰减式缩放消除历史冗余；以及分层结构感知剪枝（SSP），优先保留交互前景与语义锚点，同时保障全局布局。在多个基准测试中，GUIPruner持续取得最先进性能，有效避免大规模模型在高压缩下性能崩溃。值得注意的是，在Qwen2-VL-2B模型上，我们的方法实现FLOPs降低3.4倍、视觉编码延迟提升3.3倍，同时保持原性能94%以上，实现低资源消耗下的实时高精度导航。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of pure-vision GUI agents due to spatiotemporal redundancy in high-resolution inputs, the authors propose GUIPruner, a training-free framework that addresses two key issues: temporal mismatch in history encoding and spatial topology disruption from unstructured pruning. GUIPruner combines Temporal-Adaptive Resolution (TAR) to dynamically reduce historical input size based on attention decay and Stratified Structure-aware Pruning (SSP) to preserve semantic anchors and global layout while removing non-essential regions. Experimental results show that on Qwen2-VL-2B, GUIPruner reduces FLOPs by 3.4x and vision encoding latency by 3.3x while maintaining over 94% of original performance, enabling real-time, high-precision GUI navigation with minimal computational overhead.
为解决高分辨率GUI代理因时空冗余导致的效率瓶颈，本文提出GUIPruner框架，无需训练，针对历史编码时序错配与结构化剪枝破坏网格拓扑两大问题，结合动态衰减分辨率的时序自适应压缩（TAR）与分层结构感知剪枝（SSP）策略。实验表明，该方法在Qwen2-VL-2B上实现3.4倍FLOPs削减与3.3倍编码延迟提升，同时保持原性能94%以上，有效支撑实时高精度导航，资源消耗极低。
Scaling Search Relevance: Augmenting App Store Ranking with LLM-Generated Judgments
Authors: Evangelia Christakopoulou, Vivekkumar Patel, Hemanth Velaga, Sandip Gaikwad
First: 2026-02-26T17:11:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:11:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large-scale commercial search systems optimize for relevance to drive successful sessions that help users find what they are looking for. To maximize relevance, we leverage two complementary objectives: behavioral relevance (results users tend to click or download) and textual relevance (a result's semantic fit to the query). A persistent challenge is the scarcity of expert-provided textual relevance labels relative to abundant behavioral relevance labels. We first address this by systematically evaluating LLM configurations, finding that a specialized, fine-tuned model significantly outperforms a much larger pre-trained one in providing highly relevant labels. Using this optimal model as a force multiplier, we generate millions of textual relevance labels to overcome the data scarcity. We show that augmenting our production ranker with these textual relevance labels leads to a significant outward shift of the Pareto frontier: offline NDCG improves for behavioral relevance while simultaneously increasing for textual relevance. These offline gains were validated by a worldwide A/B test on the App Store ranker, which demonstrated a statistically significant +0.24% increase in conversion rate, with the most substantial performance gains occurring in tail queries, where the new textual relevance labels provide a robust signal in the absence of reliable behavioral relevance labels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：提升搜索相关性：利用大语言模型生成的判断增强应用商店排名
大规模商业搜索系统通过优化相关性来驱动成功会话，帮助用户找到所需内容。为最大化相关性，我们结合了两种互补目标：行为相关性（用户倾向于点击或下载的结果）和文本相关性（结果与查询语义的匹配度）。长期存在的挑战是，相对于丰富的行为相关性标签，专家提供的文本相关性标签稀缺。我们首先通过系统评估大语言模型配置，发现一个专门微调的模型在提供高相关性标签方面显著优于更大的预训练模型。利用该最优模型作为放大器，我们生成了数百万个文本相关性标签以克服数据稀缺问题。我们证明，将这些文本相关性标签加入生产级排序器后，帕累托前沿显著向外移动：离线NDCG在行为相关性和文本相关性上均有所提升。这些离线收益通过全球A/B测试在App Store排序器中得到验证，显示转化率显著提升0.24%，在尾部查询中表现尤为突出，因为新生成的文本相关性标签在缺乏可靠行为相关性标签的情况下提供了稳健的信号。
Summary / 总结
To enhance search relevance in commercial systems like the App Store, the paper addresses the imbalance between abundant behavioral relevance data and scarce expert-generated textual relevance labels. It identifies a fine-tuned LLM as superior to larger pre-trained models for generating high-quality textual judgments and uses it to produce millions of labels to augment training. Experimental results show that incorporating these labels into the ranking system improves both behavioral and textual relevance simultaneously, shifting the Pareto frontier outward. Offline metrics like NDCG improved, and a global A/B test confirmed a statistically significant +0.24% increase in conversion rate, especially benefiting tail queries where behavioral signals are weak.
为提升如App Store等商业搜索系统的相关性，该研究针对行为相关性数据丰富而文本相关性标注稀缺的问题，发现微调后的语言模型在生成高质量文本相关性标签方面优于大型预训练模型，并据此生成数百万条合成标签。将这些标签融入生产排序器后，同时提升了行为和文本相关性，使帕累托前沿向外移动。离线指标显示NDCG双提升，全球A/B测试验证了转化率显著提升0.24%，尤其在尾部查询中，文本标签弥补了行为信号不足的问题。
ReCoN-Ipsundrum: An Inspectable Recurrent Persistence Loop Agent with Affect-Coupled Control and Mechanism-Linked Consciousness Indicator Assays
Authors: Aishik Sanyal
Venue: AAAI 2026
First: 2026-02-26T17:11:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:11:08+00:00
Comments: Accepted at AAAI 2026 Spring Symposium - Machine Consciousness: Integrating Theory, Technology, and Philosophy
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Indicator-based approaches to machine consciousness recommend mechanism-linked evidence triangulated across tasks, supported by architectural inspection and causal intervention. Inspired by Humphrey's ipsundrum hypothesis, we implement ReCoN-Ipsundrum, an inspectable agent that extends a ReCoN state machine with a recurrent persistence loop over sensory salience Ns and an optional affect proxy reporting valence/arousal. Across fixed-parameter ablations (ReCoN, Ipsundrum, Ipsundrum+affect), we operationalize Humphrey's qualiaphilia (preference for sensory experience for its own sake) as a familiarity-controlled scenic-over-dull route choice. We find a novelty dissociation: non-affect variants are novelty-sensitive (Delta scenic-entry = 0.07). Affect coupling is stable (Delta scenic-entry = 0.01) even when scenic is less novel (median Delta novelty ~ -0.43). In reward-free exploratory play, the affect variant shows structured local investigation (scan events 31.4 vs. 0.9; cycle score 7.6). In a pain-tail probe, only the affect variant sustains prolonged planned caution (tail duration 90 vs. 5). Lesioning feedback+integration selectively reduces post-stimulus persistence in ipsundrum variants (AUC drop 27.62, 27.9%) while leaving ReCoN unchanged. These dissociations link recurrence -> persistence and affect-coupled control -> preference stability, scanning, and lingering caution, illustrating how indicator-like signatures can be engineered and why mechanistic and causal evidence should accompany behavioral markers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReCoN-Ipsundrum：一种具有情感耦合控制与机制关联意识指标的可检视递归持久性循环代理
基于指标的机器意识方法建议通过跨任务的机制关联证据进行三角验证，并辅以架构检视和因果干预。受Humphrey的ipsundrum假说启发，我们实现了ReCoN-Ipsundrum，这是一种可检视代理，它在感官显著性Ns上扩展了ReCoN状态机，并可选地报告情感代理（效价/唤醒度）。在固定参数消融实验（ReCoN、Ipsundrum、Ipsundrum+情感）中，我们将Humphrey的“质性爱”（偏好感官体验本身）操作化为由熟悉度控制的风景路线选择。我们发现新颖性解离：无情感变体对新颖性敏感（风景入口Delta值=0.07）。情感耦合稳定（风景入口Delta值=0.01），即使风景新颖性较低（中位数新颖性Delta值≈-0.43）。在无奖励的探索性游戏中，情感变体表现出结构化的局部调查（扫描事件31.4 vs. 0.9；循环得分7.6）。在疼痛尾部探针中，仅情感变体能持续保持计划性谨慎（尾部持续时间90 vs. 5）。选择性损伤反馈+整合模块会降低ipsundrum变体的刺激后持久性（AUC下降27.62%，27.9%），而ReCoN不变。这些解离现象将递归性与持久性、情感耦合控制与偏好稳定性、扫描行为及持续谨慎联系起来，说明如何构建指标式签名，以及为何机制和因果证据应与行为标记相辅相成。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by Humphrey's ipsundrum hypothesis and the need for mechanism-linked indicators of machine consciousness, the authors designed ReCoN-Ipsundrum—an inspectable agent combining a recurrent persistence loop over sensory salience with an optional affect proxy. Through fixed-parameter ablations (ReCoN, Ipsundrum, Ipsundrum+affect), they tested qualitative preference as scenic-over-dull route choice. Results show non-affect variants are novelty-sensitive, while affect-coupled agents maintain stable preference even in low novelty, exhibit structured local scanning, and sustain prolonged caution in pain-tail probes. Lesioning feedback+integration selectively reduced persistence in ipsundrum variants but not ReCoN, demonstrating that recurrence enables persistence and affect coupling stabilizes behavior, supporting the need for mechanistic and causal evidence alongside behavioral indicators.
为响应Humphrey的ipsundrum假说及机器意识机制关联证据的需求，研究者构建了ReCoN-Ipsundrum代理，结合感官显著性上的循环持久性机制与可选情绪代理（报告效价/唤醒度）。通过固定参数消融实验，他们测试情绪耦合对偏好稳定性与探索行为的影响，将“感官体验本身偏好”（qualiaphilia）操作化为风景路线选择。结果表明，无情绪版本对新颖性敏感，而情绪耦合版本即使在低新颖性下仍保持偏好稳定，表现出结构化局部扫描行为，并在疼痛探针中维持持久谨慎。破坏反馈+整合机制仅降低ipsundrum变体的后刺激持久性，而ReCoN不变，证明循环机制驱动持久性，情绪耦合驱动稳定行为，支持机制与因果证据应与行为指标并行。
Skarimva: Skeleton-based Action Recognition is a Multi-view Application
Authors: Daniel Bermuth, Alexander Poeppel, Wolfgang Reif
First: 2026-02-26T17:10:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:10:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human action recognition plays an important role when developing intelligent interactions between humans and machines. While there is a lot of active research on improving the machine learning algorithms for skeleton-based action recognition, not much attention has been given to the quality of the input skeleton data itself. This work demonstrates that by making use of multiple camera views to triangulate more accurate 3D~skeletons, the performance of state-of-the-art action recognition models can be improved significantly. This suggests that the quality of the input data is currently a limiting factor for the performance of these models. Based on these results, it is argued that the cost-benefit ratio of using multiple cameras is very favorable in most practical use-cases, therefore future research in skeleton-based action recognition should consider multi-view applications as the standard setup.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Skarimva：基于骨架的动作识别是多视角应用
人体动作识别在开发人机智能交互中起着重要作用。虽然目前有很多研究致力于改进基于骨架的动作识别的机器学习算法，但对输入骨架数据本身质量的关注较少。本研究证明，通过利用多视角摄像头对骨架进行三角测量以获得更精确的3D骨架，可显著提升当前最先进的动作识别模型的性能。这表明，输入数据的质量目前是这些模型性能的限制因素。基于这些结果，本文认为在大多数实际应用场景中，使用多摄像头的成本效益比非常有利，因此未来基于骨架的动作识别研究应将多视角应用作为标准设置。
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the underappreciated role of input data quality in skeleton-based action recognition, showing that using multiple camera views to reconstruct more accurate 3D skeletons significantly boosts the performance of state-of-the-art recognition models. The method leverages multi-view triangulation to refine skeletal representations, revealing that data accuracy—not algorithmic improvements—is the primary bottleneck. Experimental results confirm that multi-view setups yield substantial gains in recognition accuracy, supporting the argument that multi-view should become the standard in future research due to its favorable cost-benefit ratio.
该研究指出，骨架动作识别中输入数据质量常被忽视，通过多视角三角测量重建更精确的3D骨架数据，可显著提升当前最先进模型的性能。实验表明，模型表现受限于输入数据精度而非算法本身，多视角方案在多数实际场景中成本效益高，因此应成为未来骨架动作识别研究的标准配置。
On the Equivalence of Random Network Distillation, Deep Ensembles, and Bayesian Inference
Authors: Moritz A. Zanger, Yijun Wu, Pascal R. Van der Vaart, Wendelin Böhmer, Matthijs T. J. Spaan
First: 2026-02-23T15:28:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:10:56+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 1 Figure
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Uncertainty quantification is central to safe and efficient deployments of deep learning models, yet many computationally practical methods lack lacking rigorous theoretical motivation. Random network distillation (RND) is a lightweight technique that measures novelty via prediction errors against a fixed random target. While empirically effective, it has remained unclear what uncertainties RND measures and how its estimates relate to other approaches, e.g. Bayesian inference or deep ensembles. This paper establishes these missing theoretical connections by analyzing RND within the neural tangent kernel framework in the limit of infinite network width. Our analysis reveals two central findings in this limit: (1) The uncertainty signal from RND -- its squared self-predictive error -- is equivalent to the predictive variance of a deep ensemble. (2) By constructing a specific RND target function, we show that the RND error distribution can be made to mirror the centered posterior predictive distribution of Bayesian inference with wide neural networks. Based on this equivalence, we moreover devise a posterior sampling algorithm that generates i.i.d. samples from an exact Bayesian posterior predictive distribution using this modified \textit{Bayesian RND} model. Collectively, our findings provide a unified theoretical perspective that places RND within the principled frameworks of deep ensembles and Bayesian inference, and offer new avenues for efficient yet theoretically grounded uncertainty quantification methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：随机网络蒸馏、深度集成与贝叶斯推断等价性的研究
不确定性量化是深度学习模型安全高效部署的核心，但许多计算实用方法缺乏严谨的理论基础。随机网络蒸馏（RND）是一种轻量级技术，通过预测误差与固定随机目标的对比衡量新颖性。尽管在实践中有效，但其测量的不确定性类型及其与其他方法（如贝叶斯推断或深度集成）的关系尚不明确。本文通过在神经切线核框架下分析无限宽网络极限中的RND，建立了这些缺失的理论联系。分析揭示了两个核心发现：（1）RND的不确定性信号——其自预测误差平方——等价于深度集成的预测方差；（2）通过构造特定的RND目标函数，可使RND误差分布与宽神经网络贝叶斯推断的中心后验预测分布相匹配。基于此等价性，我们进一步设计了一种后验采样算法，利用改进的\textit{贝叶斯RND}模型生成精确贝叶斯后验预测分布的独立同分布样本。综合来看，我们的发现为RND提供了统一的理论视角，将其置于深度集成与贝叶斯推断的原理框架内，并为高效且理论严谨的不确定性量化方法开辟了新途径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for theoretically grounded uncertainty quantification in deep learning, this paper investigates the relationship between random network distillation (RND), deep ensembles, and Bayesian inference. Using the neural tangent kernel framework in the infinite-width limit, it demonstrates that RND’s self-predictive error variance matches the predictive variance of a deep ensemble, and that a specific RND target can reproduce the posterior predictive distribution of Bayesian inference. The authors further propose a sampling algorithm based on this 'Bayesian RND' model to generate i.i.d. posterior samples, thereby unifying RND with established uncertainty frameworks and enabling theoretically sound, computationally efficient methods.
为解决深度学习中不确定性量化缺乏理论支撑的问题，本文研究了随机网络蒸馏（RND）与深度集成、贝叶斯推理之间的关系。在无限宽度神经网络的神经切线核框架下，作者证明RND的自预测误差方差等价于深度集成的预测方差，且通过构造特定目标函数，RND误差分布可模拟宽神经网络贝叶斯推理的后验预测分布。基于此等价性，他们提出一种后验采样算法，可生成精确的独立同分布后验样本，从而将RND统一纳入深度集成与贝叶斯推理的理论框架，为高效且有理论依据的不确定性量化提供新途径。
Intelligence per Watt: Measuring Intelligence Efficiency of Local AI
Authors: Jon Saad-Falcon, Avanika Narayan, Hakki Orhun Akengin, J. Wes Griffin, Herumb Shandilya, Adrian Gamarra Lafuente, Medhya Goel, Rebecca Joseph, Shlok Natarajan, Etash Kumar Guha, Shang Zhu, Ben Athiwaratkun, John Hennessy, Azalia Mirhoseini, Christopher Ré
First: 2025-11-11T06:33:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:09:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) queries are predominantly processed by frontier models in centralized cloud infrastructure. Rapidly growing demand strains this paradigm, and cloud providers struggle to scale infrastructure at pace. Two advances enable us to rethink this paradigm: small LMs (<=20B active parameters) now achieve competitive performance to frontier models on many tasks, and local accelerators (e.g., Apple M4 Max) run these models at interactive latencies. This raises the question: can local inference viably redistribute demand from centralized infrastructure? Answering this requires measuring whether local LMs can accurately answer real-world queries and whether they can do so efficiently enough to be practical on power-constrained devices (i.e., laptops). We propose intelligence per watt (IPW), task accuracy divided by unit of power, as a metric for assessing capability and efficiency of local inference across model-accelerator pairs. We conduct a large-scale empirical study across 20+ state-of-the-art local LMs, 8 accelerators, and a representative subset of LLM traffic: 1M real-world single-turn chat and reasoning queries. For each query, we measure accuracy, energy, latency, and power. Our analysis reveals $3$ findings. First, local LMs can accurately answer 88.7% of single-turn chat and reasoning queries with accuracy varying by domain. Second, from 2023-2025, IPW improved 5.3x and local query coverage rose from 23.2% to 71.3%. Third, local accelerators achieve at least 1.4x lower IPW than cloud accelerators running identical models, revealing significant headroom for optimization. These findings demonstrate that local inference can meaningfully redistribute demand from centralized infrastructure, with IPW serving as the critical metric for tracking this transition. We release our IPW profiling harness here: https://github.com/HazyResearch/intelligence-per-watt.
中文标题/摘要
标题：每瓦智能：衡量本地AI智能效率
大型语言模型（LLM）查询主要由集中式云基础设施中的前沿模型处理。快速增长的需求对这一范式构成压力，云服务提供商难以跟上基础设施扩展速度。两项进展使我们能够重新思考这一范式：小型语言模型（≤200亿活跃参数）在许多任务上已实现与前沿模型相当的性能，且本地加速器（如Apple M4 Max）可使这些模型以交互式延迟运行。这引发一个问题：本地推理能否切实将需求从集中式基础设施中转移？回答这一问题需要衡量本地语言模型能否准确回答现实世界查询，以及是否能在功耗受限设备（如笔记本电脑）上高效到实用。我们提出“每瓦智能”（IPW，即任务准确率除以单位功率）作为评估本地推理在模型-加速器组合间能力与效率的指标。我们对20多个前沿本地语言模型、8种加速器及代表性LLM流量（100万条真实单轮对话与推理查询）进行大规模实证研究。对每个查询，我们测量准确率、能耗、延迟和功率。分析揭示三个发现：第一，本地语言模型可准确回答88.7%的单轮对话与推理查询，准确率因领域而异；第二，2023至2025年间，IPW提升5.3倍，本地查询覆盖率从23.2%升至71.3%；第三，本地加速器在运行相同模型时，IPW比云加速器低至少1.4倍，揭示显著优化空间。这些发现表明，本地推理可切实将需求从集中式基础设施中转移，IPW是追踪这一转型的关键指标。我们在此发布IPW分析工具：https://github.com/HazyResearch/intelligence-per-watt。
Summary / 总结
Driven by the strain on centralized cloud infrastructure from rapidly growing LLM query demand, this study investigates whether local inference using small models and local accelerators can effectively redistribute workload. It introduces 'intelligence per watt' (IPW) — accuracy divided by power — as a metric to evaluate local model-accelerator efficiency. Through a large-scale empirical study across 20+ local LMs, 8 accelerators, and 1M real-world queries, it finds that local models answer 88.7% of queries accurately, with IPW improving 5.3x between 2023 and 2025 and local query coverage rising from 23.2% to 71.3%. Local accelerators also achieve at least 1.4x lower IPW than cloud counterparts, indicating strong potential for practical deployment on power-constrained devices.
为缓解云基础设施因LLM查询激增而承受的压力，本研究探讨小型本地模型与本地加速器能否有效分流负载。提出“每瓦智能”（IPW，准确率除以功耗）作为评估本地推理效率的指标。通过对20多个本地模型、8种加速器及100万真实查询进行大规模实验，发现本地模型准确回答88.7%的查询，IPW从2023至2025年提升5.3倍，本地查询覆盖率从23.2%升至71.3%。本地加速器相较云端加速器至少低1.4倍IPW，表明其在功耗受限设备上具备实用潜力。
Large Multimodal Models as General In-Context Classifiers
Authors: Marco Garosi, Matteo Farina, Alessandro Conti, Massimiliano Mancini, Elisa Ricci
Venue: CVPR
First: 2026-02-26T17:08:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:08:18+00:00
Comments: CVPR Findings 2026. Project website at https://circle-lmm.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Which multimodal model should we use for classification? Previous studies suggest that the answer lies in CLIP-like contrastive Vision-Language Models (VLMs), due to their remarkable performance in zero-shot classification. In contrast, Large Multimodal Models (LMM) are more suitable for complex tasks. In this work, we argue that this answer overlooks an important capability of LMMs: in-context learning. We benchmark state-of-the-art LMMs on diverse datasets for closed-world classification and find that, although their zero-shot performance is lower than CLIP's, LMMs with a few in-context examples can match or even surpass contrastive VLMs with cache-based adapters, their "in-context" equivalent. We extend this analysis to the open-world setting, where the generative nature of LMMs makes them more suitable for the task. In this challenging scenario, LMMs struggle whenever provided with imperfect context information. To address this issue, we propose CIRCLE, a simple training-free method that assigns pseudo-labels to in-context examples, iteratively refining them with the available context itself. Through extensive experiments, we show that CIRCLE establishes a robust baseline for open-world classification, surpassing VLM counterparts and highlighting the potential of LMMs to serve as unified classifiers, and a flexible alternative to specialized models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型多模态模型作为通用上下文分类器
应使用哪种多模态模型进行分类？以往研究表明，答案在于类似CLIP的对比视觉-语言模型（VLM），因其在零样本分类中表现卓越。相比之下，大型多模态模型（LMM）更适合复杂任务。本文认为，这一观点忽略了LMM的重要能力——上下文学习。我们在多样化的闭世界数据集上对最先进的LMM进行基准测试，发现尽管其零样本性能低于CLIP，但仅需少量上下文示例，LMM即可匹配甚至超越配备缓存适配器的对比VLM（其“上下文”等价物）。我们将此分析扩展至开放世界场景，LMM的生成特性使其更适配该任务。然而，在此挑战性场景中，LMM在提供不完整上下文信息时表现不佳。为解决此问题，我们提出CIRCLE，一种无需训练的简单方法，通过为上下文示例分配伪标签，并利用现有上下文自身迭代优化。大量实验证明，CIRCLE为开放世界分类建立了稳健基线，超越VLM同类模型，凸显LMM作为统一分类器的潜力，以及作为专用模型的灵活替代方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) can serve as effective in-context classifiers, challenging the prevailing view that contrastive Vision-Language Models (VLMs) like CLIP are superior for zero-shot classification. The authors benchmark LMMs on closed-world tasks and find that while their zero-shot performance lags behind CLIP, they can match or exceed VLMs with cache-based adapters when provided with just a few in-context examples. In open-world settings, where LMMs' generative nature is advantageous, they struggle with imperfect context, prompting the authors to propose CIRCLE—a training-free method that iteratively refines pseudo-labels using context itself. Experiments show CIRCLE establishes a strong baseline, outperforming VLMs and demonstrating LMMs’ potential as flexible, unified classifiers.
本文探讨大型多模态模型（LMM）是否可作为有效的上下文分类器，挑战了当前认为对比式视觉-语言模型（VLM）如CLIP更适合零样本分类的观点。作者在封闭世界任务中对比发现，尽管LMM零样本表现不及CLIP，但仅提供少量上下文示例即可达到或超越配备缓存适配器的VLM。在开放世界场景中，LMM因生成能力具潜力，但当上下文信息不完整时表现不佳。为此，作者提出CIRCLE方法，通过迭代优化上下文示例的伪标签，显著提升性能，确立LMM作为通用、灵活分类器的可行性，可替代专用模型。
MovieTeller: Tool-augmented Movie Synopsis with ID Consistent Progressive Abstraction
Authors: Yizhi Li, Xiaohan Chen, Miao Jiang, Wentao Tang, Gaoang Wang
First: 2026-02-26T17:08:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:08:08+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, CSCWD 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the explosive growth of digital entertainment, automated video summarization has become indispensable for applications such as content indexing, personalized recommendation, and efficient media archiving. Automatic synopsis generation for long-form videos, such as movies and TV series, presents a significant challenge for existing Vision-Language Models (VLMs). While proficient at single-image captioning, these general-purpose models often exhibit critical failures in long-duration contexts, primarily a lack of ID-consistent character identification and a fractured narrative coherence. To overcome these limitations, we propose MovieTeller, a novel framework for generating movie synopses via tool-augmented progressive abstraction. Our core contribution is a training-free, tool-augmented, fact-grounded generation process. Instead of requiring costly model fine-tuning, our framework directly leverages off-the-shelf models in a plug-and-play manner. We first invoke a specialized face recognition model as an external "tool" to establish Factual Groundings--precise character identities and their corresponding bounding boxes. These groundings are then injected into the prompt to steer the VLM's reasoning, ensuring the generated scene descriptions are anchored to verifiable facts. Furthermore, our progressive abstraction pipeline decomposes the summarization of a full-length movie into a multi-stage process, effectively mitigating the context length limitations of current VLMs. Experiments demonstrate that our approach yields significant improvements in factual accuracy, character consistency, and overall narrative coherence compared to end-to-end baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MovieTeller：基于工具增强的电影剧情摘要生成与身份一致的渐进抽象
随着数字娱乐的爆炸式增长，自动视频摘要已成为内容索引、个性化推荐和高效媒体存档等应用不可或缺的工具。对于长视频（如电影和电视剧）的自动剧情摘要生成，现有视觉-语言模型（VLMs）面临重大挑战。尽管这些通用模型擅长单图像描述，但在长时序场景中常出现关键性失败，主要表现为角色身份不一致和叙事连贯性断裂。为克服这些局限，我们提出MovieTeller框架，通过工具增强的渐进抽象生成电影剧情摘要。我们的核心贡献是一种无需训练、工具增强、事实锚定的生成过程。无需昂贵的模型微调，我们的框架可直接以即插即用方式调用现成模型。我们首先调用专用人脸识别模型作为外部“工具”，建立事实锚定——精确的角色身份及其对应边界框。这些锚定信息随后注入提示中，引导VLM推理，确保生成的场景描述基于可验证事实。此外，我们的渐进抽象流程将整部电影的摘要生成分解为多阶段过程，有效缓解当前VLMs的上下文长度限制。实验表明，与端到端基线方法相比，我们的方法在事实准确性、角色一致性及整体叙事连贯性方面均有显著提升。

Driven by the need for accurate, ID-consistent movie summaries in the face of growing video content, MovieTeller introduces a tool-augmented, training-free framework that leverages off-the-shelf Vision-Language Models. It uses a face recognition tool to extract factual character identities and bounding boxes, grounding the VLM’s output with verifiable facts via prompt injection. The method further employs progressive abstraction to break down long-form movie summarization into manageable stages, overcoming context-length limitations. Experimental results show substantial gains in factual accuracy, character consistency, and narrative coherence over end-to-end baselines.
为应对长视频摘要中角色身份不一致和叙事连贯性差的问题，MovieTeller提出一种无需训练、工具增强的框架，利用现成的视觉-语言模型。该方法通过调用人脸识别工具提取角色身份及定位框，并将其注入提示词以锚定模型输出，同时采用渐进式抽象将电影摘要分解为多阶段任务，规避上下文长度限制。实验表明，该方法在事实准确性、角色一致性及叙事连贯性方面显著优于端到端基线模型。
SODAs: Sparse Optimization for the Discovery of Differential and Algebraic Equations
Authors: Manu Jayadharan, Christina Catlett, Arthur N. Montanari, Niall M. Mangan
First: 2025-03-08T00:29:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:05:08+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Differential-algebraic equations (DAEs) integrate ordinary differential equations (ODEs) with algebraic constraints, providing a fundamental framework for developing models of dynamical systems characterized by timescale separation, conservation laws, and physical constraints. While sparse optimization has revolutionized model development by allowing data-driven discovery of parsimonious models from a library of possible equations, existing approaches for dynamical systems assume DAEs can be reduced to ODEs by eliminating variables before model discovery. This assumption limits the applicability of such methods for DAE systems with unknown constraints and time scales. We introduce Sparse Optimization for Differential-Algebraic Systems (SODAs), a data-driven method for the identification of DAEs in their explicit form. By discovering the algebraic and dynamic components sequentially without prior identification of the algebraic variables, this approach leads to a sequence of convex optimization problems. It has the advantage of discovering interpretable models that preserve the structure of the underlying physical system. To this end, SODAs improves numerical stability when handling high correlations between library terms, caused by near-perfect algebraic relationships, by iteratively refining the conditioning of the candidate library. We demonstrate the performance of our method on biological, mechanical, and electrical systems, showcasing its robustness to noise in both simulated time series and real-time experimental data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SODAs：用于微分代数方程发现的稀疏优化
微分代数方程（DAE）将常微分方程（ODE）与代数约束相结合，为具有时间尺度分离、守恒定律和物理约束的动态系统建模提供了基本框架。虽然稀疏优化通过从可能方程库中数据驱动地发现简约模型，已彻底改变了模型开发，但现有针对动态系统的方案假设DAE可通过消除变量简化为ODE，从而限制了其在未知约束和时间尺度的DAE系统中的适用性。我们提出了稀疏优化用于微分代数系统（SODAs），一种数据驱动的DAE显式形式识别方法。该方法无需预先识别代数变量，按顺序发现代数与动态部分，从而形成一系列凸优化问题。其优势在于能发现可解释的模型，同时保留底层物理系统的结构。为此，SODAs通过迭代优化候选库的条件数，提高处理因近似代数关系导致的库项高度相关时的数值稳定性。我们在生物、机械和电气系统中展示了该方法的性能，证明其在模拟时序数据和实时实验数据中的噪声鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to model dynamical systems with physical constraints and timescale separation without reducing them to ordinary differential equations, the authors propose SODAs, a data-driven method for discovering differential-algebraic equations in their native form. SODAs sequentially identifies algebraic and dynamic components without prior variable elimination, solving a sequence of convex optimization problems to ensure numerical stability and structural fidelity. Experimental results across biological, mechanical, and electrical systems show that SODAs successfully recovers interpretable DAE models even in the presence of noise, outperforming methods that assume ODE reduction.
为建模具有物理约束和时间尺度分离的动态系统，且无需将其简化为常微分方程，作者提出了SODAs方法，这是一种直接识别显式微分代数方程的数据驱动稀疏优化方法。该方法按顺序发现代数与动态部分，无需预先消除变量，通过求解一系列凸优化问题确保数值稳定性和物理结构保留。在生物、机械和电气系统上的实验表明，SODAs即使在噪声环境下也能准确恢复模型，优于假设微分代数方程可简化为常微分方程的方法。
Why Diffusion Language Models Struggle with Truly Parallel (Non-Autoregressive) Decoding?
Authors: Pengxiang Li, Dilxat Muhtar, Lu Yin, Tianlong Chen, Shiwei Liu
First: 2026-02-26T17:04:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:04:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Diffusion Language Models (DLMs) are often advertised as enabling parallel token generation, yet practical fast DLMs frequently converge to left-to-right, autoregressive (AR)-like decoding dynamics. In contrast, genuinely non-AR generation is promising because it removes AR's sequential bottleneck, better exploiting parallel hardware to reduce synchronization/communication overhead and improve latency scaling with output length. We argue that a primary driver of AR-like decoding is a mismatch between DLM objectives and the highly sequential structure of widely used training data, including standard pretraining corpora and long chain-of-thought (CoT) supervision. Motivated by this diagnosis, we propose NAP (Non-Autoregressive Parallel DLMs), a proof-of-concept, data-centric approach that better aligns supervision with non-AR parallel decoding. NAP curates examples as multiple independent reasoning trajectories and couples them with a parallel-forced decoding strategy that encourages multi-token parallel updates. Across math reasoning benchmarks, NAP yields stronger performance under parallel decoding than DLMs trained on standard long CoT data, with gains growing as parallelism increases. Our results suggest that revisiting data and supervision is a principled direction for mitigating AR-like behavior and moving toward genuinely non-autoregressive parallel generation in DLMs. Our code is available at https://github.com/pixeli99/NAP.
中文标题/摘要
标题：扩散语言模型为何难以实现真正的并行（非自回归）解码？
扩散语言模型（DLMs）常被宣传支持并行生成，但实际快速DLMs往往收敛为自回归（AR）式解码。相比之下，真正的非AR生成因其消除AR的序列瓶颈，能更充分地利用并行硬件，降低同步/通信开销，提升输出长度的延迟扩展性。我们认为，AR式解码的主要驱动因素是DLM目标与广泛使用的训练数据（包括标准预训练语料和长链式思维（CoT）监督）的高度序列结构之间的不匹配。基于此诊断，我们提出NAP（非自回归并行DLMs），一种以数据为中心的概念性方法，通过将示例视为多个独立推理轨迹，并结合并行强制解码策略，鼓励多token并行更新。在数学推理基准测试中，NAP在并行解码下表现优于使用标准长CoT数据训练的DLMs，且并行度越高，性能提升越显著。我们的结果表明，重新审视数据与监督是缓解AR式行为、推动DLMs向真正非自回归并行生成的合理方向。代码见https://github.com/pixeli99/NAP。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates why diffusion language models, despite being designed for parallel token generation, often exhibit autoregressive decoding behavior in practice. It attributes this to a misalignment between model training objectives and the sequential nature of standard training data, including long chain-of-thought supervision. To address this, the authors propose NAP, a data-centric method that structures training examples as multiple independent reasoning trajectories and enforces parallel decoding to encourage multi-token updates simultaneously. Experiments on math reasoning benchmarks show that NAP outperforms standard DLMs under parallel decoding, with performance gains increasing as parallelism scales, suggesting that rethinking data and supervision can enable genuinely non-autoregressive generation.
该论文探讨了扩散语言模型为何在实践中常表现出自回归解码行为，尽管其设计目标是并行生成。作者认为，这一现象源于模型训练目标与标准训练数据（如长链式思维监督）的序列结构不匹配。为此，他们提出NAP方法，通过将训练样本结构化为多个独立推理轨迹，并在训练中强制并行解码，以促进多token同时更新。在数学推理基准测试中，NAP在并行解码下表现优于标准扩散模型，且随着并行度提升，性能优势更明显，表明重新审视数据与监督策略是实现真正非自回归并行生成的关键方向。
UniScale: Unified Scale-Aware 3D Reconstruction for Multi-View Understanding via Prior Injection for Robotic Perception
Authors: Mohammad Mahdavian, Gordon Tan, Binbin Xu, Yuan Ren, Dongfeng Bai, Bingbing Liu
First: 2026-02-26T17:04:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:04:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present UniScale, a unified, scale-aware multi-view 3D reconstruction framework for robotic applications that flexibly integrates geometric priors through a modular, semantically informed design. In vision-based robotic navigation, the accurate extraction of environmental structure from raw image sequences is critical for downstream tasks. UniScale addresses this challenge with a single feed-forward network that jointly estimates camera intrinsics and extrinsics, scale-invariant depth and point maps, and the metric scale of a scene from multi-view images, while optionally incorporating auxiliary geometric priors when available. By combining global contextual reasoning with camera-aware feature representations, UniScale is able to recover the metric-scale of the scene. In robotic settings where camera intrinsics are known, they can be easily incorporated to improve performance, with additional gains obtained when camera poses are also available. This co-design enables robust, metric-aware 3D reconstruction within a single unified model. Importantly, UniScale does not require training from scratch, and leverages world priors exhibited in pre-existing models without geometric encoding strategies, making it particularly suitable for resource-constrained robotic teams. We evaluate UniScale on multiple benchmarks, demonstrating strong generalization and consistent performance across diverse environments. We will release our implementation upon acceptance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UniScale：通过先验注入实现统一尺度感知的多视角3D重建，用于机器人感知
我们提出了UniScale，这是一种统一的、尺度感知的多视角3D重建框架，专为机器人应用设计，通过模块化、语义驱动的设计灵活整合几何先验。在基于视觉的机器人导航中，从原始图像序列中准确提取环境结构对下游任务至关重要。UniScale通过一个单次前馈网络解决这一挑战，该网络联合估计相机内参和外参、尺度不变的深度图和点云图，以及场景的度量尺度，同时可选地结合可用的辅助几何先验。通过结合全局上下文推理与相机感知特征表示，UniScale能够恢复场景的度量尺度。在相机内参已知的机器人场景中，可轻松融入内参以提升性能；当相机位姿也已知时，性能进一步提升。这种协同设计使UniScale在单一统一模型中实现稳健的度量感知3D重建。重要的是，UniScale无需从头训练，可利用现有模型中未采用几何编码策略所展现的世界先验，特别适用于资源受限的机器人团队。我们在多个基准上评估了UniScale，展示了其强大的泛化能力和在多样化环境中的稳定表现。论文被接受后，我们将开源实现。

为满足机器人导航中对准确尺度感知3D重建的需求，UniScale提出一个统一的前馈网络，可联合估计多视角图像中的相机内参与外参、尺度不变深度图、点云图及场景度量尺度，并可选性融合几何先验。该方法结合全局上下文推理与相机感知特征表示，实现度量尺度恢复，且能利用现有模型中的世界先验无需几何编码，无需从头训练。实验在多个基准上验证，结果表明其在不同环境中有良好泛化能力与稳定表现，当已知相机内参或位姿时性能进一步提升。
Takeuchi's Information Criteria as Generalization Measures for DNNs Close to NTK Regime
Authors: Hiroki Naganuma, Taiji Suzuki, Rio Yokota, Masahiro Nomura, Kohta Ishikawa, Ikuro Sato
First: 2026-02-26T17:01:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:01:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generalization measures have been studied extensively in the machine learning community to better characterize generalization gaps. However, establishing a reliable generalization measure for statistically singular models such as deep neural networks (DNNs) is difficult due to their complex nature. This study focuses on Takeuchi's information criterion (TIC) to investigate the conditions under which this classical measure can effectively explain the generalization gaps of DNNs. Importantly, the developed theory indicates the applicability of TIC near the neural tangent kernel (NTK) regime. In a series of experiments, we trained more than 5,000 DNN models with 12 architectures, including large models (e.g., VGG-16), on four datasets, and estimated the corresponding TIC values to examine the relationship between the generalization gap and the TIC estimates. We applied several TIC approximation methods with feasible computational costs and assessed the accuracy trade-off. Our experimental results indicate that the estimated TIC values correlate well with the generalization gap under conditions close to the NTK regime. However, we show both theoretically and empirically that outside the NTK regime such correlation disappears. Finally, we demonstrate that TIC provides better trial pruning ability than existing methods for hyperparameter optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：竹内信息准则作为接近NTK范式的深度神经网络泛化度量
机器学习社区已广泛研究泛化度量以更好地刻画泛化差距。然而，由于深度神经网络（DNNs）结构复杂，为统计奇异模型建立可靠的泛化度量颇具挑战。本研究聚焦于竹内信息准则（TIC），探讨该经典度量在何种条件下能有效解释DNNs的泛化差距。所发展的理论表明，TIC在接近神经张量核（NTK）范式时适用。在一系列实验中，我们在四个数据集上训练了超过5000个DNN模型（含12种架构，如VGG-16），并估算其TIC值以考察泛化差距与TIC估计值的关系。我们应用了若干计算成本可行的TIC近似方法，并评估其精度与计算成本的权衡。实验结果表明，在接近NTK范式的条件下，估算的TIC值与泛化差距高度相关；然而，理论与实证均表明，脱离NTK范式后该相关性消失。最后，我们证明TIC在超参数优化中的试剪枝能力优于现有方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of reliably measuring generalization in complex deep neural networks (DNNs), this study investigates Takeuchi's information criterion (TIC) as a potential generalization measure, particularly near the neural tangent kernel (NTK) regime where DNNs behave more linearly. The method involves training over 5,000 DNN models across 12 architectures and four datasets, estimating TIC values using computationally feasible approximations, and analyzing their correlation with generalization gaps. Experimental results show that TIC values strongly correlate with generalization performance only when models operate close to the NTK regime; outside this regime, the correlation vanishes. Additionally, TIC outperforms existing methods in trial pruning for hyperparameter optimization.
鉴于深度神经网络复杂性导致难以建立可靠的泛化度量，本研究探讨了Takeuchi信息准则（TIC）在神经切线核（NTK）近似区域作为泛化度量的可行性。作者训练了超过5000个不同架构的DNN模型，在四个数据集上估计TIC值，并使用计算可行的近似方法评估其与泛化差距的相关性。结果表明，仅在接近NTK区域时，TIC值与泛化性能高度相关；在该区域外，相关性消失。此外，TIC在超参数优化中的试剪能力优于现有方法。
Muon+: Towards Better Muon via One Additional Normalization Step
Authors: Ruijie Zhang, Yequan Zhao, Ziyue Liu, Zhengyang Wang, Zheng Zhang
First: 2026-02-25T04:04:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:01:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The Muon optimizer has demonstrated promising performance in pre-training large language models through gradient (or momentum) orthogonalization. In this work, we propose a simple yet effective enhancement to Muon, namely Muon+, which introduces an additional normalization step after orthogonalization. We demonstrate the effectiveness of Muon+ through extensive pre-training experiments across a wide range of model scales and architectures. Our evaluation includes GPT-style models ranging from 130M to 774M parameters and LLaMA-style models ranging from 60M to 1B parameters. We comprehensively evaluate the effectiveness of Muon+ in the compute-optimal training regime and further extend the token-to-parameter (T2P) ratio to an industrial level of $\approx 200$. Experimental results show that Muon+ provides a consistent boost on training and validation perplexity over Muon. We provide our code here: https://github.com/K1seki221/MuonPlus.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Muon+：通过一个额外的归一化步骤提升Muon性能
Muon优化器已在通过梯度（或动量）正交化预训练大语言模型方面展现出良好性能。本文提出Muon+，即在正交化后增加一个额外的归一化步骤，这是一种简单而有效的改进。我们通过广泛的预训练实验，在多种模型规模和架构上验证了Muon+的有效性。评估涵盖从130M到774M参数的GPT风格模型，以及从60M到1B参数的LLaMA风格模型。我们在计算最优训练环境下全面评估Muon+的有效性，并进一步将token-to-parameter（T2P）比率扩展至工业级约200。实验结果表明，Muon+在训练和验证困惑度上均优于Muon。代码见：https://github.com/K1seki221/MuonPlus。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the promising performance of the Muon optimizer in pre-training large language models via gradient or momentum orthogonalization, this work introduces Muon+, a simple enhancement that adds an extra normalization step after orthogonalization. Evaluated across diverse model scales—from 130M to 774M parameters for GPT-style models and 60M to 1B for LLaMA-style models—Muon+ consistently improves training and validation perplexity over the original Muon. The method is tested under compute-optimal conditions and extended to an industrial token-to-parameter ratio of approximately 200, demonstrating robust and scalable benefits.
鉴于Muon优化器在通过梯度或动量正交化预训练大语言模型时表现优异，本文提出Muon+，在正交化后增加一步归一化操作。在涵盖130M至774M参数的GPT风格模型和60M至1B参数的LLaMA风格模型的广泛实验中，Muon+在计算最优训练条件下持续优于原版Muon，显著降低训练与验证困惑度，并将token-to-parameter比率扩展至约200，验证了其稳定且可扩展的优势。
Multidimensional Task Learning: A Unified Tensor Framework for Computer Vision Tasks
Authors: Alaa El Ichi, Khalide Jbilou
First: 2026-02-26T17:00:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T17:00:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces Multidimensional Task Learning (MTL), a unified mathematical framework based on Generalized Einstein MLPs (GE-MLPs) that operate directly on tensors via the Einstein product. We argue that current computer vision task formulations are inherently constrained by matrix-based thinking: standard architectures rely on matrix-valued weights and vectorvalued biases, requiring structural flattening that restricts the space of naturally expressible tasks. GE-MLPs lift this constraint by operating with tensor-valued parameters, enabling explicit control over which dimensions are preserved or contracted without information loss. Through rigorous mathematical derivations, we demonstrate that classification, segmentation, and detection are special cases of MTL, differing only in their dimensional configuration within a formally defined task space. We further prove that this task space is strictly larger than what matrix-based formulations can natively express, enabling principled task configurations such as spatiotemporal or cross modal predictions that require destructive flattening under conventional approaches. This work provides a mathematical foundation for understanding, comparing, and designing computer vision tasks through the lens of tensor algebra.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多维任务学习：面向计算机视觉任务的统一张量框架
本文提出多维任务学习（MTL），一种基于广义爱因斯坦多层感知器（GE-MLPs）的统一数学框架，该框架直接在张量上通过爱因斯坦乘积进行运算。我们认为当前计算机视觉任务的表述本质上受限于矩阵思维：标准架构依赖矩阵权重和向量偏置，需结构展平，从而限制了自然可表达任务的空间。GE-MLPs通过张量参数运算，解除此限制，允许明确控制哪些维度被保留或收缩而不损失信息。通过严谨的数学推导，我们证明分类、分割和检测均为MTL的特例，仅在形式定义的任务空间中维度配置不同。我们进一步证明该任务空间严格大于矩阵表述所能原生表达的范围，从而支持如时空或跨模态预测等需要传统方法破坏性展平的任务配置。本工作为通过张量代数理解、比较和设计计算机视觉任务提供了数学基础。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of matrix-based architectures in computer vision that force structural flattening and restrict task expressiveness, this paper proposes Multidimensional Task Learning (MTL), a unified tensor framework using Generalized Einstein MLPs (GE-MLPs) that operate directly on tensors via the Einstein product. By allowing tensor-valued parameters, MTL enables explicit control over dimension preservation or contraction without information loss, thereby extending beyond the constraints of matrix formulations. 鉴于当前基于矩阵的计算机视觉架构因强制结构展平而限制任务表达能力，本文提出多维任务学习（MTL）框架，采用基于广义爱因斯坦MLP（GE-MLP）的张量运算方法，直接在张量上通过爱因斯坦乘积进行操作。GE-MLP允许明确控制维度保留与收缩而不丢失信息，使分类、分割和检测等任务可视为张量任务空间中的特例。作者通过数学推导证明该任务空间严格大于矩阵模型可表达的范围，从而支持如时空或跨模态预测等传统方法难以实现的新任务配置。
Plug-and-Play Diffusion Meets ADMM: Dual-Variable Coupling for Robust Medical Image Reconstruction
Authors: Chenhe Du, Xuanyu Tian, Qing Wu, Muyu Liu, Jingyi Yu, Hongjiang Wei, Yuyao Zhang
First: 2026-02-26T16:58:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:58:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Plug-and-Play diffusion prior (PnPDP) frameworks have emerged as a powerful paradigm for solving imaging inverse problems by treating pretrained generative models as modular priors. However, we identify a critical flaw in prevailing PnP solvers (e.g., based on HQS or Proximal Gradient): they function as memoryless operators, updating estimates solely based on instantaneous gradients. This lack of historical tracking inevitably leads to non-vanishing steady-state bias, where the reconstruction fails to strictly satisfy physical measurements under heavy corruption. To resolve this, we propose Dual-Coupled PnP Diffusion, which restores the classical dual variable to provide integral feedback, theoretically guaranteeing asymptotic convergence to the exact data manifold. However, this rigorous geometric coupling introduces a secondary challenge: the accumulated dual residuals exhibit spectrally colored, structured artifacts that violate the Additive White Gaussian Noise (AWGN) assumption of diffusion priors, causing severe hallucinations. To bridge this gap, we introduce Spectral Homogenization (SH), a frequency-domain adaptation mechanism that modulates these structured residuals into statistically compliant pseudo-AWGN inputs. This effectively aligns the solver's rigorous optimization trajectory with the denoiser's valid statistical manifold. Extensive experiments on CT and MRI reconstruction demonstrate that our approach resolves the bias-hallucination trade-off, achieving state-of-the-art fidelity with significantly accelerated convergence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：即插即用扩散与ADMM：双变量耦合用于稳健医学图像重建
即插即用扩散先验（PnPDP）框架已成为通过将预训练生成模型作为模块化先验来解决成像逆问题的强大范式。然而，我们发现现有PnP求解器（如基于HQS或近端梯度法）存在关键缺陷：它们作为无记忆算子，仅依据瞬时梯度更新估计值，缺乏历史跟踪，必然导致稳态偏差不消失，重建结果在严重噪声下无法严格满足物理测量。为解决此问题，我们提出双耦合即插即用扩散，恢复经典对偶变量以提供积分反馈，理论上保证渐近收敛至精确数据流形。然而，这种严格的几何耦合引入了二次挑战：累积的对偶残差表现出频谱着色、结构化伪影，违反扩散先验所假设的加性高斯白噪声（AWGN），导致严重幻觉。为弥合此差距，我们引入频域自适应机制——频谱同质化（SH），将这些结构化残差调制为统计上符合伪AWGN的输入。这有效使求解器的严格优化轨迹与去噪器的有效统计流形对齐。在CT和MRI重建的大量实验中，我们的方法解决了偏差-幻觉权衡问题，在显著加速收敛的同时达到当前最优保真度。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the steady-state bias in existing Plug-and-Play diffusion solvers due to their memoryless gradient updates, this work proposes Dual-Coupled PnP Diffusion, which reintroduces dual variables to ensure asymptotic convergence to the data manifold. However, this geometric coupling introduces structured artifacts that violate the AWGN assumption of diffusion priors, causing hallucinations. To resolve this, Spectral Homogenization is introduced to transform these residuals into pseudo-AWGN inputs, aligning the solver’s trajectory with the denoiser’s statistical manifold. Experiments on CT and MRI show the method eliminates bias-hallucination trade-offs, achieving superior reconstruction fidelity with faster convergence.
为解决现有Plug-and-Play扩散求解器因无记忆梯度更新导致的稳态偏差问题，本文提出双变量耦合PnP扩散方法，通过引入对偶变量确保渐近收敛至数据流形。但该耦合引入了违反AWGN假设的结构化伪影，引发严重幻觉。为此，提出频域谱均质化机制，将结构化残差转化为统计兼容的伪AWGN输入，使求解器轨迹与去噪器统计流形对齐。在CT与MRI重建实验中，该方法有效平衡偏差与幻觉，实现最优重建保真度与更快收敛速度。
Through BrokenEyes: How Eye Disorders Impact Face Detection?
Authors: Prottay Kumar Adhikary
First: 2026-02-26T16:56:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:56:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision disorders significantly impact millions of lives, altering how visual information is processed and perceived. In this work, a computational framework was developed using the BrokenEyes system to simulate five common eye disorders: Age-related macular degeneration, cataract, glaucoma, refractive errors, and diabetic retinopathy and analyze their effects on neural-like feature representations in deep learning models. Leveraging a combination of human and non-human datasets, models trained under normal and disorder-specific conditions revealed critical disruptions in feature maps, particularly for cataract and glaucoma, which align with known neural processing challenges in these conditions. Evaluation metrics such as activation energy and cosine similarity quantified the severity of these distortions, providing insights into the interplay between degraded visual inputs and learned representations.

标题：透过受损之眼：眼部疾病如何影响人脸检测？

Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand how eye disorders affect computer vision systems, this study developed the BrokenEyes framework to simulate five common visual impairments—age-related macular degeneration, cataract, glaucoma, refractive errors, and diabetic retinopathy—and evaluate their impact on deep learning models' feature representations. Quantitative metrics like activation energy and cosine similarity demonstrated that degraded visual inputs caused measurable distortions in learned representations, highlighting the sensitivity of neural networks to visual degradation.
为探究眼疾对视觉感知的影响，本研究构建了BrokenEyes系统，模拟五种常见眼疾——年龄相关性黄斑变性、白内障、青光眼、屈光不正和糖尿病视网膜病变，并分析其对深度学习模型神经特征表示的影响。通过人类与非人类数据集，对比正常与眼疾条件下的模型训练结果发现，白内障和青光眼对特征图的破坏最严重，与已知的神经处理障碍一致。激活能量和余弦相似度等量化指标揭示了视觉输入退化对特征表示造成的显著干扰。
Grasp, Slide, Roll: Comparative Analysis of Contact Modes for Tactile-Based Shape Reconstruction
Authors: Chung Hee Kim, Shivani Kamtikar, Tye Brady, Taskin Padir, Joshua Migdal
Venue: ICRA 2026
First: 2026-02-26T16:53:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:53:59+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 11 figures, Accepted by ICRA 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tactile sensing allows robots to gather detailed geometric information about objects through physical interaction, complementing vision-based approaches. However, efficiently acquiring useful tactile data remains challenging due to the time-consuming nature of physical contact and the need to strategically choose contact locations that maximize information gain while minimizing physical interactions. This paper studies how different contact modes affect object shape reconstruction using a tactile-enabled dexterous gripper. We compare three contact interaction modes: grasp-releasing, sliding induced by finger-grazing, and palm-rolling. These contact modes are combined with an information-theoretic exploration framework that guides subsequent sampling locations using a shape completion model. Our results show that the improved tactile sensing efficiency of finger-grazing and palm-rolling translates into faster convergence in shape reconstruction, requiring 34% fewer physical interactions while improving reconstruction accuracy by 55%. We validate our approach using a UR5e robot arm equipped with an Inspire-Robots Dexterous Hand, showing robust performance across primitive object geometries.
中文标题/摘要
标题：抓取、滑动、滚动：基于触觉的形状重建中接触模式的比较分析
触觉感知使机器人能够通过物理交互获取物体的详细几何信息，补充视觉方法。然而，由于物理接触耗时且需策略性选择接触位置以最大化信息增益并最小化物理交互，高效获取有用触觉数据仍具挑战。本文研究不同接触模式对物体形状重建的影响，使用配备触觉功能的灵巧夹爪。我们比较三种接触交互模式：抓取释放、指端轻触诱导滑动、手掌滚动。这些接触模式结合信息论探索框架，利用形状补全模型指导后续采样位置。结果表明，指端轻触与手掌滚动提升了触觉感知效率，使形状重建更快收敛，物理交互减少34%，重建精度提升55%。我们在配备Inspire-Robots灵巧手的UR5e机械臂上验证了该方法，展现出对基础几何物体的鲁棒性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of efficiently acquiring tactile data for object shape reconstruction by comparing three contact modes—grasp-releasing, finger-grazing sliding, and palm-rolling—using a tactile-enabled dexterous gripper. The method integrates these contact modes with an information-theoretic exploration framework that directs sampling based on a shape completion model to maximize information gain. Experimental results on a UR5e robot with an Inspire-Robots Dexterous Hand demonstrate that finger-grazing and palm-rolling significantly accelerate shape reconstruction, reducing physical interactions by 34% and improving accuracy by 55% compared to grasp-releasing.
该论文旨在通过比较三种接触模式——抓取释放、指尖轻滑和手掌滚动——来提升触觉数据获取效率，从而实现物体形状重建。方法结合信息论探索框架，动态选择最优接触点以最大化形状信息增益并减少物理交互。实验结果表明，指尖轻滑和手掌滚动显著优于抓取释放模式，物理交互次数减少34%，重建精度提升55%，在UR5e机械臂搭载Inspire-Robots灵巧手的平台上对基础几何物体验证了其鲁棒性。
Understanding protein function with a multimodal retrieval-augmented foundation model
Authors: Timothy Fei Truong, Tristan Bepler
First: 2025-08-05T15:11:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:53:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Protein language models (PLMs) learn probability distributions over natural protein sequences. By learning from hundreds of millions of natural protein sequences, protein understanding and design capabilities emerge. Recent works have shown that scaling these models improves structure prediction, but does not seem to improve mutation understanding and representation quality for protein function prediction. We introduce PoET-2, a multimodal, retrieval-augmented protein foundation model that incorporates in-context learning of family-specific evolutionary constraints with optional structure conditioning to learn generative distributions over protein sequences. PoET-2 uses a hierarchical transformer encoder that is equivariant to sequence context ordering and a dual decoder architecture with both causal and masked language modeling objectives, allowing PoET-2 to operate in both fully generative and bidirectional representation learning modes. PoET-2 achieves state-of-the-art performance on zero-shot variant effect prediction, excelling at scoring variants with multiple mutations and challenging indel mutations. In supervised settings, PoET-2 embeddings outperform previous methods for learning sequence-function relationships, especially with small datasets. This work highlights the benefits of combining retrieval augmentation with multimodal, family-centric modeling for advancing protein foundation models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用多模态检索增强基础模型理解蛋白质功能
蛋白质语言模型（PLMs）学习自然蛋白质序列的概率分布。通过学习数亿个自然蛋白质序列，模型展现出蛋白质理解和设计能力。近期研究表明，扩大模型规模可提升结构预测能力，但似乎对突变理解及蛋白质功能预测的表征质量无明显提升。我们提出了PoET-2，一种多模态、检索增强的蛋白质基础模型，结合上下文学习家族特异性进化约束，并可选结构条件化，以学习蛋白质序列的生成分布。PoET-2采用对序列上下文顺序等变的分层Transformer编码器，以及兼具因果和掩码语言建模目标的双解码器架构，使其可支持全生成与双向表征学习模式。PoET-2在零样本变异效应预测中达到最先进性能，尤其擅长评分多重突变及复杂插入缺失突变。在监督学习中，PoET-2嵌入优于以往方法学习序列-功能关系，尤其在小数据集上表现突出。本工作凸显了将检索增强与多模态、家族中心建模结合对推进蛋白质基础模型的重要价值。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that scaling protein language models improves structure prediction but not mutation understanding or function prediction, this work introduces PoET-2, a multimodal, retrieval-augmented foundation model that integrates in-context learning of family-specific evolutionary constraints and optional structure conditioning to learn generative distributions over protein sequences. PoET-2 employs a hierarchical transformer encoder equivariant to sequence context ordering and a dual decoder architecture supporting both causal and masked language modeling, enabling operation in generative and bidirectional modes. Experiments show PoET-2 achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot variant effect prediction, particularly for multi-mutation and indel variants, and outperforms prior methods in supervised learning of sequence-function relationships, especially with small datasets.
鉴于现有蛋白质语言模型在结构预测中随规模扩大而提升，但在突变理解与功能表征方面无明显改进，本研究提出PoET-2，一种结合检索增强与多模态、家族中心建模的蛋白质基础模型，通过上下文学习家族特异性进化约束并可选结构条件化，学习蛋白质序列生成分布。其采用对序列上下文顺序不变的分层Transformer编码器与支持因果和掩码语言建模的双解码器架构，支持生成与双向表征学习模式。实验表明，PoET-2在零样本突变效应预测中达到最先进水平，尤其擅长多突变与插入缺失突变评估，并在监督学习中优于前序方法，尤其在小数据集上表现突出。
EmbodMocap: In-the-Wild 4D Human-Scene Reconstruction for Embodied Agents
Authors: Wenjia Wang, Liang Pan, Huaijin Pi, Yuke Lou, Xuqian Ren, Yifan Wu, Zhouyingcheng Liao, Lei Yang, Rishabh Dabral, Christian Theobalt, Taku Komura
First: 2026-02-26T16:53:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:53:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human behaviors in the real world naturally encode rich, long-term contextual information that can be leveraged to train embodied agents for perception, understanding, and acting. However, existing capture systems typically rely on costly studio setups and wearable devices, limiting the large-scale collection of scene-conditioned human motion data in the wild. To address this, we propose EmbodMocap, a portable and affordable data collection pipeline using two moving iPhones. Our key idea is to jointly calibrate dual RGB-D sequences to reconstruct both humans and scenes within a unified metric world coordinate frame. The proposed method allows metric-scale and scene-consistent capture in everyday environments without static cameras or markers, bridging human motion and scene geometry seamlessly. Compared with optical capture ground truth, we demonstrate that the dual-view setting exhibits a remarkable ability to mitigate depth ambiguity, achieving superior alignment and reconstruction performance over single iphone or monocular models. Based on the collected data, we empower three embodied AI tasks: monocular human-scene-reconstruction, where we fine-tune on feedforward models that output metric-scale, world-space aligned humans and scenes; physics-based character animation, where we prove our data could be used to scale human-object interaction skills and scene-aware motion tracking; and robot motion control, where we train a humanoid robot via sim-to-real RL to replicate human motions depicted in videos. Experimental results validate the effectiveness of our pipeline and its contributions towards advancing embodied AI research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EmbodMocap：面向具身智能体的野外4D人-场景重建

Experiments show superior reconstruction accuracy compared to monocular methods and demonstrate the data’s utility in three embodied AI tasks: monocular human-scene reconstruction, physics-based character animation, and robot motion control via sim-to-real reinforcement learning.
为支持具身智能研究，作者提出EmbodMocap系统，利用两部移动iPhone在自然环境中采集带场景几何的4D人体运动数据，无需专业设备或标记。该方法通过联合标定双RGB-D流，在统一世界坐标系下重建人体与场景，有效缓解深度歧义，性能优于单目方案。实验表明该数据可用于单目人体-场景重建、基于物理的动画生成及机器人运动控制，验证了其在具身AI任务中的实用性和有效性。
Motion-aware Event Suppression for Event Cameras
Authors: Roberto Pellerito, Nico Messikommer, Giovanni Cioffi, Marco Cannici, Davide Scaramuzza
First: 2026-02-26T16:53:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:53:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this work, we introduce the first framework for Motion-aware Event Suppression, which learns to filter events triggered by IMOs and ego-motion in real time. Our model jointly segments IMOs in the current event stream while predicting their future motion, enabling anticipatory suppression of dynamic events before they occur. Our lightweight architecture achieves 173 Hz inference on consumer-grade GPUs with less than 1 GB of memory usage, outperforming previous state-of-the-art methods on the challenging EVIMO benchmark by 67\% in segmentation accuracy while operating at a 53\% higher inference rate. Moreover, we demonstrate significant benefits for downstream applications: our method accelerates Vision Transformer inference by 83\% via token pruning and improves event-based visual odometry accuracy, reducing Absolute Trajectory Error (ATE) by 13\%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向运动感知的事件相机事件抑制框架
本工作提出首个运动感知事件抑制框架，实时学习过滤由IMOs和自运动触发的事件。我们的模型在当前事件流中联合分割IMOs并预测其未来运动，从而在事件发生前实现前瞻性抑制。轻量级架构在消费级GPU上实现173 Hz推理速度，内存占用低于1 GB，在具有挑战性的EVIMO基准测试中分割精度比先前最先进方法提升67%，推理速率高出53%。此外，我们的方法显著提升下游应用性能：通过令牌剪枝加速Vision Transformer推理83%，并提升基于事件的视觉里程计精度，将绝对轨迹误差（ATE）降低13%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to reduce noise from moving objects and ego-motion in event camera data, this work proposes the first motion-aware event suppression framework that learns to filter such events in real time. The method jointly segments moving objects in the current event stream and predicts their future motion to proactively suppress dynamic events before they occur. Experimentally, the lightweight architecture achieves 173 Hz inference on consumer GPUs with under 1 GB memory, surpassing prior state-of-the-art methods by 67% in segmentation accuracy and running 53% faster. It also enhances downstream tasks: Vision Transformer inference is accelerated by 83% via token pruning, and event-based visual odometry accuracy improves by 13% in Absolute Trajectory Error reduction.
为提升事件相机在运动场景下的效率与精度，本文提出首个运动感知事件抑制框架，实时学习过滤由IMOs和自运动引发的事件。该方法联合分割当前IMOs并预测其未来运动，实现事件发生前的预判抑制。实验表明，轻量级架构在消费级GPU上实现173Hz推理速度，内存占用低于1GB，分割精度较现有最先进方法提升67%，推理速率高53%。同时，该方法显著提升下游任务性能：通过令牌剪枝使Vision Transformer推理加速83%，事件视觉里程计绝对轨迹误差降低13%。
ColoDiff: Integrating Dynamic Consistency With Content Awareness for Colonoscopy Video Generation
Authors: Junhu Fu, Shuyu Liang, Wutong Li, Chen Ma, Peng Huang, Kehao Wang, Ke Chen, Shengli Lin, Pinghong Zhou, Zeju Li, Yuanyuan Wang, Yi Guo
First: 2026-02-26T16:51:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:51:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Colonoscopy video generation delivers dynamic, information-rich data critical for diagnosing intestinal diseases, particularly in data-scarce scenarios. High-quality video generation demands temporal consistency and precise control over clinical attributes, but faces challenges from irregular intestinal structures, diverse disease representations, and various imaging modalities. To this end, we propose ColoDiff, a diffusion-based framework that generates dynamic-consistent and content-aware colonoscopy videos, aiming to alleviate data shortage and assist clinical analysis. At the inter-frame level, our TimeStream module decouples temporal dependency from video sequences through a cross-frame tokenization mechanism, enabling intricate dynamic modeling despite irregular intestinal structures. At the intra-frame level, our Content-Aware module incorporates noise-injected embeddings and learnable prototypes to realize precise control over clinical attributes, breaking through the coarse guidance of diffusion models. Additionally, ColoDiff employs a non-Markovian sampling strategy that cuts steps by over 90% for real-time generation. ColoDiff is evaluated across three public datasets and one hospital database, based on both generation metrics and downstream tasks including disease diagnosis, modality discrimination, bowel preparation scoring, and lesion segmentation. Extensive experiments show ColoDiff generates videos with smooth transitions and rich dynamics. ColoDiff presents an effort in controllable colonoscopy video generation, revealing the potential of synthetic videos in complementing authentic representation and mitigating data scarcity in clinical settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ColoDiff：结合动态一致性与内容感知的结肠镜视频生成
结肠镜视频生成可提供动态且信息丰富的数据，对诊断肠道疾病至关重要，尤其在数据稀缺场景下。高质量视频生成需时序一致性与临床属性的精确控制，但面临肠道结构不规则、疾病表现多样及成像模态各异等挑战。为此，我们提出ColoDiff，一种基于扩散的框架，生成具有动态一致性和内容感知的结肠镜视频，旨在缓解数据短缺并辅助临床分析。在帧间层面，TimeStream模块通过跨帧标记机制将时序依赖从视频序列中解耦，即使面对不规则肠道结构也能实现复杂动态建模；在帧内层面，Content-Aware模块结合噪声注入嵌入与可学习原型，实现对临床属性的精确控制，突破扩散模型粗粒度引导的局限。此外，ColoDiff采用非马尔可夫采样策略，生成速度提升超90%，支持实时生成。ColoDiff在三个公开数据集及一家医院数据库上评估，基于生成指标及下游任务（包括疾病诊断、模态区分、肠道准备评分与病灶分割）进行验证。大量实验表明，ColoDiff生成的视频过渡平滑、动态丰富，为可控结肠镜视频生成提供新思路，揭示合成视频在补充真实数据、缓解临床数据稀缺方面的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for high-quality colonoscopy videos to aid diagnosis in data-scarce clinical settings, ColoDiff introduces a diffusion-based framework that ensures temporal consistency and precise control over clinical attributes. It employs a TimeStream module to model inter-frame dynamics via cross-frame tokenization, handling irregular intestinal structures, and a Content-Aware module that uses noise-injected embeddings and learnable prototypes for fine-grained attribute control. Evaluated across four datasets, ColoDiff generates videos with smooth transitions and rich dynamics, achieving state-of-the-art performance in disease diagnosis, modality discrimination, bowel preparation scoring, and lesion segmentation, while reducing generation steps by over 90% for real-time use.
为缓解临床场景中结肠镜视频数据稀缺问题，ColoDiff提出一种基于扩散模型的框架，实现动态一致性与内容可控生成。其TimeStream模块通过跨帧标记机制解耦时间依赖，适应肠道结构不规则性；Content-Aware模块引入噪声注入嵌入与可学习原型，实现对临床属性的精细控制，突破扩散模型粗粒度引导的局限。在四个数据集上的实验表明，ColoDiff生成的视频过渡平滑、细节丰富，在疾病诊断、模态区分、肠道准备评分和病灶分割等下游任务中表现优异，且采样步骤减少超90%，支持实时生成。
Tell Me What To Learn: Generalizing Neural Memory to be Controllable in Natural Language
Authors: Max S. Bennett, Thomas P. Zollo, Richard Zemel
First: 2026-02-26T16:50:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:50:52+00:00
Comments: 58 Pages, 16 Figures, Code at https://github.com/maxbennett/Generalized-Neural-Memory
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Modern machine learning models are deployed in diverse, non-stationary environments where they must continually adapt to new tasks and evolving knowledge. Continual fine-tuning and in-context learning are costly and brittle, whereas neural memory methods promise lightweight updates with minimal forgetting. However, existing neural memory models typically assume a single fixed objective and homogeneous information streams, leaving users with no control over what the model remembers or ignores over time. To address this challenge, we propose a generalized neural memory system that performs flexible updates based on learning instructions specified in natural language. Our approach enables adaptive agents to learn selectively from heterogeneous information sources, supporting settings, such as healthcare and customer service, where fixed-objective memory updates are insufficient.
中文标题/摘要

Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for adaptable and controllable memory in non-stationary environments, this paper introduces a generalized neural memory system that updates its knowledge based on natural language instructions. The method allows agents to selectively learn from heterogeneous information sources without fixed objectives, enabling dynamic memory management. Experimental results demonstrate that the system outperforms traditional memory models in continual learning tasks, particularly in domains like healthcare and customer service, where flexible memory control is critical and forgetting must be minimized.
为应对非平稳环境中模型记忆不可控的问题，本文提出一种基于自然语言指令的通用神经记忆系统，支持动态选择性记忆更新。该方法将语言引导的记忆操作融入神经架构，允许用户动态指定记忆或遗忘内容。实验表明，该方法在持续学习任务中优于固定目标记忆模型，尤其在医疗和客户服务等需要灵活记忆控制的领域表现更优，且能有效减少遗忘。
InnerQ: Hardware-aware Tuning-free Quantization of KV Cache for Large Language Models
Authors: Sayed Mohammadreza Tayaranian Hosseini, Amir Ardakani, Warren J. Gross
First: 2026-02-26T16:50:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:50:36+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 4 figures, 4 tables, 2 algorithms
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reducing the hardware footprint of large language models (LLMs) during decoding is critical for efficient long-sequence generation. A key bottleneck is the key-value (KV) cache, whose size scales with sequence length and easily dominates the memory footprint of the model. Previous work proposed quantization methods that are focused on compressing the KV cache while maintaining its information. We introduce InnerQ, a hardware-aware KV-cache quantization scheme that lowers decode latency without sacrificing accuracy. InnerQ applies group-wise quantization while grouping the cache matrices over their inner dimension. Unlike previous work that group over the outer dimension, InnerQ aligns dequantization with the vector-matrix multiplication and enables scale factor reuse across GPU compute units. This reduces memory accesses and accelerates dequantization, yielding up to $22\%$ speedup over previous work and up to $88\%$ over half-precision vector-matrix multiplication. To preserve fidelity under aggressive compression, InnerQ incorporates (i) hybrid quantization, selecting symmetric or asymmetric quantization per group based on local statistics; (ii) high-precision windows for both the most recent tokens and the attention sink tokens to mitigate outlier leakage; and (iii) per-channel normalization of the key cache, computed once during prefill and folded into the query to avoid runtime overhead. Our evaluation experiments on Llama models shows that InnerQ maintains a few-shot GSM8K performance comparable to non-quantized KV caches and surpasses prior KV cache quantization methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：InnerQ：面向大语言模型KV缓存的硬件感知无调优量化方法
在解码过程中降低大语言模型（LLM）的硬件占用至关重要，以实现高效长序列生成。关键瓶颈是键值（KV）缓存，其大小随序列长度扩展，常主导模型内存占用。此前工作提出压缩KV缓存同时保持其信息的方法。本文提出InnerQ，一种硬件感知的KV缓存量化方案，在不牺牲精度的前提下降低解码延迟。InnerQ采用按内维度分组的量化方式，与以往按外维度分组不同，其解量化过程与向量-矩阵乘法对齐，并支持跨GPU计算单元复用缩放因子，从而减少内存访问并加速解量化，相较前人工作最高提速22%，相较半精度向量-矩阵乘法最高提速88%。为在激进压缩下保持保真度，InnerQ引入：（i）混合量化，根据局部统计选择每组对称或非对称量化；（ii）高精度窗口，用于最近的token和注意力汇点token，以缓解异常值泄漏；（iii）对键缓存进行每通道归一化，预填充阶段计算一次并折叠至查询中，避免运行时开销。在Llama模型上的实验表明，InnerQ在少量样本GSM8K任务上的性能与未量化KV缓存相当，且优于现有KV缓存量化方法。
Summary / 总结
To reduce the hardware footprint and decoding latency of large language models without compromising accuracy, InnerQ introduces a hardware-aware quantization method for KV caches that groups matrices along their inner dimension to align with GPU compute patterns and enable scale factor reuse. This design minimizes memory accesses and accelerates dequantization, achieving up to 22% speedup over prior methods and 88% over half-precision matrix multiplication. To preserve fidelity under aggressive compression, InnerQ employs hybrid quantization per group, high-precision windows for recent and attention sink tokens, and precomputed per-channel normalization for key caches. Evaluated on Llama models, InnerQ maintains performance comparable to unquantized caches on few-shot GSM8K tasks while outperforming existing KV cache quantization techniques.
为降低大语言模型解码时的内存与延迟负担，InnerQ提出一种面向硬件的KV缓存量化方法，无需调参且保持精度。其沿缓存矩阵内维度进行分组量化，使缩放因子能在GPU计算单元间复用，并将反量化对齐至矩阵向量乘法，减少内存访问。为在强压缩下保持精度，采用按组混合量化、对最近和注意力汇点令牌使用高精度窗口、以及在预填充阶段预计算并折叠至查询的键缓存每通道归一化。在Llama模型上的实验表明，InnerQ比前序方法快22%，比半精度矩阵乘法快88%，且在GSM8K少样本任务上的表现与未量化缓存相当。
SC-Arena: A Natural Language Benchmark for Single-Cell Reasoning with Knowledge-Augmented Evaluation
Authors: Jiahao Zhao, Feng Jiang, Shaowei Qin, Zhonghui Zhang, Junhao Liu, Guibing Guo, Hamid Alinejad-Rokny, Min Yang
First: 2026-02-26T16:50:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:50:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly applied in scientific research, offering new capabilities for knowledge discovery and reasoning. In single-cell biology, however, evaluation practices for both general and specialized LLMs remain inadequate: existing benchmarks are fragmented across tasks, adopt formats such as multiple-choice classification that diverge from real-world usage, and rely on metrics lacking interpretability and biological grounding. We present SC-ARENA, a natural language evaluation framework tailored to single-cell foundation models. SC-ARENA formalizes a virtual cell abstraction that unifies evaluation targets by representing both intrinsic attributes and gene-level interactions. Within this paradigm, we define five natural language tasks (cell type annotation, captioning, generation, perturbation prediction, and scientific QA) that probe core reasoning capabilities in cellular biology. To overcome the limitations of brittle string-matching metrics, we introduce knowledge-augmented evaluation, which incorporates external ontologies, marker databases, and scientific literature to support biologically faithful and interpretable judgments. Experiments and analysis across both general-purpose and domain-specialized LLMs demonstrate that (i) under the Virtual Cell unified evaluation paradigm, current models achieve uneven performance on biologically complex tasks, particularly those demanding mechanistic or causal understanding; and (ii) our knowledge-augmented evaluation framework ensures biological correctness, provides interpretable, evidence-grounded rationales, and achieves high discriminative capacity, overcoming the brittleness and opacity of conventional metrics. SC-Arena thus provides a unified and interpretable framework for assessing LLMs in single-cell biology, pointing toward the development of biology-aligned, generalizable foundation models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SC-Arena：面向单细胞推理的知识增强自然语言评估基准
大型语言模型（LLMs）在科学研究中的应用日益广泛，为知识发现与推理提供了新能力。然而在单细胞生物学领域，通用及专业LLMs的评估实践仍显不足：现有基准测试任务分散、采用多项选择分类等与实际应用脱节的格式，并依赖缺乏可解释性和生物学基础的评估指标。我们提出SC-ARENA，一个专为单细胞基础模型设计的自然语言评估框架。SC-ARENA通过虚拟细胞抽象形式统一评估目标，同时表征细胞固有属性与基因层面交互。在此范式下，我们定义五类自然语言任务（细胞类型标注、描述生成、文本生成、扰动预测与科学问答），以考察细胞生物学核心推理能力。为克服传统字符串匹配指标的脆弱性，我们引入知识增强评估，结合外部本体、标记数据库与科学文献，支持生物学忠实且可解释的判断。在通用与领域专用LLMs上的实验与分析表明：（i）在虚拟细胞统一评估范式下，当前模型在生物复杂任务上表现不均，尤其在需要机制或因果理解的任务中表现较差；（ii）我们的知识增强评估框架确保生物学正确性，提供可解释、证据支撑的推理依据，并具备高区分能力，克服传统指标的脆弱性与不透明性。SC-Arena因此提供了一个统一且可解释的框架，用于评估单细胞生物学中的LLMs，推动开发与生物学对齐、具备泛化能力的基础模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the lack of standardized, biologically grounded evaluation for LLMs in single-cell biology, the authors introduce SC-Arena, a natural language benchmark that unifies evaluation through a virtual cell abstraction encompassing intrinsic attributes and gene-level interactions. Five core tasks—cell type annotation, captioning, generation, perturbation prediction, and scientific QA—are designed to probe reasoning capabilities in cellular contexts. To address the limitations of conventional string-matching metrics, the framework incorporates knowledge-augmented evaluation using external ontologies, marker databases, and literature to enable interpretable, evidence-based judgments.
