为解决单细胞生物学中大语言模型缺乏标准化、生物基础的评估问题，作者提出了SC-Arena，一个通过虚拟细胞抽象统一评估的自然语言基准，涵盖细胞内在属性与基因级交互。该框架定义了五个核心任务——细胞类型标注、描述生成、文本生成、扰动预测和科学问答，以检验模型的推理能力。为克服传统字符串匹配指标的局限，SC-Arena引入知识增强评估，整合本体、标记数据库和文献，实现可解释、证据驱动的判断。实验表明，当前模型在复杂任务（尤其需机制理解的任务）上表现不一，而知识增强评估显著提升生物准确性、可解释性和区分能力，优于传统指标。
Fine-Tuning Without Forgetting In-Context Learning: A Theoretical Analysis of Linear Attention Models
Authors: Chungpa Lee, Jy-yong Sohn, Kangwook Lee
First: 2026-02-26T16:49:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:49:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Transformer-based large language models exhibit in-context learning, enabling adaptation to downstream tasks via few-shot prompting with demonstrations. In practice, such models are often fine-tuned to improve zero-shot performance on downstream tasks, allowing them to solve tasks without examples and thereby reducing inference costs. However, fine-tuning can degrade in-context learning, limiting the performance of fine-tuned models on tasks not seen during fine-tuning. Using linear attention models, we provide a theoretical analysis that characterizes how fine-tuning objectives modify attention parameters and identifies conditions under which this leads to degraded few-shot performance. We show that fine-tuning all attention parameters can harm in-context learning, whereas restricting updates to the value matrix improves zero-shot performance while preserving in-context learning. We further show that incorporating an auxiliary few-shot loss enhances in-context learning primarily on the target task, at the expense of degraded in-context learning ability on tasks not seen during fine-tuning. We empirically validate our theoretical results.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无需遗忘的上下文学习微调：线性注意力模型的理论分析
基于Transformer的大语言模型具备上下文学习能力，可通过少量示例提示实现下游任务的适应。实践中，此类模型常通过微调以提升零样本性能，使其无需示例即可解决任务，从而降低推理成本。然而，微调可能损害上下文学习能力，限制微调模型在未见过任务上的表现。本文利用线性注意力模型，从理论上分析微调目标如何修改注意力参数，并识别导致少量示例性能下降的条件。我们证明，更新所有注意力参数会损害上下文学习，而仅更新值矩阵可提升零样本性能同时保留上下文学习能力。进一步地，我们表明引入辅助少量示例损失可显著提升目标任务的上下文学习能力，但会损害微调过程中未见过任务的上下文学习能力。我们通过实验证实了上述理论结果。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the tension between fine-tuning for improved zero-shot performance and preserving in-context learning, this paper analyzes how fine-tuning affects linear attention models theoretically and empirically. It demonstrates that updating all attention parameters during fine-tuning degrades few-shot performance, while restricting updates to the value matrix preserves in-context learning while improving zero-shot capability. Additionally, introducing an auxiliary few-shot loss enhances performance on the target task but at the cost of reduced generalization to unseen tasks. Experimental results confirm these theoretical findings across multiple benchmarks.
为解决微调后零样本性能与上下文学习能力之间的权衡问题，本文从理论上分析了线性注意力模型在微调过程中的参数变化。研究发现，对所有注意力参数进行微调会损害上下文学习能力，而仅更新值矩阵可提升零样本性能同时保留上下文学习能力。进一步研究表明，引入辅助少样本损失可增强目标任务上的上下文学习，但会损害未见过任务的上下文学习能力。实验结果验证了上述理论分析，证实了全参数更新的负面影响及选择性更新或任务特定损失的优势。
ESAA: Event Sourcing for Autonomous Agents in LLM-Based Software Engineering
Authors: Elzo Brito dos Santos Filho
First: 2026-02-26T16:45:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:45:59+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 1 figure, 4 tables. Includes 5 technical appendices
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous agents based on Large Language Models (LLMs) have evolved from reactive assistants to systems capable of planning, executing actions via tools, and iterating over environment observations. However, they remain vulnerable to structural limitations: lack of native state, context degradation over long horizons, and the gap between probabilistic generation and deterministic execution requirements. This paper presents the ESAA (Event Sourcing for Autonomous Agents) architecture, which separates the agent's cognitive intention from the project's state mutation, inspired by the Event Sourcing pattern. In ESAA, agents emit only structured intentions in validated JSON (agent.result or issue.report); a deterministic orchestrator validates, persists events in an append-only log (activity.jsonl), applies file-writing effects, and projects a verifiable materialized view (roadmap.json). The proposal incorporates boundary contracts (AGENT_CONTRACT.yaml), metaprompting profiles (PARCER), and replay verification with hashing (esaa verify), ensuring the immutability of completed tasks and forensic traceability. Two case studies validate the architecture: (i) a landing page project (9 tasks, 49 events, single-agent composition) and (ii) a clinical dashboard system (50 tasks, 86 events, 4 concurrent agents across 8 phases), both concluding with run.status=success and verify_status=ok. The multi-agent case study demonstrates real concurrent orchestration with heterogeneous LLMs (Claude Sonnet 4.6, Codex GPT-5, Antigravity/Gemini 3 Pro, and Claude Opus 4.6), providing empirical evidence of the architecture's scalability beyond single-agent scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ESAA：基于大语言模型的自主代理事件溯源架构
基于大语言模型（LLM）的自主代理已从被动助手演进为能够规划、通过工具执行动作并根据环境观测迭代的系统。然而，它们仍受结构限制：缺乏原生状态、长时程下上下文退化，以及概率生成与确定性执行需求之间的鸿沟。本文提出ESAA（自主代理事件溯源）架构，受事件溯源模式启发，将代理的认知意图与项目状态变更分离。在ESAA中，代理仅输出结构化意图（agent.result或issue.report）；一个确定性编排器验证意图，将事件持久化至追加日志（activity.jsonl），应用文件写入效果，并投影可验证的物化视图（roadmap.json）。该方案结合边界契约（AGENT_CONTRACT.yaml）、元提示配置文件（PARCER）及哈希验证回放（esaa verify），确保已完成任务的不可变性与可追溯性。两个案例验证该架构：（i）落地页项目（9项任务，49个事件，单代理组合）；（ii）临床仪表板系统（50项任务，86个事件，8阶段中4个并发代理），均以run.status=success和verify_status=ok结束。多代理案例展示了异构LLM（Claude Sonnet 4.6、Codex GPT-5、Antigravity/Gemini 3 Pro、Claude Opus 4.6）下的真实并发编排，实证了该架构超越单代理场景的可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the structural limitations of LLM-based autonomous agents—such as lack of persistent state and context degradation—this paper introduces ESAA, an architecture inspired by Event Sourcing that decouples agent intentions from state mutations. Agents emit structured JSON events (e.g., agent.result) validated by a deterministic orchestrator, which persists them in an append-only log, applies file effects, and maintains a verifiable materialized view. The system enforces immutability via boundary contracts and replay verification with hashing. Two case studies demonstrate success: a single-agent landing page project and a multi-agent clinical dashboard system with 86 events and 4 concurrent agents across 8 phases, both achieving successful execution and verification with heterogeneous LLMs including Claude Sonnet 4.6 and Codex GPT-5.
为解决基于LLM的自主代理在状态持久化和长时序上下文退化方面的结构性缺陷，本文提出ESAA架构，借鉴事件溯源模式，将代理意图与状态变更解耦。代理仅输出结构化JSON事件，由确定性编排器验证、持久化至不可篡改日志，并更新可验证的物化视图，辅以边界合约与哈希验证机制。两个案例验证其有效性：单代理落地页项目与四代理并发临床仪表盘系统（含Claude、Codex、Gemini等多模型），均成功完成任务并经验证，证明该架构可扩展至多代理场景。
FairQuant: Fairness-Aware Mixed-Precision Quantization for Medical Image Classification
Authors: Thomas Woergaard, Raghavendra Selvan
First: 2026-02-26T16:44:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:44:47+00:00
Comments: Source code available at https://github.com/saintslab/FairQuant
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Compressing neural networks by quantizing model parameters offers useful trade-off between performance and efficiency. Methods like quantization-aware training and post-training quantization strive to maintain the downstream performance of compressed models compared to the full precision models. However, these techniques do not explicitly consider the impact on algorithmic fairness. In this work, we study fairness-aware mixed-precision quantization schemes for medical image classification under explicit bit budgets. We introduce FairQuant, a framework that combines group-aware importance analysis, budgeted mixed-precision allocation, and a learnable Bit-Aware Quantization (BAQ) mode that jointly optimizes weights and per-unit bit allocations under bitrate and fairness regularization. We evaluate the method on Fitzpatrick17k and ISIC2019 across ResNet18/50, DeiT-Tiny, and TinyViT. Results show that FairQuant configurations with average precision near 4-6 bits recover much of the Uniform 8-bit accuracy while improving worst-group performance relative to Uniform 4- and 8-bit baselines, with comparable fairness metrics under shared budgets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FairQuant：面向医学图像分类的公平感知混合精度量化
通过量化模型参数压缩神经网络，可在性能与效率间取得有益平衡。量化感知训练和后训练量化等方法旨在保持压缩模型与全精度模型的下游性能。然而，这些技术并未显式考虑其对算法公平性的影响。本文研究在显式比特预算下，面向医学图像分类的公平感知混合精度量化方案。我们提出FairQuant框架，结合组感知重要性分析、预算约束下的混合精度分配，以及可学习的比特感知量化（BAQ）模式，在比特率与公平性正则化约束下联合优化权重与每单元比特分配。我们在Fitzpatrick17k和ISIC2019数据集上，基于ResNet18/50、DeiT-Tiny和TinyViT进行评估。结果表明，平均精度接近4-6比特的FairQuant配置，在恢复接近8比特均匀量化精度的同时，相较4比特和8比特均匀量化基线显著提升最差组性能，且在共享预算下公平性指标相当。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to preserve algorithmic fairness during neural network compression for medical image classification, this work introduces FairQuant, a fairness-aware mixed-precision quantization framework. It combines group-aware importance analysis, budgeted mixed-precision allocation, and a learnable Bit-Aware Quantization (BAQ) module to jointly optimize weight precision and per-unit bit assignments under bitrate and fairness constraints. Evaluated on Fitzpatrick17k and ISIC2019 with ResNet18/50, DeiT-Tiny, and TinyViT, FairQuant achieves performance close to uniform 8-bit models while significantly improving worst-group accuracy compared to uniform 4-bit and 8-bit baselines, all under shared bit budgets.
为在医学图像分类中压缩神经网络时保持算法公平性，本文提出FairQuant框架，结合群体感知重要性分析、预算约束的混合精度分配和可学习的位感知量化（BAQ）模块，联合优化权重精度与单元级位分配，满足比特率与公平性约束。在Fitzpatrick17k和ISIC2019数据集上，使用ResNet18/50、DeiT-Tiny和TinyViT模型评估，FairQuant在平均精度4-6比特下恢复接近8比特的精度，同时相较均匀4比特和8比特基线显著提升最差群体性能，且在共享比特预算下保持相近的公平性指标。
Uni-Animator: Towards Unified Visual Colorization
Authors: Xinyuan Chen, Yao Xu, Shaowen Wang, Pengjie Song, Bowen Deng
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-02-26T16:44:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-02-26T16:44:37+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 8 figures. Submitted to CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose Uni-Animator, a novel Diffusion Transformer (DiT)-based framework for unified image and video sketch colorization. Existing sketch colorization methods struggle to unify image and video tasks, suffering from imprecise color transfer with single or multiple references, inadequate preservation of high-frequency physical details, and compromised temporal coherence with motion artifacts in large-motion scenes. To tackle imprecise color transfer, we introduce visual reference enhancement via instance patch embedding, enabling precise alignment and fusion of reference color information. To resolve insufficient physical detail preservation, we design physical detail reinforcement using physical features that effectively capture and retain high-frequency textures. To mitigate motion-induced temporal inconsistency, we propose sketch-based dynamic RoPE encoding that adaptively models motion-aware spatial-temporal dependencies. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that Uni-Animator achieves competitive performance on both image and video sketch colorization, matching that of task-specific methods while unlocking unified cross-domain capabilities with high detail fidelity and robust temporal consistency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Uni-Animator：迈向统一视觉着色
我们提出Uni-Animator，一种基于扩散Transformer（DiT）的框架，用于统一图像与视频素描着色。现有素描着色方法难以统一处理图像与视频任务，存在单参考或多参考时色彩传递不精确、高频物理细节保留不足、大运动场景中时间一致性受损等问题。为解决色彩传递不精确问题，我们引入实例补丁嵌入的视觉参考增强，实现参考色彩信息的精准对齐与融合；为解决物理细节保留不足问题，我们设计物理细节强化机制，利用物理特征有效捕捉并保留高频纹理；为缓解运动导致的时间不一致性，我们提出基于素描的动态RoPE编码，自适应建模运动感知的空间-时间依赖关系。大量实验表明，Uni-Animator在图像与视频素描着色任务中均取得竞争力表现，性能可媲美专用方法，同时具备跨域统一能力，兼具高细节保真度与强时间一致性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing sketch colorization methods in handling both image and video tasks with consistent quality, Uni-Animator introduces a Diffusion Transformer-based framework that unifies these domains. It enhances color transfer through instance patch embedding for precise reference alignment, reinforces physical details using physical feature extraction to preserve high-frequency textures, and ensures temporal coherence via sketch-based dynamic RoPE encoding that models motion-aware spatial-temporal dependencies. Experimental results show Uni-Animator achieves performance comparable to task-specific methods while enabling cross-domain colorization with high detail fidelity and robust temporal consistency.
为解决现有草图着色方法在图像与视频任务间缺乏统一性、颜色转移不准、高频细节丢失及运动场景时序不一致等问题，Uni-Animator 提出基于扩散Transformer的统一框架。通过实例块嵌入增强视觉参考对齐、物理特征强化高频纹理保留、以及基于草图的动态RoPE编码建模运动感知时空依赖，有效提升着色精度与稳定性。实验表明，该方法在图像与视频草图着色任务中均达到与专用方法相当的性能，同时具备跨域泛化能力、高细节保真度与强时序一致性。
